atha śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamī vāyavīyasaṃhitā prārabhyate śrī gaṇeśāya namaḥ śrī gaurī śaṃkarābhyām namaḥ atha saptamī vāyavīya saṃhitā prārabhyate uvāca namaḥ śivāya somāya sa gaṇāya sa sūnave svāmi tvam ca vibhu tvam ca svabhāvam saṃpracakṣate tam ajam viśvakarmāṇam śāśvatam śivam avyayam mahādevam mahātmānam vrajāmi śaraṇam śivam dharmakṣetre mahā tīrthe gaṅgā kālindī saṃgame munayaḥ śaṃsita ātmānaḥ satya vrata parāyaṇāḥ tatra sattram samākarṇya teṣām akliṣṭa karmaṇām sākṣāt satyavatī sūnoḥ vedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ śiṣyaḥ mahātmā medhāvī triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ madhuraḥ śravaṇānām ca manojña pada parvaṇām kathānām nipuṇaḥ vaktā kāla vid naya vid kaviḥ saḥ tam deśam sūtaḥ paurāṇika uttamaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sūtam āyāntam munayaḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ tasmai sāma ca pūjām ca yathāvat pratyapādayan pratigṛhya satām pūjām munibhiḥ pratipāditām uddiṣṭa mānasam bheje niyuktaḥ yuktam ātmanaḥ tatas tad saṃgamāt eva munīnām bhāvitātmanām sa utkaṇṭham abhavat citam śrotum paurāṇikām kathām tadā tam anukūlābhiḥ vāgbhiḥ pūjya mahā ṛṣayaḥ atīva abhimukham kṛtvā vacanam ca idam abruvan ūcuḥ saṃprāpta udyaiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ śaiva rājaiḥ mahāmate purāṇa vidyām akhilām vyāsāt pratyakṣam īyivāḥ tasmāt āścarya bhūtānām kathānām tvam hi bhājanam ratnānām uru sārāṇām ratna ākaraḥ iva arṇavaḥ tvam adṛṣṭa vaśāt asmat darśana artham iha āgataḥ tasmāt śrāvyataram puṇyam sat kathā jñāna saṃhitam vedānta sāra sarvasvam purāṇam śrāvaya āśu naḥ ślakṣṇām ca nyāya saṃyuktām pratyuvāca śubhām giram uvāca kasmāt samyak na vibrūyām purāṇam ṛṣi pūjitam abhivandya mahādevam devīm skandam vināyakam nandinam ca tathā vyāsam sākṣāt satyavatī sutam mā mā mā saṃmitam mahā śiva jñāna arṇavam sākṣāt bhakti mukti phala pradam śabda artha nyāya saṃyuktaiḥ rāgama arthaiḥ vibhūṣitam mahā kalpa prasaṅgeṇa vāyunā kathitam purā aṅgāni vedāḥ catvāraḥ mīmāṃsā nyāya vistaraḥ purāṇam dharma śāstram ca vidyāḥ cetāḥ caturdaśa arthaśāstram param tasmāt vidyāḥ hi aṣṭādaśa smṛtāḥ aṣṭādaśānām vidyānām etāsām bhinna vartmanām hi brahmānam vidadhe sākṣāt putram agre sanātanam vidyāḥ ca imāḥ dadau pūrvam viśva sṛṣṭi artham īśvaraḥ pālanāya harim devam rakṣā śaktim dadau tatas madhyamam tanayam viṣṇum pātāram brahmaṇaḥ api hi labdha vidyena vidhinā prajā sṛṣṭim vitanvatā prathamam sarva śāstrāṇām purāṇam brahmanā smṛtam pravṛttiḥ sarva śāstrāṇām tad mukhāt abhavat tatas yadā asya vistaram śaktāḥ na adhigantum prajāḥ bhuvi tadā vidyā samāsa artham viśveśvara niyogāt dvāpara anteṣu viśvātmā viṣṇuḥ viśvambharaḥ prabhuḥ evam vyastāḥ ca vedāḥ ca dvāpare dvāpare dvijāḥ nirmitāni purāṇāni anyāni ca māyayā vṛtaḥ sambandhaḥ mūlakarmabhyām śivaḥ prerakaḥ īśvaraḥ ūcuḥ kā iyam māyā samā khyātā kiṃrūpaḥ māyayā vṛtaḥ mūlam kīdṛṅ kutas vā asya kim śiva tvam kutas śivaḥ uvāca māyā māheśvarī śaktiḥ cit rūpaḥ māyayā vṛtaḥ malaḥ cicchādakaḥ naijaḥ viśuddhiḥ śivatā svatas ūcuḥ āvṛṇoti katham māyā vyāpinam kena hetunā kimartham ca āvṛtiḥ puṃsaḥ kena vā vinivartate uvāca syāt vyāpi yasmāt kalā ādi api ūcuḥ tat kimādi kim antam vā kim phalam vā kimāśrayam mala kṣayasya kaḥ hetuḥ kīdṛṅ kṣīṇa malaḥ pumān uvāca kalā ādayaḥ samākhyātāḥ yaḥ bhoktā puruṣaḥ bhavet anādi mala bhoga antam ajñāna ātma samāśrayam bāhya antaḥkaraṇa dvāram śarīram bhoga sādhanam bhāva atiśaya labdhena prasādena mala kṣayaḥ ūcuḥ kalā ādi pañcatattvānām kim karma pṛthak ucyate tat avyaktam kena ākāreṇa bhujyate kim tasya śaraṇam bhuktau śarīram ca kim ucyate uvāca diś kriyā vyañjakāḥ vidyā kālaḥ rāgaḥ pravartakaḥ avyaktam kāraṇam yat tat triguṇam prabhava apyayam pradhānam prakṛtiḥ ca iti yat āhuḥ tattva cintakāḥ sukha duḥkha vimoha ātmā bhujyate guṇavān tridhā sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ iti guṇāḥ prakṛti saṃbhavāḥ prakṛtau sūkṣma rūpeṇa tile tailam iva sthitāḥ sukham ca sukha hetuḥ ca samāsāt sāttvikam smṛtam sāttvikā ūrdhva gatiḥ proktā tāmasā syāt adhas gatiḥ madhyamā tu gatiḥ yā sā rājasā paripaṭhyate tanmātra pañcakam ca eva bhūta pañcakam eva ca pañca aikyam pañca karmendriyāṇi ca pradhāna buddhi ahaṃkāra manāṃsi ca catuṣṭayam samāsāt evam avyaktam sa vikāram udāhṛtam man kārya daśā āpannam śarīra ādi ghaṭa ādi vat yathā ghaṭa ādikam kāryam mṛd ādeḥ na ati bhidyate śarīra ādi tathā vyaktam avyaktāt na ati bhidyate tasmāt avyaktam eva aikya kāraṇam karaṇāni ca mahīram ca tad ādhāram tad bhogyam ca api na itarat ūcuḥ uvāca buddhīndriya śarīrāṇām na ātmatā sadbhiḥ iṣyate smṛtyāḥ aniyata jñānāt ayāvat deha vedanāt atas smartā anubhūtānām aśeṣa jñeya gocaraḥ antaryāmī iti vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate sarvam tatra sa sarvatra vyāpya tiṣṭhati śāśvataḥ tathā api kvāpi kena api vyaktam eṣa na dṛśyate na eva ayam cakṣuṣā grāhyaḥ na aparaiḥ indriyaiḥ api yat ca strī na pumān eṣa na eva ca api napuṃsakaḥ aśarīram śarīreṣu caleṣu sthāṇum avyayam sadā paśyati tam dhīraḥ naraḥ pratyavamarśanāt vīja bhūtena puruṣaḥ tena saṃyutaḥ sukhī duḥkhī ca mūḍhaḥ ca bhavati svena karmaṇā adbhiḥ āplavitam kṣetram janayati aṅkuram yathā mā ajñānāt plāvitam karma deham janayate tathā atyantam asukha āvāsāḥ smṛtāḥ ca ekānta mṛtyavaḥ anāgatāḥ atītāḥ ca tanavaḥ asya sahasraśas āgatya āgatya śīrṇeṣu śarīreṣu śarīriṇaḥ chāditaḥ ca viyuktaḥ ca śarīraiḥ eṣu lakṣyate aṣṭāpada parikṣepe hi akṣamudrā iva lakṣyate pathini saṃgamaḥ eva ayam dāraiḥ putraiḥ ca bandhubhiḥ yathā kāṣṭham ca kāṣṭham ca sameyātām mahā udadhau sametya ca vyapeyātām tadvat bhūta samāgamaḥ sa paśyati śarīram tat śarīram tat na paśyati tau paśyati paraḥ kaścid tau ubhau tam na paśyataḥ brahma ādyāḥ sthāvara antar ca paśavaḥ parikīrtitāḥ paśūnām eva sarveṣām proktam etat nidarśanam saḥ eṣa badhyate pāśaiḥ sukha duḥkha aśanaḥ paśuḥ līlā sādhana bhūtaḥ yaḥ īśvarasya iti sūrayaḥ ajñaḥ jantuḥ anīśaḥ ayam ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya anila vacaḥ munayaḥ prīta mānasāḥ procuḥ praṇamya tam vāyum śaiva āgama vicakṣaṇam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śivatattvajñānavarṇanam nāma pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ ayam paśuḥ iti proktaḥ yaḥ ca pāśaḥ udāhṛtaḥ madbhyām vilakṣaṇaḥ kaścid koyam asti tayoḥ patiḥ uvāca asti kaścid aparyanta ramaṇīya guṇa āśrayaḥ patiḥ viśvasya nirmātā paśu pāśa vimocanaḥ abhāve tasya viśvasya sṛṣṭiḥ eṣā katham bhavet acetana tvāt ajñānāt anayoḥ paśu pāśayoḥ pradhāna paramāṇu ādi yāvat kiṃcid acetanam tad kartṛkam svayam dṛṣṭam buddhimat kāraṇam vinā jagant ca kartṛ sāpekṣam kāryam sa avayavam yatas tasmāt kāryasya kartṛ tvam pateḥ na paśu pāśayoḥ paśoḥ api ca kartṛ tvam pateḥ preraṇa pūrvakam ayathā karaṇa jñānam andhasya gamanam yathā ātmānam ca pṛthak matvā preritāram tatas pṛthak bibharti īśaḥ viśvam viśva vimocakaḥ na atas param vijānadbhiḥ veditavyam hi kiṃcanaḥ yathā apaḥ srotasi vyāptāḥ yathā araṇyām hutāśanaḥ evam eva mahātmānam ātmani ātma vilakṣaṇam yaḥ ekaḥ jālavān īśaḥ īśānībhiḥ sva śaktibhiḥ sarvān lokān imān kṛtvā ekaḥ eva saḥ īśate saṃsṛjya viśva bhuvanam goptā te saṃcukoca yaḥ viśvatas cakṣuḥ eva ayam uta ayam viśvatomukhaḥ tathā eva viśvatobāhu viśvatas pāda saṃyutaḥ ca janayan devaḥ ekaḥ maheśvaraḥ mahāntam amṛtam dhruvam hi tamasaḥ parastāt saṃsthitam prabhum asmāt na asti param kiṃcid aparam paramātmanaḥ na aṇīyaḥ asti na ca jyāyaḥ tena pūrṇam idam jagat sarva ānana śiraḥ grīvaḥ sarva bhūta guhā āśayaḥ sarva vyāpī ca bhagavant tasmāt sarva gataḥ śivaḥ sarvatas pāṇi pādaḥ ayam sarvatas akṣi śiraḥ mukhaḥ sarvatas śrutimān loke sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati sarvasya prabhuḥ īśānaḥ sarvasya śaraṇam suhṛd a cakṣūḥ api yaḥ paśyati a karṇaḥ api śṛṇoti yaḥ sarvam vetti na vettā asya tam āhuḥ puruṣam param aṇoḥ aṇīyān mahataḥ mahīyāḥ ayam avyayaḥ guhāyām nihitaḥ ca api jantoḥ asya maheśvaraḥ tam akratum kratu prāyam mahima atiśaya anvitam dhātuḥ prasādāt īśānam vīta śokaḥ prapaśyati mama enam ajaram purāṇam sarvagam vibhum ekaḥ api trīn imān lokān bahudhā śakti yogāt ca tām ajām lohitām śuklām kṛṣṇām ekām tu ajaḥ prajām janitrīm anuśete anyaḥ juṣamāṇaḥ svarūpiṇīm puruṣaḥ magnaḥ guhyamānaḥ ca śocati yadā paśyet īśam parama kāraṇam tadā asya mahimānam ca vīta śokaḥ sukhī bhavet chandāṃsi yajñāḥ ṛtavaḥ yat bhūtam bhavyam eva ca māyī viśvam sṛjati asmin niviṣṭaḥ māyayā paraḥ māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt māyinam tu maheśvaram sūkṣma ati sūkṣmam īśānam kalalasya api madhyatas sraṣṭāram api viśvasya veṣṭitāram ca tasya tu hi śivam eva īśvaram jñātvā śāntim atyantam ṛcchati saḥ eva kālaḥ goptā ca viśvasya adhipatiḥ prabhuḥ tam viśva adhipatim jñātvā mṛtyu pāśāt pramucyate ghṛtāt param maṇḍam iva sūkṣmam jñātvā sthitam prabhum sarva bhūteṣu gūḍham ca sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭam tam jñātvā eva amṛtam aśnute kevalaḥ śivaḥ eva ekaḥ yatas prajñā purātanā rudrasya asya prapadyante rakṣā artham dakṣiṇam sukham kṣaram tu avidyā hi amṛtam vidyā iti parigīyate sarva ādhipatyam kurute sṛṣṭvā sarvān pratāpavān svabhāva vācakān sarvān vācyān ca pariṇāmayan guṇān ca bhogya bhoktṛ tve tat viśvam adhitiṣṭhati te vai guhya upaṇiṣadi gūḍham brahma parātparam bhāva grāhyam anīha ākhyam bhāva abhāva karam śivam yena idam āvṛtam nityam kāla kāla ātmanā yatas tat karma bhūyaśas kṛtvā vinivṛtya ca bhūyaśas aṣṭābhiḥ ca tribhiḥ ca evam dvābhyām ca ekena vā punar tat kālena ātma guṇaiḥ ca api kṛtsnam eva jagant svayam guṇaiḥ ārabhya karmāṇi svabhāva ādīni yojayet teṣām abhāve nāśaḥ syāt kṛtasya api ca karmaṇaḥ sarva vid triguṇa adhīśaḥ brahma sākṣāt parātparaḥ tam viśvarūpam abhavam bhavam īḍyam prajāpatim yasmāt prapañcaḥ parivartate harma āvaham pāpa nudam bhoga īśam viśva dhām ca tam īśvarāṇām paramam maheśvaram tam devatānām paramam ca daivatam patim patīnām paramam parastāt vidāma devam bhuvaneśvara īśvaram parā asya vividhā śaktiḥ śrutau svābhāvikī śrutā jñānam balam kriyā ca eva yābhyaḥ viśvam idam kṛtam tasya asti patiḥ kaścid na eva liṅgam na ca īśitā tat kāraṇam kāraṇānām ca saḥ teṣām adhipa adhipaḥ na janma hetavaḥ tadvat mala māyā ādi saṃjñakāḥ saḥ ekaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍhaḥ vyāptaḥ ca viśvatas sarva bhūta adhivāsaḥ ca sākṣī cetā ca nirguṇaḥ ekaḥ vaśī niṣkriyāṇām bahūnām vivaśa ātmanām nityānām api asau nityaḥ cetanānām ca cetanaḥ ekaḥ bahūnām ca akāmaḥ kāmān īśaḥ prayacchati sāṃkhya yoga adhigamyam yatkāraṇam jagantām patim jñātvā devam paśuḥ pāśaiḥ sarvaiḥ eva vimucyate pradhānaḥ kṣetrajña patiḥ guṇa īśaḥ pāśa mocakaḥ brahmānam vidadhe pūrvam vedān ca upādiśat svayam mumukṣuḥ asmāt saṃsārāt prapadye śaraṇam śivam niṣphalam niṣkriyam śāntam niravadyam nirañjanam yadā carma vat ākāśam veṣṭayiṣyanti mānavāḥ tadā śivam a vijñāya duḥkhasya antaḥ bhaviṣyati tapaḥ prabhāvāt devasya prasādāt ca mahā ṛṣayaḥ ati āśrama ucita jñānam pavitram pāpa nāśanam na apraśāntāya dātavyam etat jñānam anuttamam na putrāya āśu vṛttāya na a śiṣyāya ca sarvathā tasya ete kathitāḥ ahi arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ atas ca saṃkṣepam idam śṛṇudhvam śivaḥ parastāt prakṛtyāḥ ca puṃsaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śivatattvavarṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ yadā asya antargatam viśvam śaśvat saṃsāra maṇḍalam brahmā hariḥ ca rudraḥ ca tathā anye ca sura asurāḥ kaḥ eṣa bhagavān kālaḥ kasya vā vaśa vartī ayam uvāca kāla kāṣṭhā nimeṣa ādi kalā kalita vigraham kāla ātmā iti samākhyātam tejaḥ māheśvaram param niyoga rūpam īśasya balam viśva niyāmakam tasya aṃśa aṃśa mayī muktiḥ kāla ātmani mahātmani tatas niṣkramya saṃkrāntā visṛṣṭa agreḥ iva āyasī tasmāt kāla vaśe viśvam na saḥ viśva vaśe sthitaḥ śivasya tu vaśe kālaḥ na kālasya vaśe śivaḥ yatas apratihatam śārvam tejaḥ kāle pratiṣṭhitam yaḥ kālam prajñā viśeṣeṇa kaḥ ativartitum arhati eka chatrām mahīm kṛtsnām ye parākramya śāsati mad bhava tu anuṣṭhita rasāyanāḥ śriyā rūpeṇa śīlena balena ca kulena ca durvijñeya svabhāvasya kālaḥ asya aho vicitra tā yaḥ śrīmān saḥ niḥśrīkaḥ kālaḥ citra gatiḥ dvijāḥ na ābhijātyam na vai śīlam na balam na ca naipuṇam bhavet kāryāya paryāptam kālaḥ ca hi anirodhakaḥ ye sa nāthāḥ ca dātāraḥ gīta vādyaiḥ upasthitāḥ ye ca anāthāḥ para anna ādāḥ kālaḥ teṣu sama kriyaḥ tāni eva kālena samāhṛtāni siddhim prayānti āśu sukham diśanti na akālatas ayam mriyate jāyate vā na akālatas puṣṭim agryām upaiti na akālatas sukhitam duḥkhitam vā na akālikam vastu samasti kiṃcid tat kālena śītaḥ prativāti vātaḥ kālena vṛṣṭiḥ jaladān upaiti kālena ca ūṣmā praśamam prayāti kālena sarvam saphalatvam eti prayānti kālena sasyāni layam prayānti kālena saṃjīvati jīva lokaḥ ittham kāla ātmanaḥ tattvam yaḥ vijānāti tattvāt kāla ātmānam atikramya kāla atītam sa paśyati iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe kālamahimavarṇanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ saṃkhyā rūpasya kālasya kaḥ punar paramaḥ avadhiḥ uvāca āyuṣaḥ atra nimeṣa ākhyam ādya mānam pracakṣate saṃkhyā rūpasya kālasya śānttu atīta kalā avadhi akṣi pakṣma parikṣepaḥ nimeṣaḥ parikalpitaḥ tādṛśāṇām nimeṣāṇām kāṣṭhāḥ daśa ca pañca ca kāṣṭhān triṃśatkalāḥ nāma kalān triṃśat muhūrtakaḥ muhūrtānām api triṃśat ahorātram pracakṣate triṃśat saṃkhyaiḥ ahorātraiḥ māsaḥ pakṣa dvaya ātmakaḥ māsaḥ kṛṣṇa sita ātmakaḥ māsaiḥ taiḥ ayanam ṣaḍbhiḥ varṣam dve ca ayanam matam laukikena eva mānena abdaḥ yaḥ mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ dakṣiṇam ca ayanam rātriḥ tathā udagayanam dinam māsaḥ triṃśat ahorātraiḥ divyaḥ mānuṣa vat smṛtaḥ devānām māsaiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ tathā trīṇi varṣa śatāni eva ṣaṣṭi varṣa yutāni api divyaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ jñeyaḥ mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ pūrvam kṛta yugam nāma tatas tretā vidhīyate dvāparam ca kaliḥ ca eva yugāni etāni kṛtsnaśas catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇām tat kṛtam yugam tasya tāvacchatī sandhyā sandhyā aṃśaḥ ca tathāvidhaḥ itareṣu sa sandhyeṣu sa saṃdhyāṃśeṣu ca triṣu eka apāyena vartante sahasrāṇi śatāni ca etat dvādaśa sāhasram sa adhikam ca caturyugam caturdaśa ekasmin manūnām parivṛttayaḥ sa prajāni vyatītāni śataśas atha sahasraśas ajñeya tvāt ca sarveṣām asaṃkhyeya tayā punar śakyaḥ na eva ānupūrvyāt vai teṣām vaktum su vistaraḥ tat tat tat tat tat tat tat iha ucyate varṣāṇām aṣṭa sāhasram yat ca tat brahmanaḥ yugam savanānām sahasram ca triguṇam trivṛtam tathā tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tatra tatra tatra śatāni māse catvāri viṃśatyā sahitāni ca abde pañca sahasrāṇi catvāriṃśat yutāni ca catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi pañca lakṣāṇi ca āyuṣi brahmā viṣṇoḥ dine ca ekaḥ viṣṇuḥ rudra dine tathā sākṣāt śivasya tad saṃkhyaḥ tathā saḥ api sadāśivaḥ catvāriṃśat sahasrāṇi pañca lakṣāṇi ca āyuṣi tasmin sākṣāt śivena eṣa kāla ātmā sampravartate yat tat sṛṣṭyāḥ samākhyātam kāla antaram iha dvijāḥ etat kāla antaram jñeyam ahar vai pārameśvaram rātriḥ ca tāvatī jñeyā parameśasya kṛtsnaśas ahar tasya tu yā sṛṣṭiḥ rātriḥ ca pralayaḥ smṛtaḥ eṣa upacāraḥ kriyate lokānām hita kāmyayā prajāḥ prajānām patayaḥ mūrtayaḥ ca sura asurāḥ indriyāṇi indriya arthāḥ ca mahābhūtāni pañca ca tanmātrāṇi atha bhūtādiḥ buddhiḥ ca saha daivāt ahar tiṣṭhanti sarvāṇi pārameśasya dhīmataḥ yaḥ viśvātmā karma kāla svabhāva ādi arthe śaktiḥ yasya na ullaṅghanīyā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva bhāge kālaprabhāve tridevāyurvarṇanam nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ katham jagat idam kṛtsnam vidhāya ca nidhāya ca mahā ājñayā paramām krīḍām karoti parameśvaraḥ u vā punar eva idam grasyate pṛthu kukṣiṇā uvāca śaktiḥ prathama sambhūtā śānti atīta pada uttarā tatas māyā tatas avyaktam śivāt śaktimataḥ prabhoḥ śānti atīta padam śaktyāḥ tatas śānti pada kramāt tatas vidyā padam tasmāt pratiṣṭhā pada sambhavaḥ nivṛtti padam utpannam pratiṣṭhā padāt kramāt evam uktā samāsena sṛṣṭiḥ īśvara coditā ānulomyāt tathā eteṣām pratilomyena saṃhṛtiḥ pañca pada uddiṣṭāt paraḥ sraṣṭā samiṣyate kalābhiḥ pañcabhiḥ vyāptam tasmāt viśvam idam jagant avyaktam kāraṇam yat tat ātmanā samanuṣṭhitam mahat ādi viśeṣa antam sṛjati iti api saṃmatam kim tu tatra api kartṛ tvam na avyaktasya na ca ātmanaḥ pradhāna paramāṇu ādi yāvat kiṃcid acetanam tad kartṛkam svayam dṛṣṭam buddhimat kāraṇam vinā jagant ca kartṛ sāpekṣam kāryam sa avayavam yatas an ādi nidhanaḥ ca ayam mahā aiśvarya saṃyutaḥ saḥ eva jagataḥ kartā mahādevaḥ maheśvarāḥ tatas pṛthak ananvayaḥ pariṇāmaḥ pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ puruṣasya ca iti iyam śāśvatī niṣṭhā satām manasi vartate yāvat ādi samārambhaḥ yāvat yaḥ pralayaḥ mahān tāvat apyeti sakalam brahmanaḥ śāradām śatam tat avyaktam ātmanaḥ kāryam ādāya ātmani tiṣṭhati sādharmyeṇa adhitiṣṭhete pradhāna puruṣau ubhau śānta vāta eka nīre ca na prājñāyata kiṃcana upāsya rajanīm kṛtsnām parām māheśvarām tatas prabhātāyām tu śarvaryām pradhāna puruṣau ubhau praviśya kṣobhayāmāsa māyā yogāt maheśvaraḥ tatas punar aśeṣāṇām bhūtānām prabhava apyayāt tasmāt abhavat sṛṣṭiḥ ājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva bhāge sṛṣṭipālanapralayakartṛtvavarṇanam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca puruṣa adhiṣṭhitāt pūrvam avyaktāt īśvara ājñayā buddhi ādayaḥ viśeṣa antāḥ vikārāḥ ca abhavan kramāt trayaḥ devāḥ prajajñire mahat apratimam śaśvat aiśvaryam ca aṇima ādikam sṛṣṭi sthiti laya ākhyeṣu karmasu triṣu hetutām prabhu tvena saha eteṣām prasīdati maheśvaraḥ sarga rakṣā laya ācāram pratyekam pradadau ca saḥ teṣām ādhikyam aiśvaryam ca atiricyate mūrkhāḥ nindanti tān vāgbhiḥ saṃrambha abhiniveśinaḥ yātudhānāḥ bhavanti eva piśācāḥ ca na saṃśayaḥ devaḥ guṇatraya atītaḥ catur vyūhaḥ maheśvaraḥ saḥ uyam ātmā trayasya asya prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca līlā kṛta jagat sṛṣṭiḥ īśvara tve vyavasthitaḥ saḥ eva ca tad ādhāraḥ tad ātmā tad adhiṣṭhitaḥ tasmāt maheśvaraḥ ca eva prakṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ tathā sadāśiva bhavaḥ viṣṇuḥ brahmā sarva śiva ātmakam pradhānāt prathamam jajñe vṛddhiḥ khyātiḥ matiḥ mahant ahaṃkāraḥ ca bhūtāni tanmātrāṇi indriyāṇi ca tu buddhīndriyāṇi pañca eva pañca karmendriyāṇi ca tamas yuktāt ahaṃkārāt bhūta tanmātra sambhavaḥ bhūtānām ādi bhūta tvāt bhūtādiḥ kathyate tu saḥ bhūtādeḥ śabda mātram syāt tatra ca ākāśa sambhavaḥ bhāsaḥ sparśaḥ utpannaḥ sparśāt vāyu samudbhavaḥ ca puruṣa dhiṣṭhita tvāt ca avyakta anugrahena ca mahat ādi viśeṣa antāḥ hi aṇḍam utpādayanti te tatra kāryam ca karaṇam saṃsiddham brahmaṇaḥ yadā tad aṇḍe kṣetrajñaḥ brahma saṃjñitaḥ mādikartā sa bhūtānām brahma agre samavartata tasya īśvarasya pratimā jñāna vairāgya lakṣaṇā dharma aiśvarya karā buddhiḥ brāhmā yajñe abhimāninaḥ caturddhā pravibhakta tvāt cāturvyūhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ādi tvāt ādidevaḥ asau ajāta tvāt ajaḥ smṛtaḥ pāti yasmāt prajāḥ sarvāḥ prajāpatiḥ iti smṛtaḥ garbha udakam samudrāḥ ca jarāyuḥ ca api parvatāḥ adbhiḥ daśaguṇābhiḥ tu bāhya toṇḍam samāvṛtam apaḥ daśaguṇena eva tejasā bahis āvṛtāḥ tejaḥ daśaguṇena eva vāyunā bahis āvṛtam mākāśena āvṛtaḥ vāyuḥ kham ca bhūtādinā āvṛtam bhūtādiḥ mahatā tadvat avyaktena āvṛtaḥ mahant etaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ aṇḍam saptabhiḥ bahis āvṛtam etat āvṛttya ca anyonyam aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ sṛṣṭi pālana vidhvaṃsa karma kartryaḥ dvijottamāḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvena vikārāḥ tu vikāriṣu yathā pūrvam prasārya viniyacchati yathā avyaktam sṛṣṭvā bhūyas niyacchati guṇāḥ kāla vaśāt eva bhavanti viṣamāḥ samāḥ guṇa sāmye layaḥ jñeyaḥ vaiṣamye sṛṣṭiḥ ucyate tat idam brahmaṇaḥ yoniḥ etat aṇḍam ghanam mahat brahmaṇaḥ kṣetram uddiṣṭam brahmā kṣetrajñaḥ ucyate iti īdṛśāṇām aṇḍānām koṭayaḥ jñeyāḥ sahasraśas sṛṣṭā pradhānena tathā labdhvā śambhoḥ tu saṃnidhim aṇḍāt jajñe vibhuḥ brahmā lokāḥ tena kṛtāḥ tu ime ātyantikaḥ ca pralaya unta kāle līlā kṛtaḥ kevalam īśvarasya yat tat smṛtam kāraṇam aprameyam brahmā pradhānam prakṛtyāḥ prasūtiḥ anādi madhya antam ananta vīryam śuklam su raktam puruṣeṇa yuktam aṣṭau vikārān api ca ādi kāle sṛṣṭvā samaśnāti tathā antakāle prakṛti avasthāpita kāraṇānām yā ca sthitiḥ yā ca punar pravṛttiḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām brahmāṃḍasthitivarṇanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ manvantarāṇi sarvāṇi kalpa bhedān ca sarvaśas uvāca kāla saṃkhyā vivṛttasya parārddhaḥ brahmanaḥ smṛtaḥ tāvān ca eva asya kālaḥ nyaḥ tasya ante pratisṛjyate caturdaśa mahābhāgāḥ manūnām parivṛttayaḥ anādi tvāt ananta tvāt ajñeya tvāt ca kṛtsnaśas manvantarāṇi kalpāḥ ca na śakyāḥ vacanāt pṛthak ukteṣu api ca sarveṣu śṛṇvatām vaḥ vacaḥ mama tatra saṃkṣipya vartante sṛṣṭayaḥ pratisṛṣṭayaḥ yaḥ tu ayam vartate kalpaḥ vārāhaḥ nāma nāmnaḥ svāyambhuva ādayaḥ sapta sapta sāvarṇika ādayaḥ manvantareṣu sarveṣu sarga saṃhāra vṛttayaḥ prāyas samābhavanti iti tarkaḥ kāryaḥ vijānatā pūrva kalpe parāvṛtte pravṛtte kālamārute samunmūlita mūleṣu vṛkṣeṣu ca vaneṣu ca ca dikṣu sarvāsu magnāsu vāripūre mahīyasi tad adbhiḥ caṭula ākṣepaiḥ taraṃga bhuja maṇḍalaiḥ prārabdha caṇḍa nṛtyeṣu tatas pralaya vāriṣu brahmā nārāyaṇaḥ bhūtvā suṣvāpa salile sukham imam ca udāharan mantram ślokam nārāyaṇam prati tam śṛṇudhvam muni śreṣṭhāḥ tad artham ca akṣara āśrayam apaḥ nārāḥ iti proktāḥ apaḥ vai nara sūnavaḥ ayanam tasya tāḥ yasmāt tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ maya yoga mayām nidrām kurvantam tridaśeśvaram baddhāñjali puṭāḥ siddhāḥ jana loka nivāsinaḥ stotraiḥ prabodhayāmāsuḥ prabhāta samaye surāḥ yathā sṛṣṭi ādi samaye īśvaram śrutayaḥ purā udaikṣata diśaḥ sarvāḥ yoga nidrā alasa īkṣaṇaḥ sa vismayaḥ iva āsīnaḥ parām cintām upāgamat kva sā bhagavatī yā tu manojñā mahatī mahī nānāvidha mahā śaila nadī nagara kānanā magnām dharaṇīm dharaṇīpatiḥ tatas bhūmyāḥ samuddhāram kartu kāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ asmarat mahā parvata varṣmāṇam mahā jalada niḥsvanam nīla megha pratīkāśam dīpta śabdam bhayānakam pīna vṛtta ghana skandha pīna unnata kaṭi taṭam hrasva vṛtta ūru jaṅghā agram su tīkṣṇa pura maṇḍalam padmarāga maṇi prakhyam vṛtta bhīṣaṇa locanam udīrṇa ucchvāsa niśvāsa ghūrṇita pralaya arṇavam maṇibhiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ citraiḥ mahā ratnaiḥ pariṣkṛtam āsthāya vipulam rūpam vārāham amitam vidhiḥ rasātalam sa tadā śuśubhe atīva sūkaraḥ giri saṃnibhaḥ liṅga ākṛteḥ maheśasya pāda mūlam gataḥ yathā tatas sa salile magnām pṛthivīm pṛthivīṃdharaḥ uddhṛtya āliṅgya daṃṣṭrābhyām unmamajja rasātalāt tam dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ siddhāḥ jana loka nivāsinaḥ śuśubhe tatas saṃsthānam ānīya varāhaḥ mahatīm mahīm svam eva rūpam āsthāya sthāpayāmāsa vai vibhuḥ pṛthivīm ca samīkṛtya pṛthivyām sthāpayan girīn bhūḥ ādyān caturaḥ lokān kalpayāmāsa pūrvavat iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām sṛṣṭyādivarṇanam nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tamas mohaḥ mahā mohaḥ tāmisraḥ ca andha saṃjñitaḥ avidyā pañcamā ca eṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ sarvatas tamasā atīva bīja kumbha vat āvṛtaḥ bahis antar ca aprakāśaḥ stabdhaḥ niḥsaṃjñaḥ eva ca tasmāt teṣām vṛtā buddhiḥ mukhāni karaṇāni ca tasmāt te saṃvṛta ātmānaḥ nagāḥ mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ tam dṛṣṭvā asādhakam brahmā prathamam sargam īdṛśam antar prakāśāḥ tiryyañcaḥ āvṛtāḥ ca bahis punar paśu ātmānaḥ tatas jātāḥ utpatha grāhinaḥ ca te te sukha prīti bahulāḥ bahis antar ca na āvṛtāḥ prakāśāḥ bahis antar ca svabhāvāt eva saṃjñitāḥ manuṣya nāmā sañjātaḥ sargaḥ duḥkha samutkaṭaḥ prakāśāḥ abahir antar te tama udriktāḥ rajaḥ adhikāḥ viparyayeṇa śaktyā ca tuṣṭyā asiddhyā tathā eva ca te a parigrāhiṇaḥ sarve saṃvibhāga ratāḥ punar yad api aśīlāḥ ca bhūta ādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ tanmātrāṇām dvitīyaḥ tu bhūta sargaḥ saḥ ucyate iti eṣa prakṛtyāḥ sargaḥ sambhṛtaḥ a buddhi pūrvakaḥ mukhya sargaḥ caturthaḥ tu mukhyāḥ vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ tat ūrddhvasrotasaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ deva sargaḥ tu saḥ smṛtaḥ tatas srotasām sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ tad anugrahaḥ sargaḥ kaumāraḥ navamaḥ smṛ prākṛtāḥ ca trayaḥ pūrve sargāḥ te abuddhi pūrvakāḥ buddhi pūrvam pravartante mukhya ādyāḥ pañca vaikṛtāḥ agre sasarja vai brahmā mānasān ātmanaḥ samān sanandam sanakam ca eva vidvasam ca sanātanam xc eva prajāpatiḥ sarve te yoginaḥ jñeyāḥ vīta rāgāḥ vimatsarāḥ tad āsakta manasaḥ na cakruḥ sṛṣṭaye matim teṣu sṛṣṭi anapekṣeṣu gateṣu sanaka ādiṣu tatāpa paramam tapaḥ tatas dīrghena kālena duḥkhāt krodhaḥ vyajāyata prakrodha āviṣṭasya netrābhyām prāpatan aśru bindavaḥ sarvān tān aśru jān dṛṣṭvā brahmā ātmānam anindata tasya tīvrā abhavat mūrcchā krodha amarṣa samudbhavā mūrchitaḥ tu jahau prāṇān krodha āviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ tatas prāṇeśvaraḥ rudraḥ bhagavant nīlalohitaḥ prasādam atulam kartum prādurāsīt prabhoḥ mukhāt daśadhā ca ekadhā cakre sva ātmānam prabhuḥ īśvaraḥ te tena uktāḥ mahātmānaḥ daśadhā ca ekadhā kṛtāḥ yūyam sṛṣṭāḥ mayā vatsāḥ loka anugraha kāraṇāt rodanāt drāvaṇāt ca eva te rudrāḥ nāmnaḥ smṛtāḥ ye rudrāḥ te khalu prāṇāḥ ye prāṇāḥ te mahātmakāḥ tatas mṛtasya devasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ dadau punar prāṇān brahma putraḥ maheśvaraḥ prahṛṣṭa vadanaḥ rudraḥ prāṇa pratyāgamāt vibhoḥ abhyabhāṣata viśveśaḥ brahmānam paramam vacaḥ mābhaiḥ mābhaiḥ mahābhāgaiḥ viriñca jagantām guro mayā te prāṇitāḥ prāṇāḥ sukham uttiṣṭha suvrataiḥ tathā pratyāgata prāṇaḥ snigdha gambhīrayā girā uvāca vacanam brahmā tam uddiśya kṛtāñjaliḥ tvam hi darśana mātreṇa ca ānandayasi mama manaḥ kaḥ bhavān viśvamūrtyāḥ vā sthitaḥ ekādaśa ātmakaḥ tasya tat vacanam śrutvā vyājahāra maheśvaraḥ spṛśan kārābhyām brahmānam su sukhābhyām sureśvaraḥ mām viddhi paramātmānam tava putra tvam āgatam ete ca ekādaśa rudrāḥ tvā su rakṣitum āgatāḥ tasmāt tīvrām imām mūrchām vidhūya mad anugrahāt nānā aṣṭakena viśvātmā tuṣṭāva parameśvaram śarvāya kṣiti rūpāya nandī surabhaye namaḥ īśāya vasave tubhyam namaḥ sparśa maya ātmane paśūnām pataye ca eva pāvakāya ati tejase bhīmāya vyoma rūpāya śabda mātrāya te namaḥ ugrāya ugra svarūpāya yajamāna ātmane namaḥ evam stutvā mahādevam brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ prārthayāmāsa viśveśam girā praṇati pūrvayā sṛṣṭi hetoḥ tvam utpannaḥ mama aṅge anaṅga nāśanaḥ sahāyam kuru sarvatra sraṣṭum arhasi sa prajāḥ bāḍham iti eva tām vāṇīm pratijagrāha śaṃkaraḥ sraṣṭum tena abhyanujñātaḥ tathā anyāḥ ca asṛjat prajāḥ iti ete brahmanaḥ putrāḥ dvādaśa ādau prakīrtitāḥ saha rudreṇa saṃbhūtāḥ purāṇāḥ gṛhamedhinaḥ teṣām dvādaśa vaṃśāḥ syuḥ divyāḥ deva gaṇa anvitāḥ prajāvantaḥ kriyāvantaḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ atha deva asura pitR̥n manuṣyān ca catuṣṭayam saha rudreṇa sisṛkṣuḥ ambhasi etāni vai vidhiḥ sa sṛṣṭi artham samādhāya brahmā ātmānam ayūyujat ajanayat jaghanāt asurān sarvān prajanāt api mānuṣān avaskare kṣudhā āviṣṭāḥ rākṣasāḥ tasya jajñire putrāḥ tamas rajas prāyāḥ balinaḥ te niśācarāḥ sarpāḥ yakṣāḥ tathā bhūtāḥ gandharvāḥ saṃprajajñire vayāṃsi pakṣataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ vakṣasaḥ asṛjat mukha tojān tathā pārśvāt uragān ca vinirmame padbhyām ca aśvān sa mātaṃgān śarabhān gavayān mṛgān uṣṭrān aśvatarān ca eva nyaṅkūn anyāḥ ca jātayaḥ gāyatrīm ca ṛcam ca eva trivṛt sāma rathantaram agniṣṭomam ca yajñānām nirmame prathamān mukhāt yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubham chandaḥstomam pañcadaśam tathā bṛhatsāma tathā uktham ca dakṣiṇāt asṛjat mukhāt sāmāni jagatī chandaḥ stomam saptadaśam tathā vairūpyam atirātram ca paścimāt asṛjat mukhāt ekaviṃśam atharvāṇam āptoryāmāṇam eva ca anuṣṭubham sa vairājam uttarāt asṛjat mukhāt uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyaḥ tasya jajñire yakṣāḥ piśācāḥ gandharvāḥ tathā eva apsarasām gaṇāḥ nara kiṃnara rakṣāṃsi vayaḥ paśu mṛga uragāḥ teṣām vai yāni karmāṇi prāñc sṛṣṭāni prapedire tāni eva te prapadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punar punar hiṃsra hiṃsra ahiṃsre mṛdu krūre dharma adharma āvṛta anṛte mahābhūteṣu nānātvam indriyārtheṣu muktiṣu nāma rūpam ca bhūtānām prākṛtānām prapañcanam mārṣāṇi ca eva nāmāni yāḥ ca vedeṣu vṛttayaḥ śarvarī ante prasūtānām tāni eva ebhyaḥ dadau ajaḥ yathā ṛtau ṛtu liṅgāni nānā rūpāṇi paryaye tāni tāni eva tathā bhāvāḥ yuga ādiṣu mahat ādyaḥ viśeṣa antaḥ vikāraḥ prakṛtyāḥ svayam candra sūrya prabhā juṣṭaḥ graha nakṣatra maṇḍitaḥ nadībhiḥ ca samudraiḥ ca parvataiḥ ca sa maṃḍitaḥ mahābhūta pramāṇaḥ ca viśeṣa amala pallavaḥ dharma adharma supuṣpa āḍhyaḥ sukha duḥkha phala udayaḥ hi sarva bhūtānām brahmavṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ mūrdhānam tasya viprāḥ vadanti kham vai nābhim candra sūryau ca netre diśaḥ śrotre caraṇau ca kṣitim ca saḥ acintya ātmā sarva bhūta praṇetā vaktrāt tasya saṃprasūtāḥ tad vakṣasaḥ kṣatriyāḥ pūrva bhāgāt ca iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe sṛṣṭivarṇanam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ bhavatā kathitā sṛṣṭiḥ bhavasya paramātmanaḥ haraḥ bhagavant rudraḥ kapardī nīlalohitaḥ yasya brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ ca praṇāmam kurutaḥ bhayāt yaḥ ayam devaḥ svakāt aṅgāt brahma viṣṇū purā sṛjat sa katham bhagavān rudraḥ ādidevaḥ purātanaḥ sṛṣṭau parasparasya aṅgāt iti prāk api śuśruma katham punar aśeṣāṇām bhūtānām hetu bhūtayoḥ guṇa pradhāna bhāvena prādurbhāvaḥ parasparāt na a pṛṣṭam bhavatā kiṃcid na a śrutam ca kathaṃcana śrutum uvāca sthāne pṛṣṭam idam viprāḥ bhavadbhiḥ praśna kovidaiḥ idam eva purā pṛṣṭaḥ mama prāha pitāmahaḥ trayaḥ te kāraṇa ātmānaḥ jatāḥ sākṣāt maheśvarāt parama aiśvarya saṃyuktāḥ parameśvara bhāvitāḥ tad śaktyā adhiṣṭhitāḥ nityam tad kārya karaṇa kṣamāḥ pitrā niyamitāḥ pūrvam trayaḥ api triṣu karmasu brahmā sarge hariḥ trāṇe rudraḥ saṃharaṇe tathā tathā api anyonya mātsaryāt anyonya atiśaya āśinaḥ tapasā toṣayitvā svam pitaram parameśvaram labdhvā sarva ātmanā tasya prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ brahma nārāyaṇau pūrvam rudraḥ kalpa antare asṛjat mahā bhagavant rudram brahmānam asṛjat punar nārāyaṇam punar brahmā brahmānam asṛjat punar evam kalpeṣu kalpeṣu brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ śṛṇu teṣām kathām citrām puṇyām pāpa pramocinīm kalpe tatpuruṣe vṛttām brahmanaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ purā nārāyaṇaḥ nāma kalpe vai meghavāhane tasya bhāvam samālakṣya viṣṇoḥ viśva jagat guruḥ haktim labdhvā tu sarvātmā śivāt sarva īśvarāt tadā sasarja bhagāvan viṣṇuḥ viśvam viśvasṛjā saha mahar tat vaibhavam dṛṣṭvā sṛṣṭaḥ tena pitāmahaḥ parayā grastaḥ prahasan idam abravīt gaccha viṣṇo mayā jñātam tava sargasya kāraṇam āvayoḥ adhikaḥ ca asti sa rudraḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ tasya deva adhidevasya prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ sraṣṭā tvam bhagavant ādyaḥ pālakaḥ paramārthāt aham ca tapasā ārādhya rudram tridaśa nāyakam tvayā saha jagant sarvam srakṣyāmi atra na saṃśayaḥ evam viṣṇum upālabhya bhagavant abja sambhavaḥ evam vijñāpayāmāsa tapasā prāpya śaṃkaram te vāma aṅga jaḥ viṣṇuḥ dakṣiṇa aṅga bhavaḥ hi aham sa matsarāt upālabdhaḥ tvad āśraya balāt mayā tasya bhaktyā yathāpūrvam prasādam kṛtavān asi tathā mama api tat sarvam dātum arhasi śaṃkaraiḥ nyāyena vai dadau sarvam tasya api saḥ ghṛṇā nidhiḥ labdhvā evam īśvarāt eva brahmā sarva ātma tām kṣaṇāt tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra tatra ananta bhoga śayyāyām śayānam paṅkaja īkṣaṇam catur bhujam udāra aṅgam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam dharā mṛdu kara ambhoja sparśa rakta pada ambujam tat tat tat tat tat yoganidrayā tamasā kālarudra ākhyam rajasā kanaka aṇḍa jam tam dṛṣṭvā puruṣam brahmā pragalbham idam abravīt grasāmi tvām aham viṣṇo tvam ātmānam yathā purā udaikṣata mahā bāhuḥ smitam īṣat cakāra ca sṛṣṭaḥ ca brahmanā sadyas bhruvoḥ madhyāt ayatnāt tasmin avasare sākṣāt bhagavant indu bhūṣaṇaḥ ha śaktim tayoḥ api draṣṭum arūpaḥ rūpam āsthitaḥ praṇematuḥ ca bahuśas bahu mānena dūratas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe brahmaviṣṇusṛṣṭikathanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca prati kalpam pravakṣyāmi rudra āvirbhāva kāraṇam yatas vicchinna saṃtānā brahma sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate brahmā brahmāṇḍa sambhavaḥ avṛddhi hetoḥ bhūtānām mumoha bhṛśa duḥkhitaḥ tasya duḥkha praśānti artham prajānām ca vivṛddhaye tad tad kalpeṣu kāla ātmā rudraḥ rudra gaṇa adhipaḥ nirdiṣṭaḥ pamameśena maheśaḥ nīlalohitaḥ putraḥ bhūtvā anugṛhṇāti brahmānam brahmaṇaḥ anujaḥ saḥ eva bhagavant īśaḥ tejorāśiḥ anāmayaḥ bhūta saṃkocakaḥ vibhuḥ tad nāma nāmā tad rūpaḥ tad kārya karaṇa kṣamaḥ tad tulya vyavahāraḥ ca tad ājñā paripālakaḥ sahasra āditya saṃkāśaḥ candra avayava bhūṣaṇaḥ tuṅga taraṃga ardha piṅgala ānana mūrdhajaḥ bhagna daṃṣṭra aṃkura ākrānta prānta kānta dharādharaḥ savya śravaṇa pārśva anta maṇḍalīkṛta kuṇḍalaḥ mahā vṛṣabha niryāṇaḥ mahā jalada niḥsvanaḥ evam ghora mahā rūpaḥ brahmaputrīm maheśvaraḥ pravāha rūpatas nityā prajā sṛṣṭiḥ pravartate kadācid prārthitaḥ sraṣṭum brahmanā nīlalohitaḥ sva ātmanā sadṛśān sarvān sasarja manasā vibhuḥ locanān jarā maraṇa nirmuktān dīpta śūla vara āyudhān tān dṛṣṭā vividhān rudrān rudram āha pitāmahaḥ namaḥ te devadeveśaiḥ mā asrākṣīḥ īdṛśāḥ prajāḥ anyāḥ sṛja tvam bhadram te prajāḥ mṛtyu samanvitāḥ iti uktaḥ prahasan prāha brahmānam parameśvaraḥ na asti mama tādṛśaḥ sargaḥ sṛja tvam aśubhāḥ prajāḥ ye tu ime manasā sṛṣṭāḥ mahātmānaḥ mahā balāḥ cariṣyanti mayā sārdham sarve eva hi yājñikāḥ iti uktvā viśvakarmāṇam viśva bhūta īśvaraḥ haraḥ saha rudraiḥ prajā sargāt nivṛtta ātmā vyatiṣṭhata tatas prabhṛti devaḥ asau na prasūte prajāḥ śubhāḥ ūrddhvaretāḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇuḥ yāvat ābhūtasaṃplavam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe rudrāvirbhāvavarṇanam nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca yadā punar prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ na vyavardhanta vedhasaḥ tadā maithuna jām sṛṣṭim brahmā kartum amanyata na nirgatam purā yasmāt nārīṇām kulam īśvarāt tena maithuna jām sṛṣṭim na śaśāka pitāmahaḥ bhajānam eva vṛddhi artham praṣṭavyaḥ parameśvaraiḥ evam saṃcintya viśvātmā tapaḥ kartum pracakrame tad ādyā paramā śaktiḥ anantā loka bhāvinī manoharā nirguṇā niṣprapañcā ca niṣkalā nirupaplavā nirantaratarā nityā nityam īśvara pārśva gā saṃcintya hṛdaye brahmā tatāpa paramam tapaḥ tīvreṇa tapasā tasya yuktasya parameṣṭhinaḥ tatas kenacid aṃśena mūrtim āviśya kām api ardhanārīśvaraḥ bhūtvā yayau devaḥ svayam haraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā paramam devam tamasaḥ param avyayam advitīyam anirdeśyam adṛśyam akṛtātmabhiḥ acalam nirguṇam śāntam ananta mahima āspadam sarva upamāna nirmuktam śaraṇyam śāśvatam śivam praṇamya daṇḍa vat brahmā samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ tuṣṭāva devam devīm ca sūktaiḥ sūkṣma artha gocaraiḥ jaya śāśvatika aiśvarye jaya śāśvatika ālaya jaya śāśvatika ākāra jaya śāśvatika anuga jaya avalokana āyatta jagat kāraṇa bṛṃhaṇaiḥ jaya deva ādya vijñeye sva ātma sūkṣma dṛśā ujjvale tathā jaya vyāpta carācare maya ji asura śiras niṣṭha śreṣṭha anuga kadambakaiḥ maya upāśrita saṃrakṣā saṃvidhāna paṭīyasi jaya unmūlita saṃsāra viṣa vṛkṣa aṅkura udgame prādeśika aiśvarya vīrya śaurya vijṛmbhaṇa jaya praṇīta pañcārtha prayoga parama amṛta jaya ji anādi mala ajñāna tamas paṭala candrike vijñāpya evaṃvidhaiḥ sūktaiḥ viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ namaścakāra rudrāya radrāṇyai ca muhur muhur idam stotra varam puṇyam brahmanā samudīritam arddhanārīśvaram nāma śivayoḥ harṣa vardhanam yaḥ idam kīrtayet bhaktyā yasya kasya api śikṣayā saḥ tat phalam avāpnoti śivayoḥ prīti kāraṇāt sakala bhuvana bhūta bhāvanābhyām janana vināśa vihīna vigrahābhyām nara vara yuvatī vapurdharābhyām satatam aham praṇataḥ asmi śaṃkarābhyām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām śivaśivāstutivarṇanam nāma paṃcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca artha saṃpanna padayā rāja lakṣaṇa yuktayā aśeṣa viṣaya ārambha rakṣā vimala dakṣayā saṃbabhāṣe su saṃpītaḥ viśvakarmāṇam īśvaraḥ paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca prajānām eva bṛddhi artham tapaḥ taptam tvayā adhunā iti uktvā parama udāram svabhāva madhuram vacaḥ sasarja vapuṣaḥ bhāgāt devīm deva varaḥ haraḥ yām āhuḥ brahma vidvasaḥ devīm divya guṇa anvitām parasya paramām śaktim bhavasya paramātmanaḥ yā bhavānī bhavasya aṅgāt samāvirabhavat kila sā bhartuḥ vapuṣaḥ bhāgāt jātā iva samadṛśyata yā sā jagat idam kṛtsnam mahimnā vyāpya tiṣṭhati śarīriṇī iva sa devī vicitram samalakṣyata sarvam jagant idam ca eṣā saṃmohayati māyayā īśvarāt sā eva jātā abhūt ajātā paramārthāt na yasyāḥ paramaḥ bhāvaḥ surāṇām api gocaraḥ ca eva bhartuḥ tām dṛṣṭvā parameśānīm sarva loka mahā īśvarām sarvajñām sarva gām sūkṣmām sat asat vyakti varjitām paramām nikhilam bhāsā bhāsayatīm idam jagant praṇipatya mahādevīm prārthayāmāsa vai virāj na vṛddhim upagacchanti sṛjyamānāḥ punar punar mithuna prabhavām eva kṛtvā sṛṣṭim atas param na nirgatam purā tvattaḥ nārīṇām kulam avyayam tena nārī kulam sraṣṭum śaktiḥ mama na vidyate sarvāsām eva śaktīnām tvattaḥ khalu samudbhavaḥ tasmāt sarvatra sarveṣām sarva śakti pradāyinīm tvām eva vara dām māyām prārthayāmi sureśvarīm evam sā yācitā devī brahmanā brahma yoninā tām ājñām parameśasya śirasā pratigṛhya sā dattvā evam atulām śaktim brahmaṇe brahma rūpiṇīm tadā prabhṛti loke asmin striyām bhogaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ brahmā api prāpa sa ānandam saṃtoṣam muni puṃgavāḥ puṇya vṛddhi karam śrāvyam puṇyam sarvam avāpnoti putrān ca labhate śubhān iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe devīśaktyudbhavaḥ nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca evam labdhvā parām śaktim īśvarāt eva śāśvatām maithuna prabhavām sṛṣṭim kartṛ kāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ yā ardhena nārī sā tasmāt śatarūpā vyajāyata sa vai svāyambhuvaḥ pūrvam puruṣaḥ manuḥ ucyate sā devī śatarūpā tu tapaḥ kṛtvā su duścaram bharttāram dīpta yaśasam manum eva anvapadyata tasmāt tu śatarūpā sā putra dvayam asūyata kanye dve ca mahābhāge yābhyām jātāḥ tu imāḥ prajāḥ mākūtiḥ ekā vijñeyā prasūtiḥ aparā smṛtā svāyambhuvaḥ prasūtim ca dadau dakṣāya tām prabhuḥ ruceḥ prajāpatiḥ ca eva cākūtim samapādayat ākūtau mithunam jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham yajñaḥ ca dakṣiṇā ca eva yābhyām saṃvartitam jagant svāyambhuva sutāyām tu prasūtau loka mātaraḥ śraddhā lakṣmī dhṛtiḥ puṣṭiḥ tuṣṭiḥ medhā kriyā tathā buddhiḥ lajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtiḥ trayodaśā patnī artham pratijagrāha dharmaḥ dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ tābhyaḥ śiṣṭāḥ yavīyasyaḥ ekādaśa su locanāḥ saṃnatiḥ ca anasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā bhṛguḥ śarvaḥ marīciḥ ca aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ tathā pulastyaḥ atriḥ viśiṣṭhaḥ ca pāvakaḥ pitaraḥ tathā khyāti ādyāḥ jagṛhuḥ kanyā munayaḥ muni sattamāḥ kāma ādyāḥ tu yaśaḥ antāḥ ye te trayodaśa sūnavaḥ dharmasya jajñire tāḥ tu śraddhā ādyāḥ su sukha uttarāḥ duḥkha uttarāḥ ca hiṃsāyām adharmasya ca saṃtatau nikṛti ādayaḥ utpannāḥ putrāḥ ca dharma lakṣaṇāḥ na eṣām bhāryāḥ ca putrāḥ vā sarve tu aniyamāḥ smṛtāḥ yā sā dakṣasya duhitrī rudrasya dayitā satī tyaktvā dākṣāyiṇīm tanum dakṣam ca dakṣa bhāryām ca vinindya saha bandhubhiḥ sā menāyām āvirabhūt putrī himavantaḥ gireḥ rudraḥ tu tām satīm dṛṣṭvā rudrān tu ātma sama prabhān yathā asṛjat asaṃkhyātān tathā kathitam eva ca bhṛgoḥ khyātau samutpannā lakṣmī nārāyaṇa priyā devau dhātṛ vidhātārau manvantara vidhāriṇaḥ tayoḥ vai putra pautra ādyāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas svāyaṃbhuve antare nītāḥ sarve te bhārgavāḥ matāḥ marīceḥ api saṃbhūtiḥ paurṇamāsam asūyata ca eva mahīyasaḥ tad anvayāḥ yeṣām vaṃśe samutpannaḥ bahuputrasya kaśyapaḥ smṛtiḥ ca aṅgirasaḥ patnī janayāmāsa vai sutau hanta śarabham ca eva tathā kanyā catuṣṭayam tadīyāḥ putra pautrāḥ ca yā iti itāḥ te sahasraśas prītau pulastya bhāryāyām dantogniḥ abhavat sutaḥ tad saṃtatīyāḥ bahavaḥ paulastyāḥ iti viśrutāḥ tu suṣuve putrān pulahasya prajāpateḥ kardamaḥ ca suriḥ ca eva sahiṣṇuḥ ca iti te trayaḥ tretāgni varcasaḥ sarve yeṣām vaṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ na eṣām bhāryāḥ ca putrāḥ ca sarve te hi ūrdhvaretasaḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ tāni sahasrāṇi vālakhilyāḥ iti smṛtāḥ atreḥ bhāryā anusūyā ca pañca ātreyān asūyata kanyakām ca śrutim nāma mātā śaṅkhapadasya ca satyanetraḥ ca havyaḥ ca āpomūrtiḥ śanaiścaraḥ somaḥ ca pañcamaḥ tu ete pañca ātreyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām putrāḥ ca pautrāḥ ca hi ātreyāṇām mahātmanām svāyaṃbhuve antare atītāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas ūrjāyām tu vasiṣṭhasya putrāḥ vai sapta jajñire ha jyāyāḥ ca svasā teṣām puṃḍarīkā sumadhyamā rajaḥ ca savanaḥ ca anayaḥ ca yaḥ sutapāḥ śukraḥ iti ete sapta saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ gotrāṇi nāmabhiḥ teṣām vāsiṣṭhānām mahātmanām svāyambhuve antare atītāni arbudāni śatāni ca iti eṣa ṛṣi sargaḥ tu sa anubandhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ samāsāt vistarāt vaktum aśakyaḥ ayam iti dvijāḥ svāhā tasya priyā lebhe putrān trīn amita ojasaḥ pāvakaḥ pavamānaḥ ca śuciḥ iti eṣa te trayaḥ nirmanthyaḥ pavamānaḥ syāt vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ sūrye tapati yaḥ ca asau śuciḥ sauraḥ udāhṛtaḥ havyavāhaḥ kavyavāhaḥ saharakṣāḥ iti trayaḥ trayāṇām kramaśas putrāḥ deva pitṛ surāḥ ca te eteṣām putra pautrāḥ ca catvāriṃśat nava eva te sarve rudra ātmakaḥ ca eva sarve rudra parāyaṇāḥ tat sarvam rudram uddiśya dattam syāt na atra saṃśayaḥ iti evam niścaya agnīnām anukrāntaḥ yathātatham yasmāt ṣaṭ ṛtavaḥ teṣām sthānam sthāna abhimāninām māsāḥ pitaraḥ tasmāt iti eṣā vaidikā śrutiḥ tvat ṛtuṣu sarve hi jāyante sthāsnu jaṅgamā evam pitR￞ṇām eteṣām ṛtu kāla abhimāninām ātma aiśvaryāḥ mahātmānaḥ tiṣṭhanti iha abbhra saṃgamāt barhiṣadaḥ pitaraḥ dvividhāḥ smṛtāḥ ayajvānaḥ ca yajvānaḥ kramāt te mṛhamedhinaḥ menām ca dharaṇīm ca eva yābhyām viśvam idam dhṛtam tad agniṣvātta sutā menā dharaṇī barhiṣad sutā menā himavantaḥ patnī mainākam krauñcam eva ca ca suṣuve bhava aṅga āśleṣa pāvanām sākṣāt śrīkaṇṭha nāthasya śivasya āvasatham gataḥ sā āsūtā dharaṇī bhūyas triṃśat kanyāḥ ca viśrutāḥ ca niyatim ca eva tṛtīyām api ca āyatim suṣuve sāgarāt velā kanyām ekām aninditām savarṇām nāma sāmudrīm patnīm prācīnabarhiṣaḥ sāmudrī suṣuve putrān daśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ sarve prācetasāḥ nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ yeṣām svāyambhuve dakṣaḥ putra tvam agamat purā tryambakasya śāpena cākṣuṣasya antare manoḥ iti ete brahma putrāṇām dharma ādīnām mahātmanām na ati saṃkṣepāt viprāḥ na ati vistarāt kramāt varṇitāḥ vai mayā vaṃśāḥ divyāḥ deva gaṇa anvitāḥ te kriyāvantaḥ prajāvantaḥ mahā ṛddhibhiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ prajānām saṃniveśaḥ ayam prajāpati samudbhavaḥ na hi śakyaḥ prasaṃkhyātum varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api rājñām api ca yaḥ vaṃśaḥ dvidhā pravartate sūryavaṃśaḥ somavaṃśaḥ iti puṇyatamaḥ kṣitau yayātiḥ nāhuṣa ādayaḥ puṇya ślokāḥ śrutāḥ ye tatra te tad vaṃśa saṃbhavāḥ anye ca rāja ṛṣayaḥ nānā vīrya samanvitā kim taiḥ phalam anutkrāntaiḥ ukta pūrvaiḥ purātanaiḥ kim ca īśvara kathā vṛttā yatra tatra anya kīrtanam prasaṅgāt īśvarasya eva prabhāva dyotanāt api iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe sṛṣṭikathanam nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ devī dakṣasya tanayā tyaktvā dākṣāyaṇī tanum katham himavantaḥ putrī menāyām abhavat purā utpannaḥ ca katham dakṣaḥ abhiśāpāt bhavasya tu cākṣuṣasya antare pūrvam manoḥ prabrūhi māruta uvāva śṛṇvantu kathayiṣyāmi dakṣasya laghu cetasaḥ purā sura asurāḥ sarve siddhāḥ ca parama ṛṣayaḥ kadācid draṣṭum īśānam himavat śikharam yayuḥ darśanam dadatuḥ teṣām deva ādīnām dvijottamāḥ xc haram draṣṭum draṣṭum ca ātma sutām satīm deva ādibhyaḥ viśeṣeṇa na kadācid abhūt smṛtiḥ tasya tasyāḥ param bhāvam ajñātuḥ ca api kevalam putrī iti evam vimūḍhasya tasyām vairam ajāyata na ajuvāha bhavam dakṣaḥ dīkṣitaḥ tām api dviṣan anyān jāmātāraḥ sarvān āhūya sa yathākramam śataśas puṣkalām arcān cakāra ca pṛthak pṛthak tathā tān saṃgatān śrutvā nāradasya mukhāt tadā yayau rudrāya rudrāṇī vijñāpya bhavanam pituḥ atha saṃnihitam divyam vimānam viśvatomukham lakṣaṇa āḍhyam sukha āroham atimātra manoharam muktā āmaya vitāna agnyam sraj dāma samalaṃkṛtam tapta kañcana nirvyūham ratna stambha śata āvṛtam puṣpa paṭṭa paristīrṇam citra ratna mahā āsanam maṇi daṇḍa manojñena mahā vṛṣabha lakṣmaṇā alaṃkṛta purobhāgam abbhra śubbhreṇa ketunā ratna kañcuka gupta aṅgaiḥ citra vetraka pāṇibhiḥ adhiṣṭhita mahā dvāram apradhṛṣyaiḥ guṇeśvaraiḥ mṛdaṅga tāla gīta ādi veṇu vīṇā viśāradaiḥ vidagdha veṣa bhāṣaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ strī janaiḥ vṛtam cāmāra vyañjanam tasyāḥ vajra daṇḍa manohare chattram śaśi nibham tasyāḥ cūḍā upari su mālinī upari amṛta bhāṇḍasya maṇḍalam śaśinaḥ yathā atha ca agre samāsīnā su smita āsyā śubhāvatī suyaśāḥ pāduke devyāḥ śubhe ratna pariṣkṛte anyā kāñcana cāru aṅgā dīptam jagrāha darpaṇam aparā tālavṛntam ca parā tāmbūla peṭikām kācid krīḍā śukam cāru kare akuruta bhāminī kācid tu su gaṇapaḥ śrīmān svayam ugra parākramaḥ bāṇa uddhāre bhujaḥ hi asya tūṇī vadana saṃgāt pratyadṛśyata valmīkam vivekṣuḥ iva pannagaḥ samuddhṛtaḥ kare tasya tad kṣaṇam ruruce śareḥ mahā bhujaṃga saṃdaṣṭaḥ yathā bāla bhuja gamaḥ bhadraḥ rudra parākramaḥ vivyādha kupitaḥ gāḍham lalāṭe viṣṇum avyayam tad abhidhā viṣṇuḥ pūrvam eva avamānitaḥ cukopa gaṇapa indrāya mṛgendrāya iva go vṛṣaḥ tatas tu aśani kalpena krūra āsyena mahā iṣuṇā bhadraḥ mahā balaḥ sa ca viṣṇuḥ punar bhadram bhadraḥ viṣṇum tathā punar sa ca tam saḥ ca tam viprāḥ śaraiḥ tau anujaghnatuḥ tayoḥ parasparam vegāt śarān āśu vimuṃcatoḥ mahān āsīt ākāśe khecara īritaḥ tatas tu anala tuṇḍena śareṇa āditya varcasā vivyādha su dṛḍham bhadraḥ viṣṇoḥ mahati vakṣasi sa tu tīvra prapātena śareṇa dṛḍham āhataḥ mahatīm rujam āsādya nipapāta vimohitaḥ punar kṣaṇāt iva utthāya labdha saṃjñaḥ tadā hariḥ sarvāṇi api ca divya astrāṇi atha enam pratyavāsṛjat sa ca viṣṇuḥ dhanus muktān sarvān śarva camūpatiḥ sahasā vārayāmāsa ghoraiḥ pratiśaraiḥ śarān tatas viṣṇuḥ sva nāma aṅkam bāṇam avyāhatam kvacid tam bāṇam bāṇa varyeṇa bhadraḥ bhadra āhvayena tu atha ekena iṣuṇā iṣuṇā śārGgam pakṣau tatas yoga balāt viṣṇuḥ dehāt devān su dāruṇān śaṅkha cakra gadā hastān visasarja sahasraśas sarvān tān kṣaṇa mātreṇa traipurān iva śaṃkaraḥ nirdadāha mahā bāhuḥ netra sṛṣṭena vahninā smayan iva gaṇeśānaḥ vyaṣṭaṃbhayat ayatnāt icchan api samutsraṣṭum na viṣṇuḥ abhavat kṣamaḥ atiṣṭhat alasaḥ bhūtvā pāṣāṇaḥ iva niścalaḥ yathā ājīvaḥ vā yathā vṛṣaḥ yathā siṃhaḥ tathā viṣṇuḥ avasthitaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā durdaśā āpannam viṣṇum indra ādayaḥ surāḥ samunnaddhāḥ gaṇa indreṇa mṛgendreṇa iva go vṛṣāḥ pragṛhīta āyudhāḥ yauddhuṃkruddhāḥ samupatasthire tān dṛṣṭvā samare bhadraḥ kṣudrān iva hariḥ mṛgān sākṣāt rudra tanuḥ vīraḥ vara vīra gaṇa āvṛtaḥ aṭṭahāsena ghoreṇa bhaya da ninditaḥ tathā śatamakhasya api sa vajraḥ dakṣiṇaḥ karaḥ sisṛkṣoḥ eva udvajraḥ citrīkṛtaḥ iva abhavat anyeṣām api sarveṣām sa raktāḥ api bāhavaḥ alasānām iva ārambhāḥ tādṛśāḥ pratiyānti uta evam bhagavantā tena vyāhata aśeṣa vaibhavāt tasya puratas sthātum akṣamāḥ vidrutān tridaśān vīrān vīrabhadraḥ mahā bhujaḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ maghaḥ varṣaiḥ iva acalān hastraiḥ cakāśire dīptaiḥ sa agni jvālāḥ iva uragāḥ astra śastrāṇi anekāni sa vīraḥ visṛjan babhau yathā tathā vīraḥ kṣaṇāt eva śaraiḥ prācchādayat diśaḥ kha maṇḍale gaṇendrasya śarāḥ kanaka bhūṣitāḥ mahantaḥ te sura gaṇān maṇḍūkān iva ḍuṃḍubhāḥ prāṇaiḥ viyojayāmāsuḥ papuḥ ca rudhira āsavam nikṛtta bāhavaḥ kecid kecid lūna vara ānanāḥ pārśve vidāritāḥ kecid nipetuḥ amarāḥ bhuvi nipetuḥ praveṣṭum iva icchantaḥ gantum iva bhūmau kecid praviviśuḥ parvatānām guhāḥ pare evam deva balam sarvam dīnam bībhatsa darśanam gaṇeśvara samutpannam kṛpaṇam vapuḥ ādade tadā tridaśa vīrāṇām asṛj salila vāhinī prāvartata nadī ghorā prāṇinām bhaya śaṃsinī rakta ārdra vasanā śyāmā hata śumbhā iva kaiśikī tasmin mahati saṃvṛtte samare bhṛśa dāruṇe petuḥ ca ulkāḥ mahā utpātāḥ śākhāḥ ca mumucuḥ drumāḥ aprasannāḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ pavanaḥ ca aśivaḥ vavau dharma ādayaḥ sadasyāḥ ca rakṣitā garuḍadhvajaḥ bhāgān ca pratigṛhṇanti sākṣāt indra ādayaḥ surāḥ tasmāt na a veda nirdiṣṭam na ca īśvara bahiṣkṛtam na asat parigṛhītam ca karma kuryāt kadācana kṛtvā api su mahat puṇyam iṣṭvā yajña śataiḥ api kṛtvā api su mahat pāpam bhaktyā yajati yaḥ śivam mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā bahunā atra kim uktena vṛthak dānam vṛthak tapaḥ tatas sa nārāyaṇakāḥ sa rudrāḥ sa lokapālāḥ samare sura oghāḥ celuḥ kvacid kecana śīrṇa keśāḥ seduḥ kvacid kecana dīrgha gātrāḥ kecid ca tatra tridaśāḥ vipannāḥ visrasta vastra ābharaṇa astra śastrāḥ babhau gaṇeśaḥ saḥ gaṇeśvarāṇām madhye sthitaḥ siṃhaḥ iva ṛṣabhānām iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe dakṣayajñavidhvaṃsavarṇanam nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca iti sañchinna bhinna aṅgāḥ devāḥ viṣṇu purogamāḥ tresuḥ stoka avaśeṣitā trastān tān samare vīrān devān anyān ca vai gaṇāḥ pramathāḥ parama kruddhāḥ vīrabhadra praṇoditāḥ pragṛhya ca tathā doṣam nigaḍaiḥ āyasaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ babandhuḥ pāṇi pādeṣu kaṃdhareṣu udareṣu ca evam vijñāpitaḥ tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā hamam jagāma saṃprītaḥ gaṇapaḥ tasya gauravāt devāḥ ca labdha avasarāḥ devadevasya mantriṇaḥ dhārayantaḥ añjalīn mūrdhani tuṣṭuvuḥ vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ ūcuḥ namaḥ śivāya śāntāya yajña hantre triśūliṇe rudra bhadrāya rudrāṇām pataye rudra bhūtaye devatānām śiras hantre dakṣasya ca durātmanaḥ saṃsargāt asya pāpasya dakṣasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ śāsitāḥ samare vīraiḥ tvayā vayam aninditā dagdhāḥ ca amī vayam sarve tvattaḥ bhītāḥ ca bho prabho tvam eva gatiḥ asmākam trāhi naḥ śaraṇa āgatān uvāca tuṣṭaḥ tu evam stutaḥ devān visṛjya nigaḍāt prabhuḥ sa gaṇaḥ sarvagaḥ śarvaḥ sarva loka maheśvaraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā parameśānam devāḥ viṣṇu purogamāḥ prītāḥ api ca bhītāḥ ca namaḥ cakruḥ maheśvaram dṛṣṭvā tān amarān bhītān praṇata ārti haraḥ haraḥ idam āha mahādevaḥ prahasan prekṣya pārvatīm uvāca mā abhaiṣṭa tridaśāḥ sarve yūyam vai māmakāḥ prajāḥ anugraha artham eva iha dhṛtaḥ daṇḍaḥ kṛpāluṇā bhavatām nirjarāṇām hi kṣāntaḥ asmābhiḥ vyatikramaḥ uvāca iti uktāḥ tridaśāḥ sarve śarveṇa amita tejasā ūcuḥ nimajjanāt mṛtaḥ prāpa sukham mihirajājaliḥ saubhāgyam atulam prāpa somavāravratāt sutān hrīkarāya dadau devaḥ svīyam padam anuttamam sudarśanam arakṣaḥ tvam nṛpa maṇḍala bhītyāḥ meduram tārayāmāsa sa dāram ca ghṛṇā nidhiḥ hāradām vidhavām cakre sa dhavām kriyayā bhavān uvāca tvam śambho kahari īśāḥ ca rajas sattva tamas guṇaiḥ bhavat kartā pātā tathā hartā jana anugraha kāṅkṣayā sarva vidyā ādi gūḍhaḥ ca sarva anugraha kārakaḥ tvattaḥ sarvam ca tvam sarvam tvayi sarvam giri īśvaraiḥ trāhi trāhi punar trāhi kṛpām kuru mama upari atha asmin antare brahmā praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ evam tu avasaram prāpya vyajñāpayata śūline mīdṛśeṣu aparādheṣu kaḥ anyaḥ tvattaḥ prasīdati yat idam devadevānām kṛta mantuṣu dūṣaṇam tat idam bhūṣaṇam manyeta aṅgīkāra gauravāt iti vijñāpyamānaḥ tu brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā deva ādīnām yathāpūrvam aṅgāni pradadau prabhuḥ prathama ādyaiḥ ca yāḥ devyaḥ daṃḍitāḥ devamātaraḥ tāsām api yathāpūrvāṇi aṅgāni giriśaḥ dadau dakṣasya bhagavān eva svayam brahmā pitāmahaḥ saṃjñām tatas labdhvā sa dṛṣṭvā jīvitaḥ sudhī bhītaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ śambhum tuṣṭāva pralapan bahu uvāca kuru kṣamasva ha mayā jñātam viśeṣeṇa viṣṇu ādi sakala īśvaraḥ tvayā eva vitatam sarvam vyāptam sṛṣṭam na nāśitam tvad adhikāḥ kecid īśāḥ te acyutaka ādayaḥ uvāca tam tathā vyākulam bhītam pralapantam kṛta āgasam smayan iva avadat prekṣya mā bhaiḥ iti ghṛṇā nidhiḥ dadau tuṣṭuvuḥ praśrayā vācā śaṃkaram girijādhipam brahma ādayaḥ ūcuḥ jaya śaṃkaraiḥ deveśaiḥ dīnānāthaiḥ mahā prabho tām kuru maheśāna aparādham no kṣamasva vai makhapāla makha adhīśaiḥ makha vidhvaṃsa kāraka pām kuru maśāna aparādham naḥ kṣamasva vai tad duṣṭa daṇḍa prada svāmin kṛpām kuru namaḥ astu te tvam prabho garva hartā vai duṣṭānām tvām a jānatām rakṣakaḥ hi viśeṣeṇa satām tvad sakta cetasām adbhutam caritam te hi niścitam kṛpayā te sarva aparādhaḥ kṣantavyaḥ vibhavaḥ dīna vatsalāḥ uvāca cakāra anugraham teṣām brahma ādīnām divaukasām dadau narān ca su prītyā śaṃkaraḥ dīna vatsalaḥ sa ca tatas tridaśān śaraṇa āgatān parama kāruṇikaḥ parameśvaraḥ anugata smita lakṣaṇayā girā śamita sarva bhayaḥ samabhāṣata uvāca iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe giriśānunayaḥ nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ kva yātaḥ kutra vāsaḥ kim kṛtvā virarāma ha uvāca mahīdhara varaḥ śrīmān mandaraḥ citra kandaraḥ tapaḥ mahat kṛtam tena voḍhum sva śirasā śivau na śakyam vistarāt vaktum varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api parvata antara saundaryam sādhāraṇa vidhāraṇāt ṛddhyā kayā api saundaryam īśvara āvāsa yogya tā atīva ramaṇīyaḥ ayam giriḥ antaḥpurīkṛtaḥ pitṛbhyām jagantaḥ nityam snāna pāna upayogāt adhirājyena ca adrīṇām adrīreṣaḥ abhiṣicyate niśāsu śikhara prāntar vartinā sa śiloccayaḥ candreṇa acalaiḥ sāmrājya chattreṇa iva virājate sa śailaḥ cañcalībhūtaiḥ bālaiḥ ca amara yoṣitām darpaṇe deha saubhāgyam draṣṭu kāmaḥ iva sthitaḥ kūjat vihaṃga vācālaiḥ vāta uddhṛta latā bhujaiḥ maya āśiṣā saha abhyarcya niṣevyate iva adrirāj prapatan iva pātāle bhū pṛṣṭhāt utpatan iva ajīrṇa lāvaṇya tayā jṛṃbhamāṇaḥ iva acalaḥ bhūmayaḥ tāḥ tāḥ darpaṇa pratimā udarāḥ tiraskṛta ātapāḥ snigdha āśrama chāyā mahīruhāḥ sarit saras taḍāga ādi samparka śiśira anilāḥ tatra tatra niṣaṇṇābhyām śivābhyām saphalīkṛtāḥ tam imam sarvatas śreṣṭham smṛtvā sa ambaḥ tryambakaḥ raibhya āśrama samīpa sthaḥ ca antardhānam gataḥ yayau rarāma ramaṇīyāsu devyā antaḥpura bhūmiṣu tathā gateṣu kāleṣu pravṛddhāsu prajāsu ca daityau śumbha niśumbha ākhyau bhrātarau saṃbabhūvatuḥ tābhyām tapaḥ balāt dattam brahmanā parameṣṭinā tu yā kanyā hi ambikā aṃśa samudbhavā ajāta puṃsparśa ratiḥ avilaṅghya parākramā tayā tu āvayoḥ vadhaḥ saṃkhye tasyām kāma abhibhūtayoḥ tatas prabhṛti śakra ādīn vijitya samare surān niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāram jagant cakratuḥ akramāt tathā tad varṇa kośa jām śaktim akāmām kanyakā ātmakām kāli iti āha rahasyam vām nindayan iva sa smitaḥ tatas kruddhā tadā devī suvarṇā varṇa kāraṇāt smayatī ca āha bhartāram asamādheyayā girā yam eva avantam ciram kālam katham eṣā niyamyate yā ca na abhimatā bhartuḥ api sarva aṅga sundarā sā vṛthak eva hi jāyeta sarvaiḥ api guṇa antaraiḥ tathā asatī anyathābhūtā nārī kutra upayujyate varṇa antaram bhajiṣye vā na bhajiṣyāmi vā svayam iti uktvā utthāya śayanāt devī sā ācaṣṭa gadgadam pādayoḥ praṇaman eva bhavānīm pratyabhāṣata paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca a jānatī ca krīḍā uktim priye kim kupitā asi mama pṛthagjanānām rataye kāma ātmā kalpitaḥ mayā tatas katham upālabdhaḥ kāma dāhāt aham tvayā mām vai tridaśa sāmānyam manyamānaḥ manobhavaḥ vihāraḥ upya āvayoḥ asya jagantaḥ trāṇa kāraṇāt śruta pūrvam hi bhagavan te cāṭu vacaḥ mayā prāṇān api apriyā bhartuḥ nārī yā na parityajet kula aṅganā śubhā sadbhiḥ kutsitā eva hi gamyate tad uktiḥ api kāli iti ghaṭate katham anyathā uvāca mama icchayā sva icchayā vā varṇa antaravatī bhava brahmānam tapasā ārādhya kṣipram gaurī bhavāmi aham paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca mad prasādāt purā brahmā brahma tvam prāptavan purā tam āhūya mahādevi tapasā kim kariṣyasi tathā api ārādhya tapasā brahmānam tvad niyogāt purā kila satī nāmnā dakṣasya duhitrī abhavam jagantām patim evam tvā patim prāptavatī tathā na tām nirbandhayāmāsa deva kārya cikīrṣayā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śivamandaragirinivāsakrīḍoktavarṇanam nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tatas pradakṣiṇīkṛtya patim ambā pativratā tapaḥ kṛtavatī pūrvam deśe yasmin sakhī janaiḥ tatas sva pitaram dṛṣṭvā mātaram ca tayoḥ gṛhe praṇamya vṛttam vijñāpya tābhyām ca anumatā satī punar tapaḥ vanam gatvā bhūṣaṇāni visṛjya ca snātvā tapasvinaḥ veṣam kṛtvā parama pāvanam saṃkalpya ca mahā tīvram tapaḥ parama duścaram tam eva kṣaṇike liṅge dhyātvā bāhya vidhānāt tathā tapaḥ caratīm tām kāle bahutithe gate dṛṣṭaḥ kaścid mahā vyāghraḥ duṣṭa bhāvāt upāgamat gātram citra arpitam iva stabdham tasyāḥ sakāśatas tam dṛṣṭvā api tathā vyāghram duṣṭa bhāvāt upāgatam sa tu viṣṭabdha sarva aṅgaḥ bubhukṣā paripīḍitaḥ nirīkṣyamāṇaḥ satatam devīm eva tadā aniśam devyāḥ ca hṛdaye nityam mama eva ayam upāsakaḥ trātā ca duṣṭa sattvebhyaḥ iti pravavṛte kṛpā tasyāḥ eva kṛpā yogāt sadyas naṣṭa mala trayaḥ babhūva sahasā vyāghraḥ devīm ca bubudhe tadā tadā parama bhāvena jñātvā kārtārthyam ātmanaḥ duṣṭānām api sattvānām tathā anyeṣām durātmanām tapaḥ ca vavṛdhe devyāḥ tīvram tīvratara ātmakam devāḥ ca daitya nirbandhāt brahmānam śaraṇam gatāḥ cakruḥ nivedanam devāḥ sva duḥkhasya ari pīḍanāt saḥ api śrutvā vidhiḥ duḥkham surāṇām kṛpayā anvitaḥ bhāsīt daitya vadhāya eva smṛtvā hetu āśrayām kathām dadarśa ca suraśreṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhe tapasi niṣṭhitām pratiṣṭhām iva viśvasya bhavānīm parameśvarīm rudrasya ca pituḥ bhāryām āryām adrīśvara ātmajām brahmānam āgatam dṛṣṭvā devī deva gaṇaiḥ saha tapas phalānām sarveṣām tvad adhīnāḥ hi siddhayaḥ bhartāram ātmanā prāpya prāptam ca tapasaḥ phalam sarga ādau bhavataḥ devāt utpattiḥ śrūyate yadā tadā prajānām prathamaḥ tvam mama prathama jaḥ sutaḥ yadā punar prajā vṛddhyai lalāṭāt bhavataḥ bhavaḥ tvam mama guruḥ śvaśura bhāvataḥ tat īdṛśasya bhavataḥ lokayātrā vidhāyinaḥ kim atra bahunā dehe yaḥ ca ayam mama kālimā etāvatā kim arthena tīvram devi tapaḥ kṛtam sva icchā eva kim aparyāptā krīḍā iyam hi tava īdṛśā atas mama iṣṭam anayā phalam kim api sādhyatām niśumbha śumbha nāmnau daityau datta varau mayā alam vilambanena atra tvam kṣaṇena sthirā bhava brāhmaṇa abhyarthitā ca eva devī giri vara ātmajā tvac kośam sahasā utsṛjya gaurī sā samajāyata sā tvac kośa ātmanā utsṛṣṭā kauśikī nāma nāmataḥ kālī kāla ambuda prakhyā kanyakā samapadyata sā tu māyā ātmakā śaktiḥ yoganidrā ca vaiṣṇavī mahā cakra triśūla ādi sa āyudha aṣṭa mahā bhujā saumyā ghorā ca miśrā ca trinetrā candraśekharā ajāta puṃsparśa ratiḥ adhṛṣyā ca ati sundarā dattā ca brahmaṇe devyā śaktiḥ eṣā sanātanā niśumbhasya ca śumbhasya nihantrī daitya siṃhayoḥ brahmaṇā api prahṛṣṭena tasyai parama śaktaye ca māṃsaiḥ matsyaiḥ apūpaiḥ ca nirvartya asau samādiśat sā ca eva saṃmatā śaktiḥ brahmanaḥ viśvakarmaṇaḥ praṇamya mātaram gaurīm brahmānam ca anupūrvaśas śaktibhiḥ ca api tulyābhiḥ sva ātmajābhiḥ anekaśas tad bāṇaiḥ kāma bāṇaiḥ ca chinna bhinna aṅga mānasau mā ūhanīyam parasmāt ca prastutam varṇayāmi vaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe devīgauratvabhavanam nāma paṃcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca utpādya kauśikīm gaurī brahmaṇe pratipādya tām dṛṣṭaḥ kim eṣa bhavatā śārdūlaḥ mad upāśrayaḥ bhavitavyam anena atas mama antaḥpura cāriṇā dāsyati pradīyatām anujñā mama prajānām patinā tvayā tasya tīvraiḥ purāvṛttaiḥ daurātmyam samavarṇayat paśau devi mṛgāḥ krūrāḥ kva ca te anugrahaḥ śubhaḥ māśīviṣa mukhe sākṣāt amṛtam kim niṣicyate vyāghra mātreṇa san eṣa duṣṭaḥ kaḥ api niśācaraḥ bhakṣitāḥ gāvaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca tapodhanāḥ tarpayan tān yathākāmam kāmarūpī carati asau avaśyam khalu bhoktavyam phalam pāpasya karmaṇaḥ atas kim kṛpayā kṛtyam īdṛśeṣu durātmasu anena devyāḥ kim kṛtyam prakṛtyā kaluṣa ātmanā yat uktam bhavatā sarvam tathyam astu ayam īdṛśaḥ tathā api mām prapannaḥ abhūt na tyājyaḥ mām upāśritaḥ puṇya karmā api kim kuryāt tvadīya ajñāna apekṣayā tvam eva parameśvarī tvad adhīnā hi sarveṣām bandha mokṣa vyavasthitiḥ tvat ṛte paramā śaktiḥ saṃsiddhiḥ kasya karmaṇā tvam eva vividhā śaktiḥ bhavānām atha vā svayam aśaktaḥ karma karaṇe kartā vā kim kariṣyati viṣṇoḥ ca mama ca anyeṣām deva dānava rakṣasām tad tad aiśvarya samprāptaye te eva ājñā hi kāraṇam atītāḥ khalu asaṃkhyātāḥ brahmāṇaḥ harayaḥ bhavāḥ anāgatāḥ tu asaṃkhyātāḥ tvad ājñā anuvidhāyinaḥ tvām an ārādhya deveśi puruṣa artha catuṣṭayam sukṛtam duṣkṛtam ca api tvayā iva sthāpitam yatas anādi madhya nidhanā śaktiḥ ādyā sanātanā samasta lokayātrā artham mūrtim āviśya kām api tvam krīḍase vividhaiḥ bhāvaiḥ kaḥ tvā jānāti tattvāt iti ātmanaḥ param bhāvam smārayitvā anurūpatas devīm ca mātaram dṛṣṭvā menām himavantā saha praṇamya āśvāsya bahudhā pitarā viraha asahau viprayoga śucā iva agre puṣpa bāṣpam vimuṃcataḥ tad tuccha ākhā samārūḍha vihagaḥ dīritaiḥ rutaiḥ bahudhā dīnam vilāpam iva kurvataḥ sarveṣām jagantām dhātā kartā pātā vināśa kṛt iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe vyāghragativarṇanam nāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ kṛtvā gauram vapuḥ divyam devī giri vara ātmajā katham dadarśa bhartāram praviṣṭā manditam satī uvāca añjasā yena praṇaya garbhena bhāvaḥ bhāvavatām hṛtaḥ mānā praviṣṭā antar tat ca sā samapaśyata praṇamya na utthitā yāvat tāvat tām parameśvaraḥ pragṛhya dorbhyām āśliṣya paritas parayā mudā sva aṅke dhartum pravṛttā api sā paryaṅke nyaṣīdata tayā sambhāṣaṇāya īśaḥ pūrva bhāṣitam abravīt sā daśā ca vyatītā kim te sarva aṅga sundari sva icchayā api na kālī iti na anya varṇavatī iti ca tvad svabhāva āhṛtam cittam subhru cintā āvaham mama aham agni śiraḥ niṣṭhaḥ tvam soma śirasi sthitā agnīṣoma ātmakam viśvam āvābhyām samadhiṣṭhitam jagat hitāya caratoḥ sva icchā dhṛta śarīrayoḥ tvam hi vāc amṛtam sākṣāt aham artha amṛtam param katham na karmaṇā sṛjāmi idam jagant pratisṛjāmi ca sarvasya ājñā eka labhya tvāt ājñā tvam hi garīyāḥ mā ājñā eka sāram aiśvaryam yasmāt svātantrya lakṣaṇam kīdṛśam devānām kāryam uddiśya līlā uktim kṛtavan aham iti priyaṃvade sākṣāt īśvare parameśvare śṛṃgāra bhāva sārāṇām janma bhūmiḥ akṛtrimā lajjayā na kim api ūce kauśikī varṇanāt param tat eva varṇayāmi adya śṛṇu devyāḥ ca varṇanam kim devena na sā dṛṣṭā yā sṛṣṭā kauśikī mayā tādṛśā kanyakā loke na bhūtā na bhaviṣyati tasyāḥ vīryam balam vindhya nilayam vijayam tathā hasya ca niśumbhasya māraṇe ca raṇe tayoḥ lokānām rakṣaṇam śaśvat brahmā vijñāpayiṣyati iti saṃbhāṣamāṇāyāḥ devyāḥ eva ājñayā tadā vyāghraḥ sakhinā samānīya puras avasthāpitaḥ tadā tam prekṣya āha punar devī deva ānītam upāyatam vyāghram paśya na ca anena sadṛśaḥ mad upāsakaḥ atīva mama bhaktaḥ ca viśrabdhaḥ ca sva rakṣaṇāt sva deśam ca parityajya prasāda artham samāgataḥ yadi prītiḥ abhūt mattaḥ parām prītim karoṣi me uvāca madhuram praṇaya udarkam śrutvā devyāḥ śubham vacaḥ prītaḥ asmi iti āha tam devaḥ sa ca adṛśyata tad kṣaṇāt churikām uraga prakhyām gaṇeśaḥ rakṣa veṣa dhṛk somanandī iti vikhyātaḥ tasmāt eṣa samākhyayā ittham devyāḥ priyam kṛtvā devaḥ ca ṛddha indu bhūṣaṇaḥ bhūṣayāmāsa tat divyaiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ ratna bhūṣitaiḥ tatas saḥ gaurīm giriśaḥ girīndrajām sa gauravām sarva manoharām haraḥ paryaṅkam āropya varāṅga bhūṣaṇaiḥ vibhūṣayāmāsa śaśāṅka bhūṣaṇaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ devīm samādadhānena devena idam kim īritam agniṣoma ātmakam viśvam vāc artha ātmakam iti api mad ājñā eka sāram aiśvaryam ājñā tvam iti ca uditam tat idam śrotum icchāmaḥ yathāvat anupūrvaśas uvāca mayaḥ śaktyāḥ śānti karā tanuḥ amṛtam yat pratiṣṭhā sā tejaḥ vidyā kalā svayam bhūta sūkṣmeṣu sarveṣu te eva rasa tejasī dvividhā tejasaḥ vṛtti sūrya ātmā ca anala ātmakā tathā eva rasa vṛttiḥ ca soma ātmā ca jala ātmakā haviṣe sasya sampattiḥ vṛṣṭiḥ sasya abhivṛddhaye tasmāt eva haviḥ tasmāt agnīṣoma dhṛtam jagat agniḥ ūrdhvam jvalati eṣa yāvat saumyam para amṛtam yāvat ādahanam ca ūrdhvam adhas ca āplāvanam bhavet ādhāra śaktyā eva dhṛtaḥ kālāgniḥ ayam ūrdhva gaḥ tathā eva nimna gaḥ sa umaḥ śiva śakti pada āspadaḥ śivaḥ ca ūrddhvam adhas śaktiḥ ūrddhvam śaktiḥ adhas śivaḥ tat ittham śiva śaktibhyām na avyāptam iha kiṃcana yaḥ ca ittham bhasma sadbhāvam jñātvā snāti ca bhasmanā śāktena amṛtavarṣeṇa ca adhikārān nivartayet atas mṛtyuṃjayāya ittham amṛta plāvanam sadā agnīṣoma padam hitvā na saḥ bhūyas abhijāyate śiva agninā tanum dagdhvā śakti saumyā mṛtena yaḥ agnīṣoma ātmakam viśvam jagant iti anurūpatas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe bhasmatattvavarṇanam nāma aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca nivedayāmi jagataḥ vāc arthātmyam kṛtam yathā ṣaḍadhva vedanam samyak samāsāt na tu vistarāt na asti kaścid aśabda arthaḥ na api śabdaḥ nirarthakaḥ prakṛteḥ pariṇāmaḥ dvidhā śabda artha bhāvanā tām āhuḥ prākṛtām mūrtim śivayoḥ parama ātmanoḥ śabda ātmakā vibhūtiḥ yā sā tridhā kathyate budhaiḥ sthūlā sūkṣmā parā ca iti sthūlā yā śruti gocarā sūkṣmā cintā mayā proktā cintayā rahitā parā yā śaktiḥ sā parā śaktiḥ śivatattva samāśrayā sarva śakti samaṣṭi ātmā śakti tattva samākhyayā samasta kārya jātasya mūlaprakṛti tām gatā sā eva kuṇḍalinī māyā śuddha adhva paramā satī sā vibhāga svarūpā eva ṣaḍadhva ātmā vijṛṃbhate tatra śabdāḥ trayaḥ adhvānaḥ trayaḥ ca arthāḥ samīritāḥ sarveṣām api vai puṃsām naija śuddhi anurūpatas parasyāḥ prakṛtyāḥ ādau pañcadhā pariṇāmāt kalāḥ ca tāḥ nivṛttya ādyāḥ paryāptāḥ iti niścayaḥ mantrādhvā ca padādhvā ca varṇādhvā ca iti śabdāt bhuvana adhvā ca tattva adhvā kalā adhvā ca arthāt kramāt atra anyonyam ca sarveṣām vyāpya vyāpaka tā ucyate mantrāḥ sarvaiḥ padaiḥ vyāptāḥ vākya bhāvāt padāni ca āhuḥ varṇāḥ tu bhuvanaiḥ vyāptāḥ teṣām teṣu upalambhanāt vyāptāni kāraṇaiḥ tattvaiḥ ārabdha tvāt anekaśas paurāṇikāni ca anyāni vijñeyāni śiva āgame śivaśāstra prasiddhāni tatonyāni api kṛtsnaśas parasyāḥ prakṛtyāḥ ādau pañcadhā pariṇāmāt kalāḥ ca tāḥ nivṛttya ādyāḥ vyāptāḥ pañca yathottaram atas parā śaktiḥ avibhaktā ṣaḍadhvanām yathā śaivam tat paramam dhāma yat prāpyam ṣaḍbhiḥ adhvabhiḥ mātrā śaktiḥ pañcatattva viśodhanāt tat ūrdhvam vidyayā madhye yāvat viśveśvara avadhi tad ūrdhvam madhu ante viśuddhiḥ śānti atītayā yām āhuḥ paramam vyom para prakṛti yogāt śaktipāta samāyogāt ṛte tattvāni tattvāt tad vyāptiḥ tad vivṛddhiḥ ca jñātum evam na śakyate marameśvarī tiṣṭhati akhilam yayā kāraṇa bhūtayā na ātmanaḥ na eva māyā eṣā na vikāraḥ vicārāt sarva aiśvarya parākāṣṭā śivasya vyabhicāriṇī samāna dharmiṇī tasya taiḥ taiḥ bhāvaiḥ viśeṣataḥ sa tayā eva gṛhī sā api tena eva gṛhiṇī sadā ekaḥ eva śivaḥ sākṣāt dvidhā asau samavasthitaḥ tu parā śaktiḥ śivasya samavāyinī tasmāt śivaḥ paraḥ hetuḥ tasya ājñā parameśvarī tayā eva preritā śaivī mūlaprakṛtiḥ avyayā mahāmāyā ca māyā ca prakṛtiḥ triguṇā iti ca trividhā kārya vedhena sā prasūte ṣaḍadhvanaḥ sa vāc artha mayaḥ ca adhvā ṣaḍvidhaḥ nikhilam jagant tasya eva vistaram prāhuḥ śāstra jātam aśeṣatas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe vāgarthakatattvavarṇanam nāma ekonatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ caritāni vicitrāṇi gṛhyāṇi gahanāni ca durvijñeyāni devaiḥ ca mohayanti manāṃsi naḥ brahma ādayaḥ lokānām sṛṣṭi sthiti anta hetavaḥ yadi evam īdṛśa aiśvaryam tat tu svātantrya lakṣaṇam mūrta ātmā sakalaḥ kaścid sa ca anyaḥ niṣphalaḥ śivaḥ mūrti ātmā eva tadā mūrtiḥ śivasya asya bhavet iti anyathā nirapekṣeṇa mūrtiḥ svīkriyate katham mūrti svīkaraṇam tasmāt mūrtau sādhya phala īpsayā sva icchā eva tādṛśā puṃsām yasmāt karma anusāriṇī brahma ādayaḥ piśāca antāḥ kim te karma ativartinaḥ icchayā deha nirmāṇam indrajāla upamam viduḥ aṇima ādi guṇa aiśvarya vaśīkāra anatikramāt mahā rūpam dadhat viṣṇuḥ dadhīcena mahā ṛṣiṇā śarīravat tayā anya ātma sādharmyam pratibhāti naḥ sarva anugrāhakam prāhuḥ śivam parama kāraṇam sa nirgṛhṇāti devānām sarva anugrāhakaḥ katham ciccheda bahuśas devaḥ brahmaṇaḥ pañcamam śiraḥ api deva strīṣu ca deveṣu dakṣasya adhvara kāraṇāt hi krośatām eva devānām hutaḥ netra hutāśane sa prekṣya devena tad kṣaṇe bhasmasātkṛtaḥ malaṃdhara asuraḥ dīrṇaḥ cakrīkṛtya jalam padā baddhvā anantena yaḥ viṣṇum cikṣepa śata yojanam tam eva jala saṃdhāyī śūlena eva jaghāna saḥ jighāṃsatām surārīṇām kulam nirghṛṇa cetasām triśūleṇa andhakasya uraḥ śikhinā eva upatāpitam kaṇṭhāt kāla aṅganām sṛṣṭvā dārakaḥ api nipātitaḥ tu gauryāḥ tvac kośa gocarām śumbhaḥ saha niśumbhena prāpitaḥ maraṇam raṇe śrutam ca mahat ākhyānam skānde skanda samāśrayam vihṛtya su ciram devyāḥ vihārāḥ rasām rasātalam nītām iva kṛtvā abhidhām tatas devīm ca vañcayan tasyām sva vīrya mati durvaham a visṛjya visṛjya agnau haviḥ pūtam iva amṛtam svāhayā kṛttikā rūpāt sva bhartrā ramamāṇayā suvarṇībhūtayā nyastam merau śaravaṇe kvacid saṃdīpayitvā kālena tasya bhāsā diśaḥ daśa rañjayitvā girīn sarvān kāñcanīkṛtya meruṇā sukumāra aṅge kumārāṇām nidarśane tat śaiśavam svarūpam ca tasya dṛṣṭvā manoharam devaḥ api svayam āyātaḥ putra darśana lālasaḥ pīta amṛtam iva sneha vivaśena antarātmanā anubhūya ca tad krīḍām saṃbhāvya ca parasparam stanyam ājñāpayan devyāḥ pāyayitvā amṛta upamam tava avatāraḥ jagantām hitāya iti anuśāsya ca tatas śakreṇa saṃdhāya bibhyatā tāraka asurāt kārayitvā abhiṣekam ca senāpatye divaukasām cheditam tārakasya api śiraḥ śakra bhyā saha stutim cakruḥ viśeṣeṇa hari dhātṛ mukhāḥ surāḥ tathā rakṣodhipaḥ sākṣāt rāvaṇaḥ bala garvitaḥ pada aṅguṣṭha parispandāt mamajja mṛditaḥ bhuvi baṭoḥ kenacid arthena sva āśritasya gata āyuṣaḥ sva vāhanam a vijñāya vṛṣa indram vaḍavānalaḥ śāntaḥ eva sadā sarvam anugṛhṇāti ced śivaḥ kāraṇam khalu karma api bhavet īśvara kāritam iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śivatattvapraśnaḥ nāma triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca jijñāsā hi na nāstikyam sādhayet sādhu buddhiṣu asatām tu anyathābhāvaḥ prasādena vinā prabhoḥ param sarvam anugrāhyam paśu pāśa ātmakam jagant parasya anugraha artham tu pateḥ ājñā samanvayaḥ patiḥ ājñāpakaḥ sarvam anugṛhṇāti sarvadā atas svātantrya śabdārthān anapekṣa tva lakṣaṇaḥ mūrta ātmanaḥ api anugrāhyā śiva ajñāna nivartanāt ajñāna dhiṣṭhitam śambhoḥ na kiṃcid iha vidyate sa mūrti ātmā śivaḥ śaiva mūrtiḥ iti upacaryate na hi asau niṣkalaḥ sākṣāt śivaḥ parama kāraṇam sa ākāreṇa anubhāvena kena api anupalakṣitaḥ pramāṇa gamya tā mātram tad svabhāva upapādakam na tāvatā atra upekṣā dhī upalakṣaṇam antarā ātma upama ulvaṇam sākṣāt mūrtiḥ eva hi kācana mūrtiḥ mūrti ātmā paraḥ tasya upalakṣaṇam yathā kāṣṭheṣu an ārūḍhaḥ na vahniḥ upalabhyate evam śivaḥ api mūrti ātmani anārūḍhaḥ iti sthitiḥ yathā agnim ānaya iti ukte jvalat kāṣṭhāt ṛte svayam tadvat pūjyaḥ mūrti ātmanā śivaḥ mūrti ātmani kṛtam sākṣāt śive eva kṛtam yatas liṅga ādau api tat kṛtyam arcāyām ca viśeṣataḥ yathā anugṛhyate saḥ mūrti ātmā pārameṣṭhinā tathā mūrti ātma niṣṭhena śivena paśavaḥ vayam loka anugrahaṇāya eva śivena parameṣṭhinā sadāśiva ādayaḥ sarve mūrti ātmanaḥ api adhiṣṭhitāḥ viśeṣataḥ tattva atattva svarūpeṣu mūrti ātmasu śiva anvayaḥ bhogaḥ karma vipāka ātmā sukha duḥkha ātmakaḥ mataḥ sarvam śivaḥ anugṛhṇāti na nigṛhṇāti kiṃcana nigṛhṇatām tu ye doṣāḥ śive teṣām asaṃbhavāt ye punar nigrahāḥ kecid brahma ādiṣu nidarśitāḥ te api loka hitāya eva kṛtāḥ śrīkaṇṭha mūrtinā brahmāṇḍasya ādhipatyam hi śrīkaṇṭhasya na saṃśayaḥ mūrtim krīḍatīm adhitiṣṭhati sa doṣāḥ eva deva ādyāḥ nigṛhītāḥ yathā uditam tatas te api vipāpmānaḥ prajāḥ ca api gata jvarāḥ nigrahaḥ sva rūpeṇa viduṣām na jugupsitaḥ atas eva hi daṇḍyeṣu daṇḍaḥ rājñām praśasyate na saḥ ced īśatām kuryāt jagantaḥ katham īśvaraḥ īśa icchā ca vidhātṛ tvam vidheḥ ājñāpanam param mājñā vaśyam idam kuryāt na kuryāt iti śāsanam tad śāsana anuvarti tvam sādhu bhāvasya lakṣaṇam viparīta samādhoḥ syāt na sarvam tat tu dṛśyate sādhu saṃrakṣaṇīyam ced vinivartyam asādhu yat hita artha lakṣaṇam ca idam daṇḍa antam anuśāsanam hite sadā niṣaṇṇānām īśvarasya nidarśanam ayukta kāriṇaḥ loke garhaṇīyā aviveki tā na hi dveṣṭi pitā putram yaḥ nigṛhya ati śikṣayet mādhyasthena api nigrāhyā anyaḥ nigṛhṇāti mārgāt tasmāt duḥkha ātmakām hiṃsām kurvāṇaḥ yaḥ sa nirghṛṇaḥ nidāna jñasya bhiṣajaḥ rugṇaḥ hiṃsām prayuṃjataḥ na kiṃcid api nairghṛṇyam ghṛṇā eva atra prayojakā ghṛṇā api na guṇāya eva hiṃsreṣu pratiyogiṣu tādṛśeṣu ghṛṇī bhrāntyā ghṛṇā antarita nirghṛṇaḥ upekṣā api iha doṣā āha rakṣyeṣu pratiyogiṣu doṣa ābhāsān samutprekṣya phalatas nirghṛṇaḥ tasmāt ghṛṇā guṇāya eva sarvathā iti na saṃmatam mūrti ātmasu api rāga ādyāḥ doṣāḥ santi eva vastutas agnau api samāviṣṭam tāmram khalu sa kālikam iti na agniḥ asau duṣyet tāmra saṃsarga kāraṇāt na agneḥ aśuci saṃsargāt aśuci tvam apekṣate evam śodhya ātma saṃsargāt na hi aśuddhaḥ śivaḥ bhavet ayasi agnau samāviṣṭe dāhaḥ agneḥ eva na ayasaḥ mūrta ātmani evam aiśvaryam īśvarasya eva na ātmanām kāṣṭhasya aṅgāra tā na agneḥ evam atra api yojyatām atas eva jaganti asmin kāṣṭha pāṣāṇa mṛtsu api śiva āveśa vaśāt eva śiva tvam upacaryate maitrī ādayaḥ guṇāḥ gauṇāḥ tasmāt te bhinna vṛttayaḥ taiḥ guṇaiḥ uparaktānām doṣāya ca guṇāya ca yat tu gauṇam agauṇam ca tat sarvam anugṛhṇataḥ na guṇāya na doṣāya śivasya guṇa vṛttayaḥ na ca anugraha śabda artham gauṇam āhuḥ vipaścitaḥ saṃsāra mocanam kim tu śaivam ājñā mayam hitam hitam tat ājñā karaṇam yat hitam tat anugrahaḥ sarvam hite niyuñjāvaḥ sarva anugraha kārakaḥ tasya api hita rūpa tvāt śivaḥ sarva upakārakaḥ yathā vikāsayati eva raviḥ padmāni bhānubhiḥ svabhāvaḥ api hi bhāvānām bhāvinaḥ arthasya kāraṇam suvarṇam eva na aṅgāram drāvayati agni saṃgamaḥ svabhāva vimalaḥ yadvat sarva anugrāhakaḥ śivaḥ svabhāva malināḥ tadvat ātmanaḥ jīva saṃjñitāḥ māgantuka tve kasya api bhāvyam kena api hetunā baddhāḥ muktāḥ pare yatas bhajante yānti kecid mūrti ātma tām yānti kecid āsanna gocarāḥ mūrti ātmasu śivāḥ kecid adhvanām mūrdhasu sthitāḥ madhye maheśvarāḥ rudrāḥ tu arvācīna pade sthitāḥ pratipad api ca māyāyāḥ parasmāt kāraṇāt trayam tatra api ātmā sthitaḥ adhastāt antarātmā ca madhyatas parastāt paramātmā iti brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ vartante vasavaḥ kecid paramātma pada āśrayāḥ śānti atīta pade śaivāḥ śānte māheśvare tatas tu nivṛttau ca tathā ātmānaḥ brahmā brahma aṅga yonayaḥ pakṣi ādayaḥ adhamāḥ pañcayonayaḥ tāḥ caturdaśa malaḥ yathā āma bhāvaḥ muktasya pūrvam paścāt tu pakva tā malaḥ api āmaḥ ca pakvaḥ ca bhavet saṃsāra kāraṇam madhye tu adhara tā puṃsām pakve tu uttara tā kramāt paśu ātmānaḥ tridhā bhinnāḥ eka dvi tri malāḥ kramāt atra uttarāḥ eka malāḥ dvi malāḥ madhyamāḥ matāḥ tri malāḥ tu adhamāḥ jñeyāḥ yathottaram adhiṣṭhitāḥ yathā aṇḍa antā hi mahā bhūmiḥ śata rudra ādi adhiṣṭhitā māyā antam antarikṣam tu hi amara īśa ādibhiḥ kramāt mahāmāyā avasānā dyauḥ vāyu ādyaiḥ bhuvana adhipaiḥ anāśrita antaiḥ adhva antarvartibhiḥ samadhiṣṭhitāḥ te hi sākṣāt diviṣadaḥ tu antarikṣa sadaḥ tathā pṛthivī padaḥ iti evam devā deva vrataiḥ stutā nidāna bhūtaiḥ saṃsāra rogaḥ puṃsām pravartate bhiṣaj ājñāpakaḥ śambhuḥ śivaḥ parama kāraṇam aduḥkhena a api śaktaḥ asau paśūn mocayitum śivaḥ katham duḥkham karoti iti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā katham duḥkham aduḥkham syāt svabhāvaḥ hi aviparyayaḥ na hi rogī hi arogī syāt bhiṣaj bhaiṣajya kāraṇāt evam svabhāva malinān svabhāvāt duḥkhinaḥ paśūn sva ajña auṣadha vidhānena duḥkhāt mocayate śivaḥ na bhiṣaj kāraṇam roge śivaḥ saṃsāra kāraṇam duḥkhe svabhāva saṃsiddhe katham tad kāraṇam śivaḥ svābhāvikaḥ malaḥ puṃsām saḥ hi saṃsārayati amūn saṃsāra kāraṇam yat tu malam māyā ādi acetanam yathā maṇiḥ ayaskāntaḥ sāṃnidhyāt upakārakaḥ na nivartayitum śakyam sāṃnidhyam sat akāraṇam tatas nityam ajñātaḥ jagantaḥ śivaḥ śaktiḥ rājñā ātmakā tasya niyantrī viśvatomukhā tayā tatam idam śaśvat tathā api saḥ na duṣyati anidam prathamam sarvam īśitavyam saḥ īśvaraḥ īśanāt ca tadīya ājñā tathā api saḥ na duṣyati etasmin antare vyomnaḥ śrutāḥ vāgarīriṇī tatas hṛṣṭatarāḥ sarve vinaṣṭa aśeṣa saṃśayāḥ munayaḥ vismaya āviṣṭāḥ preṇemuḥ pavanam prabhum na ete pratiṣṭhita jñānāḥ iti matvā evam abravīt uvācva parokṣam aparokṣam ca dvividham jñānam iṣyate hetu upadeśa gamyam yat tat parokṣam pracakṣate aparokṣam punar śreṣṭhāt anuṣṭhānāt bhaviṣyati na aparokṣāt ṛte mokṣaḥ iti kṛtvā viniścayam hi śreṣṭha anuṣṭhāna siddhi artham prayatadhvam atandritāḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe jñānopadeśaḥ nāma ekatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ kim tat śreṣṭam anuṣṭhānam mokṣaḥ yena parokṣitaḥ uvāca śaivaḥ hi paramaḥ dharmaḥ śreṣṭha anuṣṭhāna śabditaḥ yatra aparokṣaḥ lakṣyeta sākṣāt mokṣa pradaḥ śivaḥ saḥ tu pañcavidhaḥ jñeyaḥ pañcabhiḥ parvabhiḥ kramāt parokṣam aparokṣam ca jñānam yatra ca mokṣa dam dharma śabda abhidheya īrthe pramāṇam śrutiḥ eva naḥ sādhāraṇaḥ tatas anyaḥ tu sarveṣām adhikārāt dharma śāstra ādibhiḥ samyak sāṅgaḥ eva upabṛṃhitaḥ śaivaḥ yaḥ paramaḥ dharmaḥ śreṣṭha anuṣṭhāna śabditaḥ itihāsa purāṇābhyām kathaṃcid upabṛṃhitaḥ śaiva āgamaiḥ tu saṃpannaḥ tad saṃskāra adhikāraiḥ ca samyak eva upabṛṃhitaḥ mahā āgamaḥ hi dvividhaḥ śrautaḥ aśrautaḥ ca saṃskṛtaḥ svatantraḥ daśadhā pūrvam tathā aṣṭādaśadhā punar kāmikā ādi samākhyābhiḥ siddhaḥ siddhānta saṃjñitaḥ param pāśupatam yatra vratam jñānam ca kathyate yuga āvarteṣu śiṣyeta yoga ācārya svarūpiṇā saṃkṣipya asya pravaktāraḥ catvāraḥ parama ṛṣayaḥ ruruḥ dadhīcaḥ agastyaḥ ca upamanyuḥ mahā yaśāḥ te ca pāśupatāḥ jñeyāḥ saṃhitānām pravartakāḥ tad saṃtatīyāḥ guravaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas teṣu pāśupataḥ yogaḥ śivam pratyakṣayet dṛḍham tasmāt śreṣṭham anuṣṭhānam yogaḥ pāśupataḥ mataḥ nāma aṣṭaka mayaḥ yogaḥ śivena parikalpitaḥ tena yogena sahasā śaivī prajñā prajāyate prasīdati śivaḥ tasya yasya jñānam pratiṣṭhitam prasādāt paramaḥ yogaḥ yaḥ śivam ca aparokṣayet mad bhairava aparokṣāt saṃsāra kāraṇena viyujyate śivaḥ maheśvaraḥ ca eva rudraḥ viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ saṃsāra vaidyaḥ sarvajñaḥ paramātmā iti mukhyatas nāma aṣṭakam idam mukhyam śivasya pratipādakam pañcakam jñeyam śānti atīta ādi anukramāt saṃjñā sadāśiva ādīnām pañca upādhi parigrahāt padam eva hi tat nityam anityāḥ padinaḥ smṛtāḥ ca ātma antara abhidhānam syāt yat ādyam nāma pañcakam anādi mala saṃśleṣaḥ prāgabhāvāt svabhāvāt athavā aśeṣa kalyāṇa guṇa eka dhanaḥ īśvaraḥ prakṛtyāḥ tu param prāhuḥ puruṣam pañcaviṃśakam yam veda ādau svaram prāhuḥ vācya vācaka bhāvāt ca tad adhīna pravṛtti tvāt prakṛtyāḥ puruṣasya ca māyā tu prakṛtim vidyāt māyinam tu maheśvaram paramātmā ādiḥ sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ hetuḥ vā tat rāvayati naḥ prabhuḥ tattva ādi bhūta paryantam śarīra ādiṣu atandritaḥ tatas mūrti ātmanām api pitṛ bhāvena sarveṣām pitāmahaḥ udīritaḥ saṃsārasya īśvaraḥ nityam sa mūlasya nivartakaḥ tri kāla bhāvinaḥ bhāvān sthūlān sūkṣmān aśeṣatas aṇavaḥ na eva jānanti māyayā eva mala āvṛtāḥ svāt parātma virahāt paramātmā śivaḥ svayam nāma aṣṭakam idam ca eva labdhvā ācārya prasādāt nivṛttya ādi kalā granthim śiva ādyaiḥ pañca nāmbhiḥ yathāsvam kramaśas chitvā śodhayitvā yathāguṇam chittvā paryaṣṭaka ākāram sva ātmānam ca suṣumṇayā saṃhṛtyam vadanam paścāt yathā saṃskaraṇam layāt śāktena amṛta varṣeṇa saṃsiktāyām tanau punar avatārya svam ātmānam amṛta ātma ākṛtim hṛdi dvādaśāntar sthitasya indoḥ parastāt śveta paṅkaje samāsīnam mahādevam śaṃkaram bhakta vatsalam arddhanārīśvaram devam nirmalam madhura ākṛtim hasta sphaṭika saṃkāśam prasannam śītala dyutim mahā nāma aṣṭakena eva bhāva puṣpaiḥ samarcayet abhyarcana ante tu punar prāṇān āyamya mānavaḥ samyak cittam samādhāya śārvam nāma aṣṭakam japet nābhau ca aṣṭa āhutīḥ hutvā pūrṇāhutyā namaḥ tatas evam kṛtvā cirāt eva jñānam pāśupatam śubham labhate tad pratiṣṭhām ca vṛttam ca anuttamam tathā yogam ca paramam labdhvā mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe śreṣṭhānuṣṭhānavarṇanam nāma dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ brahma ādayaḥ api yat kṛtvā sarve pāśupatāḥ smṛtāḥ uvāca vratam pāśupatam śrautam atharvaśirasi śrutam bhāgaḥ caitrī paurṇamāsī deśaḥ śiva parigrahaḥ kṣetra ārāma ādi araṇyam vā praśastaḥ śubha lakṣaṇaḥ tatra pūrvam trayodaśyām su snātaḥ su kṛta āhnikaḥ anujñāpya svam ācāryam saṃpūjya praṇipatya ca pūjām vaiśeṣikīm kṛtvā śukla ambara dharaḥ svayam śukla yajña upavītī ca śukla mālya anulepanaḥ darbha āsane samāsīnaḥ darbha muṣṭim pragṛhya ca prāṇāyāma trayam kṛtvā prāñc mukhaḥ vā api udañc mukhaḥ dhyātvā devam ca devīm ca tad vijñāpana vartmanā yāvat śarīrapātam vā dvādaśa abdam atha api vā tad ardham vā tad ardham vā māsa dvādaśakam tu vā tad ardham vā tad ardham vā māsam ekam atha api vā api agnim ādhāya vidhivat virajā homa kāraṇāt pūrṇām āpūrya tām bhūyas tattvānām śuddhim uddiśan pañcabhūtāni tanmātrāḥ pañca karma indriyāṇi ca jñāna karma vibhedena pañcakarma vibhāgaśaḥ tvac ādi dhātavaḥ sapta pañca prāṇa ādi vāyavaḥ manas buddhiḥ aham khyātiḥ guṇāḥ prakṛti pūruṣau māyā ca śuddhi vidyā ca maheśvara sadāśivau ca ca viduḥ mahā anugraham āsādya jñānavān saḥ hi jāyate atha gomayam ādāya piṇḍīkṛtya abhimantrya ca prabhāte tu caturdaśyām kṛtvā sarvam purā uditam dine tasmin nirāhāraḥ kālam śeṣam samāpayet prātar parvaṇi ca api evam kṛtvā homāḥ vasānataḥ upasaṃhṛtya rudra agnim gṛhṇīyāt bhasma yatnatas tatas ca jaṭilaḥ muṇḍī śikhā eka jaṭaḥ eva vā bhūtvā snātvā tatas vīta lajjaḥ ced syāt digambaraḥ api kāṣāya vasanaḥ carma cīra ambaraḥ atha vā hi eka ambaraḥ valkalī vā bhavet daṇḍī ca mekhalī prakṣālya caraṇau paścāt dvis ācamya ātmanaḥ tanum agniḥ ityādibhiḥ mantraiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ātharvaṇaiḥ kramāt sarva aṅga uddhūlanam kuryāt praṇavena śivena vā śiva bhāvam samāgamya śiva yogam atha ācaret tad paśu tvam parityajya kṛtvā pāśupatam vratam pūjanīyaḥ mahādevaḥ liṅga mūrtiḥ sanātanaḥ padmam tasya api abhāve tu kevalam bhāvanā mayam tad padma karṇikā madhye kṛtvā liṅgam kanīyasam sphīṭikam pīṭhikā upetam pūjayet vidhivat kramāt pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānena tad liṅgam kṛta śodhanam parikalpya āsanam mūrtim pañcavaktra prakārāt pañcagavya ādibhiḥ pūrṇaiḥ yathā vibhava saṃbhṛtaiḥ snāpayet kalaśaiḥ pūrṇaiḥ aṣṭāpada samudbhavaiḥ sa vedikam samālipya liṅgam bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitam puṇyaiḥ praśastaiḥ pattraiḥ ca citraiḥ dūrvā akṣata ādibhiḥ samabhyarcya yathālābham mahā pūjā vidhānāt dhūpam dīpam tathā ca api naivedyam ca samādiśet iṣṭāni ca viśiṣṭāni nyāyena upārjitāni ca sarva dravyāṇi deyāni vrate tasmin viśeṣataḥ śrīpattra utpala padmānām saṃkhyā sāhasrikā matā pratyekam aparā saṃkhyā śatam aṣṭa uttaram dvijāḥ aṣṭāṅgam arghyam utkṛṣṭam dhūpa ālepau viśeṣataḥ candanam vāmadeva ākhye haritālam ca pauruṣe īśāne bhasitam kecid ālepanam iti īdṛśām sita agurum aghora ākhye mukhe kṛṣṇa agurum punar api hi uśīra ādi deyāt dhūpam viśeṣataḥ śarkarā madhu karpūra kapilā ghṛta saṃyutam candana aguru kāṣṭha ādyam sāmānyam saṃpracakṣate bhū brahma aṅgāni tatas ca eva prathama āvaraṇa īrcite dvitīya āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ vighneśāḥ cakravartinaḥ tṛtīya āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ bhava ādyāḥ aṣṭa mūrtayaḥ mahādeva ādayaḥ tatra tathā ekādaśa mūrtayaḥ caturtha āvaraṇe pūjyāḥ sarve eva gaṇeśvarāḥ daśa dikpatayaḥ pūjyāḥ sa astrāḥ sa anucarāḥ tathā brahmaṇaḥ mānasāḥ putrāḥ sarve api jyotiṣām gaṇāḥ sarvāḥ devyaḥ ca devāḥ ca sarve sarve ca khecarāḥ pātāla vāsinaḥ ca anye sarve muni gaṇāḥ api pālāḥ ca sa gaṇāḥ sarvam ca etat carācaram pūjanīyam śiva prītyā mat tvā śambhu vibhūtimat atha āvaraṇa pūjā ante saṃpūjya parameśvaram sa ājyam savyam janam hṛdyam haviḥ bhaktyā nivedayet mukha vāsa ādikam dattvā tāmbūlam sa upadaṃśakam alaṃkṛtya ca bhūyas api nānā puṣpa vibhūṣaṇaiḥ nīrājana ante vistīrya pūjā śeṣam samāpayet caṣakam sa upakāram ca śayanam ca samarpayet candra saṃkāśa hāram ca śayanīyam samarpayet madhyam nṛpa ucitam hṛdyam tat sarvam anurūpatas kṛtvā ca kārayitvā ca hitvā ca pratipūjanam stotram vyapohanam japtvā vidyām pañcākṣarīm japet pradakṣiṇām praṇāmam ca kṛtvā ātmānam samarpayet dattvā arghyam aṣṭau puṣpāṇi devam udvāsya liṅgāt saṃpūjya ca gurūn viprān vratinaḥ ca viśeṣataḥ bhaktān dvijān ca śaktaḥ ced dīna anāthān ca toṣayet svayam ca anaśane śaktaḥ phala mūla aśane atha vā payas vrataḥ vā bhikṣā āśī bhavet eka aśanaḥ tathā naktam yukta aśanaḥ nityam bhū śayyā nirataḥ śuciḥ bhasma śāyī tṛṇeśāyī cīra ajina dhṛtaḥ athavā arkavāre tathā ārdrāyām pañcadaśyām ca pakṣayoḥ tasyām ca caturdaśyām śaktaḥ tu upavaset api mākhaṇḍi patita udakyāḥ
