sūtakāntya ja pūrvakān kṣama dāna dayā satya ahiṃsā śīlaḥ sadā bhavet santuṣṭaḥ ca praśāntaḥ ca japa dhyāna rataḥ tathā kuryāt triṣavaṇa snānam bhasma snānam atha api vā pūjām vaiśeṣikām ca eva manasā vacasā girā pramādāt tu tathā ācāre nirūpya gurulāghave ucitām niṣkṛtim kuryāt pūjā homa japa ādibhiḥ ca kuryāt ca sāmānyam etat kathitam vratasya asya samāsatas pratimāsam viśeṣam ca pravadāmi yathāśrutam vaiśākhe vajraliṅgam tu jyeṣṭhe mārakatam śubham bhāṣāḍhe mauktikam vidyāt śrāvaṇe nīla nirmitam hi āśvine māsi vidyāt vai liṅgam gomedakam varam baidrumam liṅgam vaiḍūryam mārgaśīrṣake puṣparāga mayam pauṣe māghe dyumaṇi jam tathā sarva māseṣu ratnānām alābhe haimam eva vā haima abhāve rājatam vā tāmra jam śaila jam tathā mṛd mayam vā yathālābham jātuṣam ca anyat eva vā kṛtvā vaiśeṣikīm pūjām hutvā ca eva yathā purā saṃpūjya ca tathā ācāryam vratinaḥ ca viśeṣataḥ deśikena api anujñātaḥ prāñc mukhaḥ vā api udañc mukhaḥ darbha āsanaḥ darbha pāṇiḥ prāṇa apānau niyamya ca japitvā śaktitas mūlam dhyātvā sa ambam tryambakam anujñāpya yathāpūrvam namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ tatas daṇḍa jaṭā cīra mekhalāḥ api ca utsṛjet yaḥ kṛtvā ātyantikīm dīkṣām ā dehāntam an ākulaḥ ca vijñeyaḥ mahāpāśupataḥ tathā saḥ eva tapatām śreṣṭhaiḥ saḥ eva ca mahāvratī na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścid kṛtakṛtyaḥ mumukṣuṣu anvaham dvādaśa aham vā vratam etat samācaret ghṛta aktaḥ yaḥ caret etat vratam vrata parāyaṇaḥ mahā arpita ātmā satatam na tena sadṛśaḥ kvacid pāpaiḥ su dāruṇaiḥ sadyas mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu vīryavān bhasma saṃyutaḥ bhasma niṣṭhasya naśyanti bhasma agni saṃgamāt bhasma snāna viśuddha ātmā bhasma niṣṭhaḥ iti smṛtaḥ bhasmanā digdha sarva aṅgaḥ bhasma dīpta tripuṇḍrakaḥ bhasma snāyī ca puruṣaḥ bhasma niṣṭhaḥ iti smṛtaḥ bhūta preta piśāsāḥ ca rogāḥ ca atīva dussahāḥ bhasma niṣṭhasya sāṃnidhyāt vidravanti na saṃśayaḥ bhāsanāt bhāsitam proktam bhasma kalmaṣa bhakṣaṇāt bhūti bhūti karā ca eva rakṣā rakṣā karā param parama astram ca śaivānām bhasma etat pārameśvaram iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe paśupativratavidhānavarṇanam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ dhaumya agrajena śuśunā kṣīra artham hi tapaḥ kṛtam tasmāt kṣīrārṇavaḥ dattaḥ tasmai devena śūlinā sa katham śiśukaḥ lebhe śiva śāstra pravaktṛ tām katham vā śiva sadbhāvam jñātvā tapasi niṣṭhitaḥ katham ca labdha vijñānaḥ tapaḥ caraṇa parvaṇi uvāca na hi eṣa śiśukaḥ kaścid prākṛtaḥ kṛtavan tapaḥ janma antareṇa saṃsiddhaḥ kena api khalu hetunā sva pada pracyutaḥ diṣṭyā prāptaḥ muni kumāra tām mahādeva prasādasya bhāgya āpannasya bhāvinaḥ dugdha abhilāṣa prabhava dvāra tām agamat tapaḥ atas sarva gaṇa īśa tvam kumāra tvam ca śāśvatam tasya jñāna āgama upyasya prasādāt eva śāṃkarāt tat hi param sākṣāt jñānam śakti mayam viduḥ dṛṣṭam tu kāraṇam tasya śiva jñāna samanvaye sva mātṛ vacanam sākṣāt śoka jam kṣīra kāraṇāt kadācid kṣīram ati alpam pītavan mātula āśrame mātula sutam santṛpta kṣīram uttamam pītvā sthitam yathākāmam dṛṣṭvā vai mātula ātmajam upamanyuḥ vyāghrapādiḥ prītyā provāca mātaram pibāmi uvāca hi vyāghrapādasya mahiṣī duḥkham āpat tadā ca sā upalālya atha su prītyā putram āliṅgya sa ādaram duḥkhitā vilalāpa atha smṛtvā nairdhanyam ātmanaḥ smṛtvā a smṛtvā punar kṣīram upamanyuḥ sa bālakaḥ tām āha rudraiḥ bhūyas mahā dyutiḥ tad haṭham sā parijñāya dvija patnī tapasvinī śāntaye tad haṭhasya atha śubha upāyam arīracat uñcha vṛttyā arjitān bījān svayam dṛṣṭvā ca sā tadā bīja piṣṭam atha āloḍya toyena kala bhāṣiṇī māliṃgya ādāya duḥkha ārtā pradadau kṛtrimam payaḥ pītvā ca kṛtrimam kṣīram mātrām dattam sa bālakaḥ na etat kṣīram iti prāha mātaram ca ati vihvalaḥ duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha saṃprekṣya āghrāya mūrdhani taṭinīḥ ratna pūrṇāḥ tāḥ svarga pātāla gocarāḥ bhāgya hīnāḥ na paśyanti bhakti hīnāḥ ca ye śive rājyam svargam ca mokṣam ca bhojanam kṣīra sambhavam na labhante priyāṇi eṣām na tuṣyati yadā śivaḥ tatra kutas naḥ vane nivasatām sadā kṛtsna abhāvena dāridryāt mayā te bhāgya hīnayā mithyādugdham idam dattam piṣṭam āloḍya vāriṇā tvam mātula gṛhe su alpam pītvā svādu payaḥ śṛtam mā jñātvā svādu tvayā pītam tad jātīyam anusmaran dattam na payaḥ iti uktvā rudan duḥkhīkaroṣi mām tad kāmānām yathā kāmam yathā ukta phala dhanāni uddiśya na asmābhiḥ itas prāk arcitaḥ śivaḥ atas daridrāḥ saṃjātāḥ vayam tasmāt na te payaḥ uvāca iti mātṛ vacaḥ śrutvā tathyam śoka ādi sūcakam śokena alam itas mataḥ sa ambaḥ yadi asti śaṃkaraḥ tyaja śokam mahābhāge sarvam bhadram bhaviṣyati cirāt vā hi acirāt vā api kṣīrodam sādhayāmi aham uvāca tadā mātā su prasannā manasvinī uvāca śubham vicāritam tāta tvayā mad prīti vardhanam mā kathāḥ tvam hi bhaja sa ambam sadāśivam tat kṛtam hi jagant sarvam brahma ādyāḥ tasya kiṃkarāḥ tad prasāda kṛta aiśvaryāḥ dāsāḥ tasya vayam prabhoḥ tam vinā anyam na jānīmaḥ śaṃkaram loka śaṃkaram anyān devān parityajya karmaṇā manasā girā tam eva sa ambam sa gaṇam bhaja bhāva puraḥsaram sākṣāt namaḥ śivāya iti mantraḥ ayam vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ sapta koṭi mahā mantrāḥ sarve sa praṇavāḥ pare sa prasādāḥ ca te mantrāḥ sva adhikāra ādi apekṣayā sarva adhikāraḥ tu ekaḥ ayam mantraḥ eva īśvara ājñayā yathā nikṛṣṭa anutkṛṣṭān sarvān api ātmanaḥ śivaḥ sarva rakṣā kṣamaḥ api eṣa na aparaḥ kaścid iṣyate tasmāt mantra antarān tyaktvā pañcākṣara paraḥ bhava adhorāstram ca śaivānām rakṣā hetuḥ anuttamam viraja anala saṃsiddham mahā vyāpad nivāraṇam mantram ca te mayā dattam gṛhāṇa mad anujñayā uvāca evam mātrā samādiśya śivam astu iti udīrya ca tam āha ca tadā mātā śubham kurvantu te surāḥ himavat parvatam prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ aṣṭa iṣṭakābhiḥ prasādam kṛtvā liṅgam ca mṛd mayam tatra āvāhya mahādevam sa ambam sa gaṇam avyayam bhaktyā pañcākṣareṇa eva putraiḥ puṣpaiḥ vana udbhavaiḥ samabhyarcya ciram kālam cacāra paramam tapaḥ tatas tapaḥ carat tam tam bālam ekākinam kṛśam purā marīcinā śaptāḥ kecid muni piśācakāḥ saṃpīḍya rākṣasaiḥ bhāvaiḥ tapasaḥ vighnam ācaran sadā namaḥ śivāya iti krośati smārta nāda vat tad nāda śravaṇāt eva tapasaḥ vighna kāriṇaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe upamanyutapovarṇanam nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atha sarve pradīpta aṅgāḥ vaikuṇṭham prayayuḥ drutam praṇamya āhuḥ ca tat sarvam haraye deva sattamāḥ śrutvā teṣām tadā vākyam bhagavant puruṣottamaḥ kim idam tu iti saṃcintya jñātvā tad kāraṇam ca saḥ mandaram tūrṇam maheśvara didṛkṣayā dṛṣṭvā devam praṇamya evam provāca su kṛta añjaliḥ uvāca tad artham adahat sarvam tapasā tat nivāraya uvāca iti śrutvā vacaḥ viṣṇoḥ prāha devaḥ maheśvaraḥ mā śiśum nivārayiṣyāmi tat tvam gaccha svam āśramam tat śrutvā śambhu vacanam saḥ viṣṇuḥ deva vallabhaḥ gam āśvāsya tān sarvān sva lokam amara ādikān ha śakrasya rūpam āsthāya gantum cakre matim tatas sa vāraṇaḥ cāru tadā vibhum tam nivījya vāla vyajanena divyam dadhāra śacyā sahitam sura indram kareṇa vāmena śita ātapatram rarāja bhagavān somaḥ śakra rūpī sadāśivaḥ āsthāya evam hi śakrasya sva rūpam parameśvaraḥ tam dṛṣṭvā parameśānam śakra rūpa dharam śivam praṇamya śirasā prāha mahā muni varaḥ svayam pāvitaḥ ca āśramaḥ saḥ mama deveśvara svayam uvāca evam uktvā sthitam prekṣya kṛta añjali puṭam dvijam prāha gambhīrayā vācā śakra rūpa dharaḥ haraḥ uvāca uvāca mārayāmi śive bhaktim iti uvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ tat niśamya hariḥ prāha mām na jānāsi lekhapam rudreṇa nirguṇena api kim te kāryam bhaviṣyati deva bahis bhūtaḥ yaḥ piśāca tvam āgataḥ uvāca prasaṅgāt eva devasya nirguṇa tvam mahātmanaḥ brahma viṣṇu maheśānām janaka prakṛtyāḥ param upāsate yam tattva jñāḥ varam tasmāt vṛṇomi aham na asti śambhoḥ param tattvam sarva kāraṇa kāraṇāt brahma viṣṇu ādi devānām sraṣṭuḥ guṇa parasmāt vibhoḥ bhava antare kṛtam pāpam śrutā nindā bhavasya ced śrutvā nindām bhavasya atha tad kṣaṇāt eva santyajet mama āstām tāvat mama iccheyam kṣīram prati sura adhama nihatya tvā śiva astreṇa tyajāmi etam kalevaram uvāca tyaktvā nihantum śakram udyataḥ smṛtvā śambhu pada dvandvam sva deham dugdhum udyataḥ māgneyīm dhāraṇām bibhrat upamanyuḥ avasthitaḥ vārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇām tasya yoginaḥ tat visṛṣṭam aghora astram nandīśvara niyogāt madhyatas kṣiptam nandī śaṃkara vallabhaḥ svam rūpam eva bhagavant āsthāya parameśvaraḥ darśayāmāsa śiprāya bāla indu kṛta śekharam eva dadhi ādeḥ arṇavān ca eva ghṛta uda arṇavam eva ca phala arṇavam ca bālasya bhakṣya bhojya arṇavam tathā apūpānām girim ca eva darśayāmāsa saḥ prabhuḥ evam sa dadṛśe devaḥ devyā sārdham vṛṣā upari gaṇeśvaraiḥ triśūla ādyaiḥ divya astraiḥ api saṃvṛtaḥ divi dundubhayaḥ neduḥ puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca papāta daṇḍa vat bhūmau bhakti namreṇa cetasā ehi ehi iti tam āhūya mūrdhani āghrāya dadau varān uvāca bhakṣya bhojyāni athākāmam bāndhavaiḥ bhukṣva sarvadā upamanyo mahābhāga tava ambā eṣā hi pārvatī mayā putrīkṛtaḥ hi adya dattaḥ kṣīra udaka arṇavaḥ madhunaḥ ca arṇavaḥ ca eva dadhi anna arṇavaḥ eva ca phala ādi arṇavaḥ eva ca ete dattāḥ mayā te hi tvam gṛhṇīṣva mahā mune mayā dattam gāṇapatyam ca śāśvatam varān varaya su prītyā mano abhilaṣitān parān maham pradāsyāmi na atra kāryā vicāraṇā uvāca evam uktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyām upagṛhyatam pṛthvī abdhiḥ api sa ākāraḥ kṣīram svādu kare dadhat upasthāya dadau piṇḍībhūtam kṣīram anaśvaram yoga aiśvaryam sadā tuṣṭim brahma vidyām anaśvarām samṛddhim paramān tasmai dadau santuṣṭa mānasaḥ atha śaṃbhuḥ prasanna ātmā dṛṣṭvā tasya tapaḥ mahaḥ ca tasmāt śivāt ca tasyāḥ ca śivāyāḥ muditaḥ abhavat tatas prasanna cetaskaḥ su praṇamya kṛtāñjaliḥ sva āsyam paramam sneham sāṃnidhyam ca eva sarvadā evam uktvā prasanna ātma aharṣa gadgadayā girā prasīda karuṇā sindho sa ambaiḥ śaṃkaraiḥ sarvadā uvāca evam uktaḥ mahādevaḥ sarveṣām ca vara pradaḥ uvāca dṛḍha bhaktaḥ asi viprarṣe mayā vijñāsitaḥ hi asi yaśasvī tejasā yuktaḥ divya jñāna samanvitaḥ akṣayāḥ bāndhavāḥ ca eva kulam gotram ca te sadā bhaviṣyati dvijaśreṣṭhaiḥ mayi bhaktiḥ ca śāśvatā sāṃnidhyam ca āśrame nityam kariṣyāmi dvijottamaiḥ upakaṇṭham mama tvam vai sa ānandam vihariṣyasi paraḥ īśānaḥ sa varān dattvā tatra eva antardadhe haraḥ upamanyuḥ prasanna ātmā prāpya tasmāt varāt varān jagāma jananī sthānam sukham prāpa adhikam ca saḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe vaiyāsikyām caturviṃśati sāhasrāyām saṃhitāyām tad antargatāyām saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām pūrva khaṇḍe upamanyucaritavarṇanam nāma pañcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ u ayam saptamyāḥ vāyavīyasaṃhitāyāḥ pūrva khaṇḍaḥ śrīḥ prārabhyate gaurī gaurī kuca taṭa dvaṃdva kuṅkuma aṃkita vakṣase uvāca ṛṣayaḥ ca api te sarve naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ atha ayam arthaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ iti kṛtvā viniścayam kṛtvā yathā svakam kṛtyam pratyaham te yathā purā bhagavantam upāyāntam samīkṣya samupāviśan sukha āsana upaviṣṭaḥ ca vāyuḥ loka namaskṛtaḥ śrīmat vibhūtim īśasya hṛdi kṛtvā idam abravīt iti ākarṇya śubhām vāṇīm ṛṣayaḥ kṣīṇa kalmaṣāḥ vibhūti vistaram śrotum ūcuḥ te paramam vacaḥ ūcuḥ tapasā yat prāptam parameśvarāt dṛṣṭaḥ asau vāsudevena kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā prāptam ca paramam jñānam iti prāk eva śuśruma katham sa labdhavan kṛṣṇaḥ jñānam pāśupatam param uvāca sva icchayā hi avatīrṇaḥ api vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ nindayan iva mānuṣyam deha śuddhim cakāra saḥ munibhiḥ dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭavan tatra vai munim bhasma avadāta sarva aṅgam tripuṇḍra aṃkita mastakam rudra akṣa mālā ābharaṇam jaṭā maṇḍala maṃḍitam tad śiṣya bhūtaiḥ munibhiḥ śāstraiḥ vedam iva āvṛtam namaścakāra tam dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭa sarva tanūruhaḥ bahu mānena kṛṣṇaḥ asau tris kṛtvā tu pradakṣiṇām stutim cakāra su prītyā nata skandhaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ tasya avalokanāt eva muneḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ naṣṭam āsīt malam sarvam māyā jam kārmam eva ca tapas kṣīṇam alam kṛṣṇam upamanyuḥ yathā vidhiḥ atha pāśupatam sākṣāt vratam dvādaśa māsikam tadā prabhṛti tam kṛṣṇam munayaḥ śaṃsita vratāḥ divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve parivṛtya upatasthire tatas guru niyogāt vai kṛṣṇaḥ parama śaktimān tapaḥ cakāra putra artham sa ambam uddiśya śaṃkaram tena varṣa ante dṛṣṭaḥ asau parameśvaraḥ śriyā paramayā yuktaḥ sa ambaḥ ca sa gaṇaḥ śivaḥ vara artham āvirbhūtasya harasya subhaga ākṛteḥ stutim cakāra natvā asau kṛṣṇaḥ samyak kṛtāñjaliḥ sa ambam sama gaṇa vyagraḥ labdhavan putram ātmanaḥ tapasā tuṣṭa cittena dattam viṣṇoḥ śivena vai yasmāt sa ambaḥ mahādevaḥ pradadau putram ātmanaḥ tasmāt jāmbavatī sūnum sāmbam cakre saḥ nāmnaḥ tat etat kathitam sarvam kṛṣṇasya amita karmaṇaḥ mahā ṛṣeḥ jñāna lābhaḥ ca putra lābhaḥ ca śaṃkarāt yaḥ idam kīrtayet nityam śṛṇuyāt śrāvayet tathā sa viṣṇoḥ jñānam āsādya tena eva saha modate iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe kṛṣṇaputraprāptivarṇanam nama prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ kim tat pāśupatam jñānam katham paśupatiḥ śivaḥ katham dhaumya agrajaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇena akliṣṭa karmaṇā etat sarvam samācakṣva vāyo śaṃkara vigrahaiḥ uvāca iti ākarṇya vacaḥ teṣām mahā ṛṣīṇām prabhañjanaḥ saṃsmṛtya śivam īśānam pravaktum upacakrame uvāca purā sākṣāt maheśena śrīkaṇṭha ākhyena mandare devyai devena kathitam jñānam pāśupatam param tat eva pṛṣṭam kṛṣṇena viṣṇunā viśvayoninā paśu tvam ca sura ādīnām pati tvam ca śivasya ca yathā upadiṣṭam kṛṣṇāya muninā hi upamanyunā tathā samāsatas vakṣye tat śṛṇudhvam atandritāḥ purā upamanyum āsīnam viṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇa vapus dharaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca divyam pāśupatam jñānam vibhūtim vā asya kṛtsnaśas katham paśupatiḥ devaḥ paśavaḥ ke prakīrtitāḥ iti saṃcoditaḥ śrīmān upamanyuḥ mahātmanā praṇamya devam devīm ca prāha puṣṭaḥ yathā tathā brahma ādyāḥ sthāvara antāḥ ca devadevasya śūlinaḥ paśavaḥ parikīrtyante saṃsāra vaśa vartinaḥ teṣām pati tvāt deveśaḥ śivaḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ mala māyā ādibhiḥ pāśaiḥ saḥ badhnāti paśūn patiḥ saḥ eva mocakaḥ teṣām bhaktyā samyak upāsitaḥ caturviṃśati tattvāni māyā karma guṇāḥ amī brahma ādi stamba paryantān paśūn baddhvā maheśvaraḥ pāśaiḥ etaiḥ patiḥ devaḥ kāryam kārayati svakam tasya ājñayā maheśasya prakṛtiḥ puruṣa ucitām buddhim prasūte sā buddhiḥ ahaṃkāram ahaṃkṛtiḥ indriyāṇi daśa ekam ca tanmātra pañcakam tathā mahā bhāsanāt devadevasya śivasya śiva dāyinaḥ tanmātrāṇi api tasya eva śāsanena mahīyasā mahābhūtāni aśeṣāṇi bhāvayanti anupūrvaśas brahma ādīnām tṛṇa antānām dehinām deha saṃgatim mahābhūtāni aśeṣāṇi janayanti śiva ājñayā śrotra ādīni ca gṛhṇanti śabda ādīn viṣayān pṛthak svān eva na anyān devasya divyena ājñā balena vai vāc ādīni api yāni āsan tāni karmendriyāṇi ca yathā svam karma kurvanti na anyat kiṃcid śiva ājñayā avilaṅghyā hi sarveṣām ājñā śambhoḥ garīyāḥ avakāśam aśeṣāṇām bhūtānām saṃprayacchati ākāśaḥ parameśasya śāsanāt eva sarva gaḥ havyam vahati devānām kavyam kavya āśinām api pāka ādyam ca karoti agniḥ parameśvara śāsanāt saṃjīvana ādyam sarvasya kurvati apaḥ tad ājñayā viśvambharā jagant nityam dhatte viśveśvara ājñayā mādhipatyam apām nityam kurute varuṇaḥ sadā pāśaiḥ badhnāti ca yathā daṃḍyān tasya eva śāsanāt dadāti nityam yakṣendraḥ draviṇam draviṇeśvaraḥ puṇya anurūpam bhūtebhyaḥ puruṣasya anuśāsanāt mad karoti saṃpadaḥ śaśvat jñānam ca api sumedhasām nigraham ca api asādhūnām īśānaḥ śiva śāsanāt dhatte tu dharaṇīm mūrdhanā śeṣaḥ śiva niyogāt hareḥ sṛjati aśeṣam īśasya śāsanāt caturānanaḥ anyābhiḥ mūrtibhiḥ svābhiḥ pāti ca ante nihanti ca viṣṇuḥ pālayate viśvam kāla kālasya śāsanāt kālaḥ karoti sakalam kālaḥ saṃharati prajāḥ yaḥ pālayate viśvam kāla kālasya śāsanāt tribhiḥ aṃśaiḥ jagant bibhrat tejobhiḥ vṛṣṭim ādiśan puṣṇāti oṣadhi jātāni bhūtāni āhlādayati api devaiḥ ca pīyate candraḥ candrabhūṣaṇa śāsanāt khecarāḥ ṛṣayaḥ siddhāḥ bhoginaḥ manujāḥ mṛgāḥ paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ ca eva kīṭa ādyāḥ sthāvarāṇi ca nadyaḥ samudrāḥ girayaḥ kānanāni sarāṃsi ca yedāḥ sa aṅgāḥ ca śāstrāṇi mantra stoma makha ādayaḥ kālāgni ādi śiva antāni bhuvanāni saha adhipaiḥ brahmāṇḍāni api asaṃkhyāni teṣām āvaraṇāni ca diśaḥ ca vidiśaḥ ca eva kāla bhedāḥ kalā ādayaḥ tat sarvam śaṃkarasya ājñā balena samadhiṣṭhitam mājñā balāt tasya dharā sthitā iha dharādharāḥ vāridharāḥ samudrāḥ jyotiḥ gaṇāḥ śakra mukhāḥ ca devāḥ sthiram ciram vā cit acit yat asti ati āścaryam idam kṛṣṇaiḥ śambhoḥ amita karmaṇaḥ ha ājñā kṛtam śṛṇuṣva etat śrutam śruti mukhe mayā tadā maheśvaraḥ teṣām madhyatas vara veṣa dhṛk sva lakṣaṇaiḥ vihīna aṅgaḥ svayam yakṣaḥ iva abhavat sa tān āha surān ekam tṛṇam ādāya bhū tale yakṣasya vacanam śrutvā vajrapāṇiḥ śacīpatiḥ kiṃcid kruddhaḥ vihasya enam tṛṇam ādātum udyataḥ na tat tṛṇam upadātum manasā api ca śakyate tat vajram nija vajreṇa saṃsṛṣṭam iva sarvatas tṛṇena abhihatam tena tiryañc agram papāta ha tatas ca anye su saṃrabdhāḥ lokapālāḥ mahā balāḥ sasṛjuḥ tṛṇam uddiśya sva āyudhāni sahasraśas evam devaiḥ samārabdham tṛṇam uddiśya yatnatas vyartham āsīt aho kṛṣṇaiḥ yakṣasya ātma balena vai tat āha yakṣam devendraḥ kaḥ bhavān iti amarṣitaḥ tad antare haimavatī devī divya vibhūṣaṇā māvirāsīt nabhasaḥ aṅge śobhamānā śuci smitā tām dṛṣṭvā vismaya āviṣṭāḥ devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ praṇamya yakṣam papracchuḥ kaḥ asau yakṣaḥ vilakṣaṇaḥ sā abravīt sa smitam devī sa yuṣmākam agocaraḥ tena idam bhramyate cakram saṃsāra ākhyam carācaram devāḥ ca vismitāḥ sarve tām praṇamya divam yayuḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe dvitīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ śṛṇu kṛṣṇaiḥ maheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ sa śivaḥ sarvam eva idam svakīyābhiḥ ca mūrtibhiḥ brahmā viṣṇuḥ tathā rudraḥ maheśānaḥ sadāśivaḥ atha anyāḥ ca api tanavaḥ pañca brahma samāhvayāḥ puruṣaḥ aghoraḥ vāmaḥ sadyaḥ tathā eva ca brahmāni etāni devasya mūrttayaḥ pañca viśrutāḥ īśāna ākhyā tu yā tasya mūrttiḥ ādyā garīyāḥ tāram prakṛtyāḥ sākṣāt kṣetrajñam adhitiṣṭhati sthāṇoḥ tatpuruṣa ākhyā yā mūrttiḥ mūrttimataḥ prabhoḥ adhitiṣṭhati dharma ādi aṣṭa aṅga saṃyuktam buddhi tattvam pinākinaḥ adhitiṣṭhati aghora ākhyā mūrtiḥ atyanta pūjitā vāmadeva āhvayām mūrttim mahādevasya vedhasaḥ ahaṃkṛteḥ adhiṣṭhātrīm āhuḥ āgama vedinaḥ sadyas jāta āhvayām mūrttim śambhoḥ amita varcasaḥ mānasaḥ samadhiṣṭhātrīm matimantaḥ pracakṣate īśvarīm īśvarasya imām īśā ākhyām hi viduḥ budhāḥ tvak pāṇi sparśa vāyūnām īśvarām mūrtim aiśvarām puruṣa ākhyam viduḥ sarve purāṇa artha viśāradāḥ cakṣuṣaḥ caraṇasya api rūpasya agneḥ tathā eva ca tad ākhyām adhiṣṭhātrīm mūrtim āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ ramanāyāḥ ca pāyoḥ ca rasasya apām tathā eva ca mūrtim tad niratām viduḥ sadyas jāta āhvayām mūrtim īśvarām saṃpracakṣate mūrtayaḥ pañca devasya vandanīyāḥ prayatnāt tasmin vyāpya sthitam viśvam sūtre maṇi gaṇāḥ iva śarvaḥ bhavaḥ tathā rudraḥ ugraḥ bhīmaḥ paśoḥ patiḥ mūrtayaḥ ca aṣṭa viśrutāḥ bhūmi ambhas agni marut vyoma kṣetrajña arka niśākarāḥ tāḥ adhiṣṭhitāḥ maheśasya śarva ādyaiḥ aṣṭamūrtibhiḥ carācara ātmakam viśvam dhatte viśvambharā ātmakā mūrtiḥ iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ bhāvi iti gīyate mūrti bhavasya paramātmanaḥ bahis antargatā viśvam vyāpya tejaḥ mayā śubhā raudrī rudra avyayā mūrtiḥ āsthitā ghora rūpiṇī sarva avakāśa dā sarva vyāpakā gagana ātmakā mūrtiḥ bhīmasya bhīma ākhyā bhūta vṛndasya bhedikā sarva ātmanām adhiṣṭhātrī sarva kṣetra nivāsinī mūrtiḥ paśupateḥ jñeyā paśu pāśa nikṛntanā dīpayatī jagant sarvam divākara samāhvayā mūrtiḥ divi visarpati āpyāyayati yaḥ viśvam amṛtāṃśuḥ niśākaraḥ mahādevasya sā mūrtiḥ mahādeva samāhvayā ātmā tasya aṣṭamā mūrtiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ vyāpikā itara mūrtīnām viśvam tasmāt śiva ātmakam vṛkṣasya mūla sekena śākhāḥ puṣyanti vai yathā sarva abhaya pradānam ca sarva anugrahaṇam tathā sarva upakāra karaṇam śivasya ārādhanam viduḥ tathā sarvasya samprītyā prītaḥ bhavati śaṃkaraḥ aniṣṭam aṣṭamūrteḥ tat kṛtam eva na saṃśayaḥ aṣṭamūrti ātmanā viśvam adhiṣṭhāya sthitam śivam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca mūrtibhiḥ viśvam eva idam yathā vyāptam tathā śrutam atha etat jñātum icchāmi yāthātmyam pamā īśayoḥ strī puṃs bhāva ātmakam ca idam tābhyām katham adhiṣṭhitam śrīmat vibhūtim śivayoḥ yāthātmyam ca samāsatas śaktiḥ sākṣāt mahādevī mahādevaḥ ca śaktimān dvayam śuddham aśuddham ca param ca aparam eva ca śivasya ca śivāyāḥ ca svāmyam ca etad svabhāvāt śivayoḥ vai vaśe viśvam na viśvasya vaśe śivau mayam īśitavyam idam yasmāt tasmāt viśveśvarau śivau yathā śivaḥ tathā devī yathā devī tathā śivaḥ na bhāti vidyamānaḥ api tathā śaktyā vinā śivaḥ prabhā ca bhānunā tena sutarām tad upāśrayā evam paraspara apekṣā śakti śaktimatoḥ sthitā na śivena vinā śaktiḥ na śaktyā ca vinā śivaḥ mādyā sā ekā parā śaktiḥ cit mayā śiva saṃśrayā samāna dharmiṇīm eva śivasya paramātmanaḥ sā ekā parā ca cit rūpā śaktiḥ prasava dharmiṇī vidadhāti sā mūlaprakṛtiḥ māyā triguṇā ca tridhā smṛtā śiva icchayā parāśaktiḥ śivatattva eka tām gatā tatas kriyā ākhyayā śaktyā śaktau śaktimat utthayā tasyām vikṣobhyamāṇāyām ādau nādaḥ samudbabhau nādāt viniḥsṛtaḥ binduḥ bindodevaḥ sadāśivaḥ tasmāt maheśvaraḥ jātaḥ śuddhavidyā maheśvarāt sā vācām īśvarā śaktiḥ vāgīśa ākhyāḥ hi śūlinaḥ yā sā varṇa svarūpeṇa mātṛkā ipi vijṛmbhate atha ananta samāveśāt māyā kālam avāsṛjat niyatim ca kalām vidyām kalātas rāga pūruṣau punar eva abhūt avyaktam triguṇa ātmakam triguṇāt ca tatas vyaktāt vibhaktāḥ syuḥ trayaḥ guṇāḥ tebhyaḥ syuḥ aṇḍa piṇḍāni tu asaṃkhyāni śiva ājñayā adhiṣṭhitāni ananta ādyaiḥ vidyeśaiḥ cakravartibhiḥ śarīra antara bhedena śaktyāḥ bhedāḥ prakīrtitāḥ nānā rūpāḥ tu vijñeyāḥ sthūla sūkṣma vibhedāt rudrasya raudrī sā śaktiḥ viṣṇauḥ vai vaiṣṇavī matā hi śakya ātmanā eva tat vyāptam yathā dehe antarātmanā kalā yā paramā śaktiḥ kathitā paramātmanaḥ evam eṣā parā śaktiḥ īśvara icchā anuyāyinī sthiram caram ca yat viśvam sṛjati iti viniścayaḥ mā ha śaktimān īśvaraḥ śaśvat viśvam vyāpya adhitiṣṭhati icchā śaktiḥ maheśasya nityā kārya jñānaśaktiḥ tu tat kāryam karaṇam kāraṇam tathā payati akhilam kāryam kṣaṇāt saṃkalpa rūpiṇī yathā śakti traya utthānam śakti prasava dharmiṇī ha śaktyā paramayā nunnā prasūte sakalam jagant evam śakti samāyogāt śaktimān ucyate śivaḥ śakti śaktimat uttham tu śāktam śaivam idam jagant yathā na jāyate putraḥ pitaram mātaram vinā tathā bhavam bhavānīm ca vinā na etat carācaram strīpuṃsa prabhavam viśvam strīpuṃsa ātmakam eva ca strīpuṃsayoḥ vibhūtiḥ ca strīpuṃsābhyām adhiṣṭhitam paramātmā śivaḥ proktaḥ śivā sā ca prakīrtitā śivaḥ sadāśivaḥ proktaḥ śivā sā ca manonmanī maheśvaraḥ jñeyaḥ śivā māyā iti kathyate puruṣaḥ parameśānaḥ prakṛtiḥ parameśvarī rudraḥ maheśvaraḥ sākṣāt rudrāṇī rudra vallabhā viṣṇuḥ viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ lakṣmī viśveśvara priyā brahmā śivaḥ yadā sraṣṭā brahmāṇī brahmanaḥ priyā bhāskaraḥ bhagavant śambhuḥ prabhā bhagavatī śivā mahendraḥ manmathārātiḥ śacī śailendra kanyakā jātavedāḥ mahādevaḥ svāhā śarva ardha dehinī nirṛtiḥ bhagavant īśaḥ nairṛtī naganandanī varuṇaḥ bhagavant rudraḥ vāruṇī bhūdhara ātmajā bāla indu śekharaḥ vāyuḥ śivā śiva manoharā tat yakṣaḥ yajñaśiraḥ hartā ṛddhiḥ himagiri indrajā īśānaḥ parameśānaḥ tad āryā parameśvarī tad agni rudraḥ kāla ariḥ kālī kāla antaka priyā puruṣa ākhyaḥ manuḥ śambhuḥ śatarūpā śivapriyā dakṣaḥ sākṣāt mahādevaḥ prasūtiḥ parameśvarī bhṛguḥ bhaga akṣi hā devaḥ khyātiḥ trinayana priyā marīci bhagavant rudraḥ sambhūtiḥ śarva vallabhā gaṃgādharaḥ aṃgirāḥ jñeyaḥ smṛtiḥ sākṣāt umā smṛ pulastyaḥ śaśabhṛt mauliḥ prītiḥ kāntā pinākinaḥ kratu dhvaṃsī kratuḥ proktaḥ saṃnatiḥ dayitā vibhoḥ trinetraḥ atriḥ umā sākṣāt anasūyā smṛtā budhaiḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ manmatha arātiḥ devī sākṣāt arundhatī maheśvarī sarve strī puruṣāḥ tasmāt tayoḥ eva vibhūtayaḥ śrāvyam sarvam umā rūpam śrotā śūla vara āyudhaḥ tu dhatte śaṃkara vallabhā praṣṭā saḥ eva viśvātmā bāla candra avataṃsakaḥ draṣṭā viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ śaśi khaṇḍa śikhāmaṇiḥ rasa jātam mahādevī devaḥ rasayitā śivaḥ ca girijā preyāḥ ca eva gara aśanaḥ mantavya vastu tām dhatte sadā devī maheśvarī mantā saḥ eva viśvātmā mahādevaḥ maheśvaraḥ prāṇaḥ pinākī sarveṣām prāṇinām bhagavant prabhuḥ prāṇa sthitiḥ tu sarveṣām ambikā ca ambu rūpiṇī tadā dhatte bhagavant antaka antakaḥ ahar śūla āyudhaḥ devaḥ śūlapāṇi priyā niśā madhyam ākāśaḥ śaṃkaraḥ devaḥ pṛthivī śaṃkara priyā hariḥ bhagavant īśaḥ velā śailendra kanyakā vṛkṣaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ devaḥ latā viśveśvara priyā puṃlliṅgam akhilam dhatte bhagavant puraśāsanaḥ tri liṅgam ca akhilam dhatte devī deva manoramā mahā jālam aśeṣam tu dhatte sarvasya vallabhā yasya yasya padārthasya yā yā śaktiḥ udāhṛtā sā sā viśveśvarī devī saḥ saḥ sarvaḥ maheśvaraḥ tat tat āha mahābhāgāḥ tayoḥ tejaḥ vijṛṃbhitam yathā dīpasya dīptasya śikhā dīpayate gṛham tṛṇa ādi śiva mūrti antam viśva khyā atiśaya kramaḥ saṃnikarṣa krama vaśāt tayoḥ iti parā śrutiḥ sarva ākāra ātmakau etau sarva śreyaḥ vidhāyinaḥ pūjanīyau namaskāryau cintanīyau ca sarvadā yathāprajñam idam kṛṣṇaiḥ yāthātmyam parameśayoḥ tat katham śakyate vaktum yāthātmyam parameśayoḥ antargatam ananyānām īśvara arpita cetasām anyeṣām buddhi anārūḍham ārūḍham ca yathā eva tat yā iyam uktā vibhūtiḥ vai prākṛtā sā parā matā aprākṛtām parām anyām guhyām guhya vidaḥ viduḥ aprākṛtā parā ca eṣā vibhūtiḥ pārameśvarā sā eva iha paramā kāṣṭhā vibhūtiḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ tām prāptum prayatante atra jita śvāsāḥ jita indriyāḥ yathā saṃsāra āśīviṣa ālīḍha mṛta saṃjīvana auṣadham yaḥ parām aparām ca eva vibhūtim vetti tattvāt saḥ aparaḥ bhūtim ullaṃghya parām bhūtim samaśnute etat te kathitam kṛṣṇaiḥ yāthātmyam parama ātmanoḥ na a śiṣyebhyaḥ api a śaivebhyaḥ na a bhaktebhyaḥ kadācana vyāharet īśayoḥ bhūtim iti veda anuśāsanam tvādṛśebhyaḥ anurūpebhyaḥ kathaya etat na ca anyathā saṃsāra sāgarāt muktaḥ śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt bhāga kīrtanāt asya naśyanti mahantyaḥ pāpa koṭayaḥ bhaktiḥ parāḥ śive sa ambe sa anuge sa paricchide yat yat iṣṭatamam ca anyat tat tat āpnoti asaṃśayam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe gaurīśaṃkaravibhūtiyogaḥ nāma caturthaḥ adhyāyaḥ tat evam na vijānanti paśavaḥ pāśa gauravāt a jānantaḥ param bhāvam avikalpam mahā ṛṣayaḥ aparam brahma rūpam ca param brahma ātmakam tathā bhūta indriya antaḥkaraṇa pradhāna viṣaya ātmakam bṛhat tvāt bṛhaṇa tvāt vā brahma ca iti abhidhīyate avidyā svarūpī iti kaiścid īśaḥ nigadyate tu cetanām prāhuḥ tathā avidyām acetanām ca eva viśvam viśva guroḥ vibhoḥ rūpam eva na saṃdehaḥ viśvam tasya vaśe yatas bhrāntiḥ vidyā parā ca iti śārvam rūpam param viduḥ kṣara akṣara ātmakam prāhuḥ kṣara akṣara param pare kṣaraḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭasthaḥ akṣaraḥ ucyate tayoḥ paraḥ śivaḥ śāntaḥ kṣara akṣara aparaḥ smṛtaḥ samaṣṭi vyaṣṭhi rūpam ca samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi kāraṇam samaṣṭim āhuḥ avyaktam vyaṣṭim vyaktam tathā eva ca te rūpe parameśasya tad icchāyāḥ pravartanāt tayoḥ kāraṇa bhāvena śivam parama kāraṇam kāraṇa artha vidaḥ prāhuḥ samaṣṭi vyaṣṭi kāraṇam māti vyakti svarūpī iti kathyate kaiścid īśvaraḥ vyaktiḥ vyāvṛtti rūpam tam piṇḍa jātyāḥ samāśrayam ca eva tad ājñā paripālitāḥ kathyate pradhānam prakṛtim prāhuḥ kṣetrajñam puruṣam tathā trayoviṃśati tattvāni vyaktam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ bhū kālaḥ kārya prapañcasya pariṇāma eka kāraṇam eṣām īśaḥ adhipaḥ dhātā pravartaka nivartakaḥ mahā bhāva tirobhāva hetuḥ ekaḥ svarāj ajaḥ tasmāt pradhānapuruṣa vyakta kāla sva rūpavān hetuḥ netā adhipaḥ teṣām dhātā ca uktā maheśvaraḥ virāj hiraṇyagarbha ātmā kaiścid īśaḥ nigadyate hiraṇyagarbhaḥ lokānām hetuḥ viśva ātmakaḥ virāj antaryāmī paraḥ ca iti kathyate kavibhiḥ śivaḥ mātā mānam ca meyam ca matim ca āhuḥ atha apare mahā kartā kriyā ca kāryam ca karaṇam kāraṇam pare tam āhuḥ viguṇam kecid guṇavantam pare viduḥ kecid saṃsāriṇam prāhuḥ tam asaṃsāriṇam pare rāgavantam pare prāhuḥ vīta rāgam tathā pare niṣkriyam ca pare prāhuḥ sa kriyam ca itare janāḥ arūpam kecid āhuḥ vai rūpavantam pare viduḥ adṛśyam apare prāhuḥ dṛśyam iti apare viduḥ śabda ātmakam pare prāhuḥ śabdātītam atha apare kecid cintā mayam prāhuḥ cintayā rahitam pare pare prāhuḥ iti ca apare evam vikalpyamānam tu yāthātmyam parameṣṭhinaḥ na adhyavasyanti munayaḥ nānā pratyaya kāraṇāt yāvat paśuḥ na eva paśyati anīśam purāṇam bhuvanasya īśitāram tāvat duḥkhe vartate baddha pāśaḥ saṃsāre asmin cakra nemi krameṇa yadā paśyaḥ paśyate rukma varṇam kartāram īśam puruṣam brahma yonim iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe paśupatitvajñānayogaḥ nāma pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ māyā iyaḥ eva vā prākṛtaḥ vā atha boddhā vā hi ahaṃkāra ātmakaḥ tathā na rāgaḥ na ca vidveṣaḥ śambhoḥ amita tejasaḥ na ca asti abhiniveśaḥ asya kuśalā akuśalāni api paras paras paras paras paras paras paras paras paras paras paras paras paras paras na tasya kāraṇam kartā na ādiḥ antaḥ tathā antaram na karma karaṇam vā api na akāryam kāryam eva ca na janma maraṇe tasya na kāṃkṣitam akāṃkṣitam mahā kalyāṇam sakalam ca asti paramātmā śivaḥ yatas apracyutaḥ svatas bhāvaḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇuḥ atas smṛtaḥ śivena adhiṣṭhitam yasmāt jagant sthāvara jaṅgamam sarva rūpaḥ smṛtaḥ śarvaḥ tathā jñātvā na muhyati hiraṇyabāhuḥ bhagavant hiraṇyapatiḥ īśvaraḥ ambikā patiḥ īśānaḥ pinākī vṛṣavāhanaḥ ekaḥ rudraḥ param brahma puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇa piṅgalaḥ bālāgra mātraḥ hṛd madhye vicintyaḥ dahara antare hiraṇyakeśaḥ padmākṣaḥ hi aruṇaḥ tāmraḥ eva ca saumyaḥ ghoraḥ tathā miśraḥ ca akṣāraḥ ca amṛtaḥ avyayaḥ sa puṃviśeṣaḥ paramaḥ bhagavant antaka antakaḥ mahena atiśaya tvena jñāna aiśvarye vilokite lokeśa atiśaya tvena sthitam prāhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ pratisarga prasūtānām brahmaṇām śāstra vistaram upadeṣṭā saḥ eva ādau kāla avaccheda vartinām ca avaccheda yuktānām gurūṇām api asau guruḥ sarveṣām eva sarva īśaḥ kāla avaccheda varjitaḥ śuddhā svābhāvikā tasya śaktiḥ sarva atiśāyinī tejaḥ prabhāvaḥ vīryam ca kṣamā kāruṇyam eva ca śiva rudra ādi śabdānām praṇavaḥ hi paraḥ smṛtaḥ śambho praṇava vācyasya bhavanāt tad japāt api yā siddhiḥ sā parā prāpyā bhavati eva na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt ekākṣaram devam āhuḥ āgama pāragāḥ vācya vācakayoḥ aikyam manyamānāḥ manasvinaḥ asya mātrāḥ samākhyātāḥ catasraḥ veda mūrdhani akāraḥ ca api ukāraḥ ca makāraḥ nādaḥ iti api akāram bahvṛcam prāhuḥ ukāraḥ yajuḥ ucyate makāraḥ sāma nādaḥ asya śrutiḥ ātharvaṇā smṛtāḥ akāraḥ ca mahābījam rajaḥ sraṣṭā caturmukhaḥ ukāraḥ prakṛtiḥ yoniḥ sattvam pālayitā hariḥ makāraḥ puruṣaḥ bījam tamaḥ saṃhārakaḥ haraḥ nādaḥ paraḥ pumān īśaḥ nirguṇaḥ niṣkriyaḥ śivaḥ sarvam tisṛbhiḥ eva idam mātrābhiḥ nikhilam tridhā abhidhāya śiva ātmānam bodhayati ardha mātrayā yasmāt param na aparam asti kiṃcid yasmāt na aṇīyaḥ na jyāyaḥ asti kiṃcid vṛkṣaḥ iva stabdhaḥ divi tiṣṭhati ekaḥ tena idam pūrṇam puruṣeṇa sarvam iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivatattvavarṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ śaktiḥ svābhavikī tasya vidyā viśva vilakṣaṇā eka anekasya rūpeṇa bhāti bhānoḥ iva prabhā anantāḥ śaktayaḥ yasyāḥ icchā jñāna kriyā ādayaḥ māyā ādyāḥ ca abhavan vahnoḥ visphuliṅgāḥ yathā tathā sadāśiva īśvara ādyāḥ hi vidyā avidyeśvara ādayaḥ abhavan puruṣāḥ ca asyāḥ prakṛtiḥ ca parātparā mahat ādi viśeṣa antāḥ tu aja ādyāḥ ca api mūrtayaḥ yat ca anyat asti tat sarvam tasyāḥ kāryam na saṃśayaḥ sā śaktiḥ sarva gā sūkṣmā prabodha ānanda rūpiṇī ucyate vedyaḥ śivaḥ śivā vidyā prajñā ca eva śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ dhṛtiḥ eṣā sthitiḥ niṣṭhā jñāna icchā karma śaktayaḥ śuddhavidyā śuddha kalā sarvam śakti kṛtam yatas māyā ca prakṛtiḥ jīvaḥ vikāraḥ vikṛtiḥ tathā sā devī māyayā sarvam brahmāṇḍam sacarācaram anayā saha sarva īśaḥ saptaviṃśa prakārayā saṃśaya āviṣṭa manasaḥ vismṛśanti yathātatham kim kāraṇam kutas jātāḥ jīvāmaḥ kena vā vayam kutra asmākam saṃpratiṣṭhā kena vā adhiṣṭhitāḥ vayam kena vartāmahe śaśvat sukheṣu anyeṣu ca aniśam avilaṅghyā ca viśvasya vyavasthā kena vā kṛtā bhūtāni yoniḥ puruṣaḥ yogī ca eṣām paraḥ atha vā acetana tvāt kāla ādeḥ cetana tve pi ca ātmanaḥ sukha duḥkhāni bhūta tvāt anīśa tvāt vicāryate tad dhyāna yoga anugatām prapaśyan śaktim aiśvarām pāśa vicchedikām sākṣāt nigūḍhām sva guṇaiḥ bhṛśam tayā vicchinna pāśāḥ te sarva kāraṇa kāraṇam haktimantam mahādevam apaśyan divya cakṣuṣā yaḥ kāraṇāni aśeṣāṇi kāla ātma sahitāni ca aprameyaḥ anayā śaktyā sakalam yaḥ adhitiṣṭhati dṛṣṭena bhakti yogena divyaḥ gatim avāpnuyuḥ tasmāt saha tathā śaktyā hṛdi paśyanti ye śivam teṣām śāśvatikī śāntiḥ na etareṣām iti śrutiḥ tasmāt śaktyāḥ śaktimataḥ tādātmyāt nirvṛtiḥ dvayoḥ yaḥ kramaḥ vivakṣitaḥ nūnam vimuktau jñāna karmaṇoḥ devaḥ vā dānavaḥ vā api paśuḥ vā vihagaḥ api vā kīraḥ vā atha kṛmiḥ vā api mucyate tad prasādāt garbha sthaḥ jāyamānaḥ vā bālaḥ vā taruṇaḥ api vā vṛddhaḥ vā mriyamāṇaḥ vā svarga sthaḥ vā atha nārakī patitaḥ vā api dharma ātmā paṇḍitaḥ mūḍhaḥ eva vā tad kṣaṇāt eva mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ ayogyānām ca kāruṇyāt bhaktānām parameśvaraḥ prasāda pūrvakā yā iyam bhukti mukti vidhāyinī aneka janma siddhānām śrauta smārta anuvartinām bhavet na eva atra saṃśayaḥ sāṅgā anaṅgā ca yā sevā sā bhaktiḥ iti kathyate śiva rūpa ādi cintā yā sā sevā mānasā smṛtā japa ādiḥ vācikī sevā karma pūjā ādi kāyikī sā iyam tri sādhanā sevā śiva dharmaḥ ca kathyate saḥ tu pañcavidhaḥ proktaḥ śivena paramātmanā tapaḥ karma japaḥ dhyānam jñānam ca iti samāsatas ca tapaḥ cāndrāyaṇa ādikam yathā śiva abhyāsaḥ cintā dhyānam śivasya tu mahā āgama uktam yat jñānam tat atra jñānam ucyate śrī kaṇṭhena śivena uktam śivāyai ca śiva āgamaḥ mad āśritānām kāruṇyāt śreyasām eka sādhanam tyajet ca viṣaya āsaṅgam śreyaḥ arthī matimān naraḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivatattvakathanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca vedasāre śiva jñānam sva āśritānām vimuktaye abhaktānām abuddhīnām ayuktānām agocaram arthaiḥ daśa ṛddhaiḥ saṃyuktam gūḍham aprājña ninditam vedāt ṣaṣ aṅgāt uddhṛtya sāṃkhyāt yogāt ca kṛtsnaśas tathitam parameśeṇa tatra pūjā katham prabhoḥ kasya adhikāraḥ pūjā ādau jñāna yoga ādayaḥ katham mahā śaivam saṃkṣipya veda uktam śivena paribhāṣitam sisṛkṣayā purā avyaktāt śivaḥ sthāṇuḥ maheśvaraḥ ca tadā ṛṣiḥ viśva adhikaḥ prabhuḥ devānām prathamam devam brahmāṇam brahmaṇaspatim brahmā api pitaram devam jāyamānam nyavaikṣata tam jāyamānam janakaḥ devaḥ prāpaśyat ājñayā dṛṣṭaḥ rudreṇa devaḥ asau asṛjat viśvam īśvaraḥ ca kāra saḥ pṛthak pṛthak dharā ca vahniḥ sūryaḥ ca yajñaḥ viṣṇuḥ śacīpatiḥ te ca anye ca surāḥ rudram rudrādhyāyena tuṣṭuvuḥ apahṛtya sva līlā artham teṣām jñānam maheśvaraḥ tam apṛcchan tatas devāḥ kaḥ bhavān iti mohitāḥ mama āsam prathamam eva aham vartāmi ca sura uttamāḥ a paśyantaḥ tam īśānam stuvantaḥ ca eva sāmabhiḥ bratam pāśupatam kṛtvā tu atharvaśirasi sthitam bhasma saṃchanna sarva aṅgāḥ babhūvuḥ amarāḥ tadā atha teṣām prasāda artham paśūnām patiḥ īśvaraḥ sa gaṇaḥ ca umayā sārdham sāṃnidhyam akarot prabhuḥ yam vinidrāḥ jita śvāsāḥ yoginaḥ dagdha kilbiṣāḥ hṛdi paśyanti tam devam dadṛśuḥ deva puṃgavāḥ yām āhuḥ paramām śaktim īśvara icchā anuvartinīm tām apaśyat maheśasya vāmatas vāma locanām ye vinirdhūta saṃsārāḥ prāptāḥ śaivam param padam nitya siddhāḥ ca ye vā anyam te ca dṛṣṭāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ atha tam tuṣṭuvuḥ devāḥ devyā saha maheśvaram devaḥ api devān ālokya ghṛṇayā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ tuṣṭaḥ asmi iti āha su prītaḥ svabhāva madhurām giram ūcuḥ kasya adhikāraḥ pūjāyām vaktum arhasi tattvāt svarūpam darśayāmāsa ghoram sūrya ātmakam param śaktibhiḥ mūrtibhiḥ ca aṅgaiḥ grahaiḥ devaiḥ ca saṃvṛtam dṛṣṭvā evam adbhuta ākāram devāḥ viṣṇu purogamāḥ buddhvā divākaram devam devīm ca eva niśākaram pañcabhūtāni śeṣāṇi tad mayam ca carācaram sindūra varṇāya su maṇḍalāya suvarṇa varṇa ābharaṇāya te padma ābha netrāya sa paṅkajāya brahma indra nārāyaṇa kāraṇāya su ratna pūrṇam sa suvarṇa toyam su kuṅkuma ādyam sa kuśam sa puṣpam namaḥ śivāya śāntāya sa gaṇāya ādi hetave rudrāya viṣṇave te brahmaṇe sūrya mūrtaye yaḥ śivam maṇḍale saure saṃpūjya eva samāhitaḥ praṇamet vā paṭhet etān ślokān śruti mukhān imān tasmāt abhyarcayet nityam śivam āditya rūpiṇam dharma kāma artha mukti artham manasā karmaṇā girā atha devān samālokya maṇḍala sthaḥ maheśvaraḥ sarva āgama uttaram dattvā śāstram antaradhāt haraḥ tatra pūjā adhikāraḥ brahma kṣatra viśām iti jñātvā praṇamya deveśam devāḥ jagmuḥ yathāgatam tayā saḥ coditaḥ devaḥ devyā candra vibhūṣaṇaḥ mayā agastyena guruṇā dadhīcena mahā ṛṣiṇā svayam api avatīrya urvyām yuga āvarteṣu śūladhṛk sva āśritānām vimukti artham kurute jñāna saṃtatim ṛbhuḥ satyaḥ bhārgavaḥ ca hi aṅgirāḥ savitā dvijāḥ mṛtyuḥ śatakratuḥ dhīmān vasiṣṭhaḥ muni puṃgavaḥ sārasvataḥ tridhāmā ca trivṛtaḥ muni puṃgavaḥ śata tejāḥ svayam dharmaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ iti śrutaḥ svarakṣaḥ ca aruṇiḥ dhīmān tathā ca eva kṛtaṃjayaḥ tṛṇabinduḥ muniḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śaktiḥ śākteyaḥ uttaraḥ muniḥ vyāsa avatārān śṛṇvantu kalpa yoga īśvarān kramāt laiṅga vyāsa avatārāḥ hi dvāparā teṣu suvrata yoga ācārya avatārāḥ ca tathā śiṣyeṣu śūlinaḥ tatra tatra vibhoḥ śiṣyāḥ catvāraḥ syuḥ mahā ojasaḥ śiṣyāḥ teṣām praśiṣyāḥ ca śataśas atha sahasraśas teṣām saṃbhāvanāt loke śaiva ājñā karaṇa ādibhiḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivatattvajñāne vyāsāvatāravarṇanam nāma aṣṭamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca avatārān hi śarvasya śiṣyān ca bhagavant vada laugākṣiḥ ca mahā māyaḥ jaigīṣavyaḥ tathā eva ca supālakaḥ gautamaḥ ca tathā vedaśirāḥ muniḥ gokarṇaḥ ca guhāvāsī śikhaṇḍī ca aparaḥ smṛtaḥ jaṭāmālī ca aṭṭahāsaḥ dārukaḥ lāṅgulī tathā mahākālaḥ ca śūlī ca ḍaṃḍī muṇḍīśaḥ eva ca sa viṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca lakuli īśvaraḥ eva ca tad aṣṭāviṃśati saṃkhyātāḥ yoga ācāryāḥ yuga kramāt śiṣyāḥ pratyekam eteṣām catvāraḥ śānta cetasaḥ śveta ādayaḥ ca ruṣya antān tān bravīmi yathākramam śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaḥ ca eva śvetāśvaḥ śvetalohitaḥ dundubhiḥ śatarūpaḥ ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumant tathā vikośaḥ ca vikeśaḥ ca vipāśaḥ pāśanāśanaḥ sudhāmā virajāḥ ca eva śaṃkhaḥ ca aṃḍajaḥ eva ca sārasvataḥ ca meghaḥ ca meghavāhaḥ suvāhakaḥ kapilaḥ ca āsuriḥ pañcaśikhaḥ bāṣkalaḥ eva ca parāśarāḥ ca gargaḥ ca bhārgavaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ tathā balabandhuḥ nirāmitrāḥ ketuśṛṅgaḥ tapodhanaḥ lambodaraḥ ca lambaḥ ca lambātmā laṃbakeśakaḥ sudhāmā kaśyapaḥ ca eva vasiṣṭhaḥ virajāḥ tathā triḥ ugraḥ guru śreṣṭhaḥ śravanāḥ utha śraviṣṭakaḥ kuṇiḥ ca kuṇibāhuḥ ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ kāśyapaḥ hi uśanāḥ ca eva cyavanaḥ ca bṛhaspatiḥ utathyaḥ vāmadevaḥ ca mahākālaḥ mahā anilaḥ yatīśvaraḥ hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyaḥ lokākṣiḥ kuthumī tathā plakṣaḥ dārbhāyaṇiḥ ca eva ketumant gautamaḥ tathā śālihotraḥ suveṣaḥ ca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ akṣapādaḥ kaṇādaḥ ca ulūkaḥ vatsaḥ eva ca ete śiṣyāḥ maheśasya yoga ācārya svarūpiṇaḥ saṃkhyā ca śatam eteṣām saha dvādaśa saṃkhyayā sarve pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasma uddhūlita vigrahāḥ sarva śāstra artha tattva jñāḥ veda vedāṅga pāragāḥ śiva āśrama ratāḥ sarve śiva jñāna parāyaṇāḥ sarve saṅga vinirmuktāḥ śiva eka āsakta cetasaḥ sarva dvaṃdva sahāḥ dhīrāḥ sarva bhūta hite ratāḥ ṛjavaḥ mṛdavaḥ svasthāḥ jita krodhāḥ jita indriyāḥ rudra akṣa mālā ābharaṇāḥ tripuṇḍra aṃkita mastakāḥ śīrṣakāḥ phala mūla aśana prāyāḥ prāṇāyāma parāyaṇāḥ mahā abhimāna saṃpannāḥ śiva dhyāna eka tatparāḥ samunmathita saṃsāra viṣa vṛkṣa aṅkura udgamāḥ prayātum eva sannaddhāḥ param śiva puram prati sa deśikān imān matvā nityam yaḥ śivam arcayet sa yāti śiva sāyujyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā iti śrī śiva mahāpurī saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivasya yogāvatāravarṇanam nāma navamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca prāyas tvam avatīrya urvyām pāśa vicchittaye nṛṇām tvattaḥ nyaḥ paramam bhāvam kaḥ jānīyāt śiva ātmakam tasmāt tava mukha udgīrṇam sākṣāt iva pinākinaḥ mad śiva jñāna amṛtam pītvā na mama tṛptam abhūt manaḥ sākṣāt sarva jagat kartuḥ bhartuḥ aṅkam samāśritā sthāne pṛṣṭam tvayā kṛṣṇa tat vakṣyāmi yathātatham tadā devyāḥ priya sakhī su smita āsyā śubhāvatī phullāni ati manojñāni puṣpāṇi samudāharat tatas svam aṃkam āropya devīm alaṃkṛtya ca tebhiḥ puṣpaiḥ āste hṛṣṭataraḥ svayam atha antaḥpura cārinyaḥ devyaḥ divya vibhūṣaṇāḥ antaraṅgāḥ gaṇa indrāḥ ca sarva loka maheśvarīm bhartāram paripūrṇam ca sarva loka mahā īśvaram cāmara āsakta hastāḥ ca devīm devam siṣevire tatas priyāḥ kathāḥ vṛttāḥ vinodāya maheśayoḥ trāṇāya ca nṝṇām loke ye śivam śaraṇam gatāḥ kena vaśyaḥ mahādevaḥ martyānām manda cetasām mad mad tattva ādi aśaktānām ātmanām akṛtātmanām paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca na karmaṇā na tapasā na japaiḥ na āsana ādibhiḥ na jñānena na ca anyena vaśyaḥ aham śraddhayā vinā śraddhā mayi asti ced puṃsām yena kena api hetunā vaśyaḥ spṛśyaḥ ca dṛśyaḥ ca pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣyaḥ eva ca sādhyā tasmāt mayi śaddhā mām vaśīkartum icchatā hetuḥ svadharmasya rakṣaṇam varṇinām iha sva varṇa āśrama dharmeṇa vartate yaḥ tu mānavaḥ mahā āmnāya siddham akhilam dharmam āśramiṇām iha brahmanā kathitam pūrvam mama eva ājñā puraḥsaram na atyanta phala bhūyiṣṭhaḥ kleśāyāḥ sa samanvitaḥ tena dharmeṇa mahatām śraddhām prāpya su durlabhām teṣām sukhena mārgeṇa dharma kāma artha muktayaḥ tasmin bhaktimatām eva madīyānām tu varṇinām adhikāraḥ na ca anyeṣām iti ājñā naiṣṭhikī mama tad ājñaptena mārgeṇa varṇinaḥ mad upāśrayāḥ mala māyā ādi pāśebhyaḥ vimuktāḥ mad prasādāt param madīyam āsādya punarāvṛtti durlabham paramam mama sādharmyam prāpya nirvṛtim āyayuḥ alabdha lābhaḥ eva eṣa koṭi koṭi guṇa adhikaḥ mama avatārāḥ hi śubhe yoga ācārya chalena tu ayuktānām abuddhīnām abhaktānām sureśvari tatas yatnāt samāśrayet yat anyatra śramam kuryāt mokṣa mārga bahiṣkṛtaḥ jñānam kriyā ca caryā ca yogaḥ ca iti sureśvari catuṣpādaḥ samākhyātaḥ mama dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ paśu pāśa pati jñānam jñānam iti abhidhīyate aśvamedha gaṇāt śreṣṭham devi citta prasādhanam mukti dam ca tathā hi etat duṣprāpyam viṣaya eṣiṇām pravartate yoga jñaḥ patitaḥ vā api mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ dayā kāryā atha satatam ahiṃsā jñāna saṃgrahaḥ adhyāpanam ca adhyayanam yajanam yājanam tathā hyānam īśvara bhāvaḥ ca satatam jñāna śīla tā acirāt eva vijñānam labdhvā yogam ca vindati dagdhvā deham imam jñānī kṣaṇāt jñāna agninā priye tasmāt niyogāt yogī puṇya apuṇyam vivarjayet samabhyaset na yajanti hi mām yuktāḥ sama loṣṭa aśma kāñcanāḥ nitya yuktaḥ muniḥ śreṣṭhaḥ mad bhaktaḥ ca samāhitaḥ āpnuyāt atha avirakta cittāḥ ye varṇinaḥ mad upāśritāḥ dvidhā mad pūjanam jñeyam bāhyam ābhyantaram tathā manaḥ kāya bhedāt ca tridhā mad bhajanam viduḥ tapaḥ karma japaḥ dhyānam jñānam vā iti anupūrvaśas mad nāma niratā vāṇī vā aGmatā khalu na itarā liṅgaiḥ mad śāsana ādiṣṭaiḥ tripuṇḍra ādibhiḥ aṃkitaḥ mama upacāra nirataḥ kāyaḥ kāyaḥ na ca itaraḥ mad arcā karma vijñeyam bāhye yāga ādinā ucyate japaḥ pañcākṣara abhyāsaḥ praṇava abhyāsaḥ eva ca rudra adhyāya ādika abhyāsaḥ na veda adhyayana ādikam na ātma ādi artha samādhayaḥ mama āgama artha vijñānam jñānam na anya artha vedanam prāk vāsanā vaśāt devi tattva niṣṭhām samācaret bāhyāt ābhyantaram śreṣṭham bhavet śataguṇa adhikam asaṃkara tvāt doṣāṇām dṛṣṭānām api asaṃbhavāt śaucam ābhyantaram vidyāt na bāhyam śaucam ucyate antar śauca vimukta ātmā śuciḥ api aśuciḥ yatas bahis vā abhyantaram vā atha mayā bhāvaḥ hi gṛhyate bhāva eka ātmā kriyā devi mama dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ manasā karmaṇā vācā hi an apekṣya phalam kvacid phala arthī tad abhāve mām parityaktum kṣamaḥ yatas phala anapekṣayā yeṣām manaḥ mad pravaṇam bhavet prārthayeyuḥ phalam paścāt bhaktāḥ te api mama priyāḥ prāk saṃskāra vaśāt eva ye viciṃtya phala aphale prapadyante mama priyatamāḥ matāḥ mama api lābhaḥ tad lābhāt na aparaḥ parameśvari mahātmanām ananyānām mayi saṃnyasta cetasām aṣṭadhā lakṣaṇam prāhuḥ mama dharma adhikāriṇām mad bhakta jana vātsalyam pūjāyām ca anumodanam mad kathā śravaṇe bhaktiḥ svara netra aṅga vikriyāḥ mama anusmaraṇam nityam yaḥ ca mām upajīvati sa vipra indraḥ muniḥ śrīmān saḥ yatiḥ saḥ ca paṇḍitaḥ tasya aham na praṇaśyāmi saḥ ca me na praṇaśyati iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivabhaktivarṇanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca atha vakṣyāmi deveśi bhaktānām adhikāriṇām tris snānam ca agni kāryam ca liṅga arcanam anukramam dānam īśrara bhāvaḥ ca dayā sarvatra sarvadā satyam santoṣam āstikyam ahiṃsā sarva jantuṣu ca mahā śaucam śikhā upavītam ca uṣṇīṣam ca uttarīyakam niṣiddha asevanam ca eva bhasma rudrākṣa dhāraṇam parvaṇi abhyarcanam devi caturdaśyām viśeṣataḥ pānam ca brahmakūrcasya māsi māsi yathāvidhi abhyarcanam viśeṣeṇa tena eva snāpya mām priye tathā paryuṣita annasya yāvakasya viśeṣataḥ sāmānyam sarva varṇānām brāhmaṇānām viśeṣataḥ kṣamā śāntiḥ ca santoṣaḥ satyam asteyam eva ca sarva saṅga nivṛttiḥ ca daśa etāni viśeṣataḥ liṅgāni yoginām bhūyas divā bhikṣā aśanam tathā vānaprastha āśrama sthānām samānam idam iṣyate rātrau na bhojanam kāryam sarveṣām brahmacāriṇām adhyāpanam yājanam ca kṣatriyasya a pratigrahaḥ vaiśyasya ca viśeṣeṇa mayā na atra vidhīyate rakṣaṇam sarva varṇānām yuddhe śatru vadhaḥ tathā duṣṭa pakṣi mṛgāṇām ca duṣṭānām śātanam nṛṇām aviśvāsaḥ ca sarvatra viśvāsaḥ mama yogiṣu strī saṃsargaḥ ca kāleṣu camū rakṣaṇam eva ca sadā saṃcāritaiḥ cāraiḥ loka vṛttānta vedanam sadā astra dhāraṇam ca eva bhasma kañcuka dhāraṇam rājñām mama āśrama sthānām eṣa dharmasya saṃgrahaḥ kathyate śuśrūṣā itara varṇānām dharmaḥ śūdrasya kathyate udyāna karaṇam ca eva mama kṣetra samāśrayaḥ brahmacaryam vanasthānām yatīnām brahmacāriṇām strīṇām tu bhartṛ śuśrūṣā dharmaḥ na anyaḥ sanātanaḥ yā nārī bhartṛ śuśrūṣām vihāya vrata tatparā sā nārī narakam yāti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā atha bhartṛ vihīnāyāḥ vakṣye dharmam sanātanam brahmacaryam sadā snānam bhasmanā salilena vā śāntiḥ maunam kṣamā nityam saṃvibhāgaḥ yathāvidhi aṣṭābhyām ca caturdaśyām paurṇamāsyām viśeṣataḥ ekādaśyām ca vidhivat upavāsa umama arcanam iti saṃkṣepāt proktaḥ mayā āśrama niṣeviṇām brahma kṣatra viśām devi yatīnām brahmacāriṇām tathā eva vānaprasthānām gṛhasthānām ca sundari hi śūdrāṇām atha nārīṇām dharmaḥ eṣa sanātanaḥ tvayā aham deveśi sadā jāpyaḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ atha ye mānavāḥ loke sva icchayā dhṛta vigrahāḥ bhāva atiśaya saṃpannāḥ pūrva saṃskāra saṃyutāḥ api teṣām mama ātma vijñānam viśuddhānām vivekinām mad prasādāt viśuddhānām duḥkham āśrama rakṣaṇāt na asti kṛtyam akṛtyam ca samādhiḥ vā parāyaṇam na vidhiḥ na niṣedhaḥ ca teṣām mama yathā tathā tathā eva kṛtakṛtyānām teṣām api na saṃśayaḥ mad bhaktānām hita arthāya mānuṣam bhāvam āśritāḥ rudra lokāt paribhraṣṭāḥ te rudrāḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ mama anuśāsanam yadvat brahma ādīnām pravartakam tathā narāṇām anyeṣām tad niyogaḥ pravartakaḥ mama ājñā dhāra bhāvena sadbhāva atiśayena ca mayi bhāvavatām puṃsām prāk adṛṣṭa artha gocarāḥ kampa svedaḥ aśru pātaḥ ca kaṇṭhe ca svara vikriyā muhur prākṛtān iva manvānaḥ na avajānīta paṇḍitaḥ avajñānam kṛtam teṣu naraiḥ vyāmūḍha cetanaiḥ āyuḥ śriyam kulam śīlam hitvā nirayam āvahet brahma viṣṇu sureśānām api tūlāyate padam mattaḥ nyat anapekṣāṇām uddhṛtānām mahātmanām aśuddham bauddham aiśvaryam prākṛtam pauruṣam tathā ittham śrīkaṇṭha nāthena śivena paramātmanā hitāya jagantām uktaḥ jñāna sāra artha saṃgrahaḥ sa itihāsa purāṇāni vidyā vyākhyāna vistaraḥ jñānam jñeyam anuṣṭheyam adhikāraḥ atha sādhanam sādhyam ca iti ṣaṣ arthānām saṃgraha tva eṣa saṃgrahaḥ guroḥ adhikṛtam jñānam jñeyam pāśaḥ paśuḥ patiḥ liṅga arcana ādi anuṣṭheyam bhaktaḥ tu adhikṛtaḥ api yaḥ sādhanam śiva mantra ādyam sādhyam śiva samāna tā ṣaṣ artha saṃgrahasya asya jñānāt sarvajña tā ucyate prathamam karma yajña ādeḥ bhaktyā vitta anusārāt na karma karaṇīyam hi bahis tasya mahātmanāḥ jñāna amṛtena tṛptasya bhaktyā śaiva śiva ātmanaḥ na antar na ca bahis kṛṣṇaiḥ kṛtyam asti kadācana nena jñeyam ālokya ajñānam ca api parityajet na ekāgram ced śive cittam kim kṛtena api karmaṇā akāgram eva ced cittam kim kṛtena api karmaṇā tasmāt karmāṇi a kṛtvā vā kṛtvā vā antar bahis kramāt mahe niviṣṭa cittānām pratiṣṭhita dhiyām satām iha unnamaḥ śivāya iti mantreṇa anena siddhayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivajñānavarṇanam nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca pañcākṣarasya māhātmyam śrotum icchāmi tattvāt pañcākṣarasya māhātmyam varṣa koṭi śataiḥ api aśakyam vistarāt vaktum tasmāt saṃkṣepāt śṛṇu yaḥ idam ubhayatra sarveṣām śiva bhaktānām aśeṣa artha sādhakaḥ tat alpa akṣaram artha āḍhyam veda sāram vimukti dam hi ājñā siddham asaṃdigdham vākyam etat śiva ātmakam nānā siddhi yutam divyam loka citta anurañjakam su niścita artham gambhīram vākyam tat pārameśvaram prāha unnamaḥ śivāya iti sarvajñaḥ sarva dehinām tat bījam sarva vidyānām mantram ādyam ṣaṣ akṣaram ati sūkṣmam mahā artham ca jñeyam tat vaṭa bīja vat devaḥ guṇatraya atītaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva kṛt prabhuḥ iśāna ādyāni sūkṣmāṇi brahmāni eka akṣarāṇi tu mantre ṣaṣ akṣare sūkṣme pañca brahma tanuḥ śivaḥ sthitaḥ sākṣāt svabhāvāt mantraḥ tad vācakaḥ smṛtaḥ ayam anādi saṃsthitaḥ tayoḥ yathā anādi pravṛttaḥ yam ghora saṃsāra sāgaraḥ api hi tathā anādi saṃsārāt mocakaḥ sthitaḥ tadvat saṃsāra doṣāṇām pratipakṣaḥ śivaḥ smṛtaḥ pradhāna paramāṇu ādi yāvat kiṃcid acetanam na tat kartṛ svayam dṛṣṭam buddhimat kāraṇam vinā dharma adharma upadeśaḥ ca bandha mokṣau vicāraṇāt na sarvajñam vinā puṃsām ādisargaḥ prasiddhi ati tasmāt anādiḥ sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaḥ sadāśivaḥ asti nāthaḥ paritrātā puṃsām saṃsāra sāgarāt sarvajñaḥ paripūrṇaḥ ca śivaḥ jñeyaḥ śiva āgame abhidhāna abhidheya tvāt mantraḥ siddhaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ etāvat tu śiva jñānam etāvat paramam padam mad om namaḥ śivāya iti śiva vākyam ṣaṣ akṣaram mad vidhi vākyam idam śaivam na artha vādam śiva ātmakam yaḥ sarvajñaḥ su saṃpūrṇaḥ svabhāva vimalaḥ śivaḥ loka anugraha karttā ca sa mṛṣārtham katham vadet yat yathā avasthitam vastu guṇa doṣaiḥ svabhāvāt yāvat phalam ca tat pūrṇam sarvajñaḥ tu yathā vadet rāga ajñāna ādibhiḥ doṣaiḥ grasta tvāt anṛtam vadet ajñāta aśeṣa doṣeṇa sarva jñeya śivena yat praṇītam amalam vākyam tat pramāṇam na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt īśvara vākyāni śraddheyāni vipaścitā rāga dveṣa anṛta krodha kāma tṛṣṇā anusāri yat saṃskṛtena api kim tena mṛdunā lalitena vā tad avidyā rāga vākyena saṃsāra kleśa hetunā yat śrutvā jāyate śreyaḥ rāga ādīnām ca saṃśayaḥ bahu tve api hi mantrāṇām sarvajñena śivena yaḥ sa aṅgāni veda śāstrāṇi saṃsthitāni ṣaṣ akṣare mantraḥ ṣaṣ akṣaraḥ bhinnaḥ sūtram vṛtyā ātmanā yathā śiva jñānāni yāvanti yāni ca ṣaṣ akṣarasya sūtrasya tāni bhāṣyam samāsatas yasya unnamaḥ śivāya iti mantraḥ ayam hṛdi saṃsthitaḥ tena adhītam śrutam tena kṛtam sarvam anuṣṭhitam yena unnamaḥ śivāya iti mantra abhyāsaḥ sthirīkṛtaḥ namaskāra ādi saṃyuktam śivāya iti akṣara trayam antyajaḥ vā adhamaḥ vā api mūrkhaḥ vā paṇḍitaḥ api vā pañcākṣara jape niṣṭhaḥ mucyate pāpa pañjarāt iti uktam parameśeṇa devyā pṛṣṭena śūlinā hitāya sarva martyānām dvijānām tu viśeṣataḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe paṃcākṣaramāhātmyavarṇanam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tasmin varṇa āśrama ācāre saṃkaṭe samupasthite paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca āśritya paramām vidyām hṛdyām pañcākṣarīm mama bhaktyā ca bhāvitātmānaḥ mucyante kali jāḥ narāḥ dūṣitānām kṛtaghnānām nindakānām chala ātmanām lubdhānām vakra manasām api mad pravaṇa ātmanām mama pañcākṣarā vidyā saṃsāra bhaya tāriṇī paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca sa mantrakam mām patitaḥ pūjayet yadi mohitaḥ nārakī syāt na saṃdehaḥ mama pañcākṣaram vinā abbhakṣāḥ vāyubhakṣāḥ ca ye ca anye vrata karśitāḥ bhaktyā pañcākṣareṇa eva yaḥ hi mām sakṛt arcayet tasmāt tapāṃsi yajñāḥ ca vratāni niyamāḥ tathā pañcākṣara arcanasya ete koṭi aṃśena api no samaḥ baddhaḥ vā api atha muktaḥ vā pāśāt pañcākṣareṇa yaḥ pūjayet mām saḥ mucyeta na atra kāryā vicāraṇā arudraḥ vā sa rudraḥ vā sakṛt pañcākṣareṇa yaḥ pūjayet patitaḥ vā api mūḍhaḥ vā mucyate naraḥ ṣaṣ akṣareṇa vā devi tathā pañca akṣareṇa vā alabdha alabdhaḥ eva iha koṭi koṭi guṇa adhikaḥ labdhvā saṃpūjayet yaḥ tu maitrī ādi guṇa saṃyutaḥ mama pañca akṣare mantre tasmāt śreṣṭhataraḥ hi saḥ pañcākṣara prabhāvena loka veda mahā ṛṣayaḥ tiṣṭhanti śāśvatāḥ dharmāḥ devāḥ sarvam idam jagant sarvam prakṛtim āpannam tatra saṃlayam eṣyati tadā vedāḥ ca śāstrāṇi sarve pañcākṣare sthitāḥ te nāśam na eva saṃprāptāḥ mad śaktyā hi anupālitāḥ tatas sṛṣṭiḥ abhūt mattaḥ prakṛti ātma prabhedāt guṇa mūrti ātmanām ca eva tatas vā antara saṃhṛtiḥ tadā nārāyaṇaḥ śete devaḥ māyā mayām tanum tad nābhi paṅkajāt jātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ sisṛkṣamāṇaḥ lokān trīn na saktaḥ hi asahāyavān munīn daśa sasarja ādau mānasān amita ojasaḥ teṣām siddhi vivṛddhi artham mām provāca pitāmahaḥ mad putrāṇām mahādevaiḥ śaktim dehi maheśvaraiḥ pañca akṣarāṇi kramaśas proktavan padmayonaye sa pañca vadanaiḥ tāni gṛhṇan lokapitāmahaḥ vācya vācaka bhāvena jñātavan mām maheśvaram jñātvā prayogam vividham siddha mantraḥ prajāpatiḥ te ca labdhvā mantra ratnam sākṣāt lokapitāmahāt tad ājñaptena mārgeṇa mad ārādhana kāṃkṣiṇaḥ mad priyaḥ satatam śrīmān mad bhaktaiḥ rakṣitaḥ sadā tasya abhyāśe tapaḥ tīvram lokam sraṣṭum samutsukāḥ divyam varṣa sahasram tu vāyubhakṣāḥ samācaran teṣām bhaktim aham dṛṣṭvā sadyas pratyakṣatām iyām bīja śaktim ca daivatam nyāsam ṣaḍaṅgam digbandham viniyogam aśeṣatas proktavan aham āryāṇām jagat sṛṣṭi vivṛddhaye tatas te mantra māhātmyāt ṛṣayaḥ tapasā idhitāḥ sṛṣṭim vitanvate samyak sa deva asura mānuṣām madhye namaḥ prayoktavyam śivāya tu tatas param sā eṣā pañcākṣarī vidyā sarva śrutiśiraḥ gatā sarva jātasya sarvasya bīja bhūtā sanātanā mad mukha udgīrṇā sā mama eva asti vācakā catur bhujā tri nayanā bāla indu kṛta śekharā padma utpala karā saumyā vara da abhaya pāṇikā sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannā sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitā sita padmāsana āsīnā nīla kuñcita mūrdhajā asyāḥ pañcavidhāḥ varṇāḥ prasphurat raśmi maṇḍalāḥ pītaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tathā dhūmraḥ svarṇa ābhaḥ raktaḥ eva ca pṛthak prayojyāḥ yadi ete bindu nāda vibhūṣitāḥ bījam dvitīyam bījeṣu mantrasya asya varānane dīrgha pūrvam turīyasya pañcamam śaktim ādiśet vāmadevaḥ nāma ṛṣiḥ paṅktiḥ chandaḥ udāhṛtam devatā śivaḥ eva aham mantrasya asya varānane atriḥ varārohe viśvāmitraḥ tathā aṅgirāḥ bharadvājaḥ ca varṇānām kramaśas ca ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ gāyatrī anuṣṭubh triṣṭubh ca chandāṃsi bṛhatī virāj mama pañca mukhāni āhuḥ sthāne teṣām varānane pūrva ādeḥ ca ūrdhva paryantam nakāra ādi yathākramam taḥ prathamaḥ varṇaḥ caturthaḥ ca dvitīyakaḥ pañcamaḥ svaritaḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ nihataḥ smṛtaḥ mūlavidyā śivam śaivam sūtram pañcākṣaram tathā nāmāni asya vijānīyāt śaivam mama hṛdayam mahat yakāraḥ yakāraḥ astram namaḥ svāhā vaṣaṭ hum vauṣaṭ iti api phaṭ iti api ca varṇānām ante yadā tadā tatra api pañcamaḥ varṇaḥ dvādaśa svara bhūṣitaḥ ha tā asmāt anena mantreṇa manaḥ vāc kāya bhedāt bhavayoḥ arcanam kuryāt japa homa ādikam tathā yathāprajñam yathākālam yathāśāstram yathāmati yathāśakti yathāsampad yathāyogam yathārati yadā kadāpi vā bhaktyā yatra kutra api vā kṛtā yena kena api vā devi pūjā muktim nayiṣyate mad priyam ca śivam ca eva krameṇa api akrameṇa vā tathā api mama bhaktāḥ ye na atyanta vivaśāḥ punar teṣām sarveṣu śāstreṣu mayā iva niyamaḥ kṛtaḥ tatra ādau saṃpravakṣyāmi mantra saṃgrahaṇam śubham yam vinā niṣphalam jāpyam yena vā saphalam bhavet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe paṃcākṣaramāhātmyavarṇanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca mājñā hīnam kriyā hīnam śraddhā hīnam varānane ājñā artham dakṣiṇā hīnam sadā japtam ca niṣphalam ātmakam jāpitam sat guṇa upetam dhyāna yoga parāyaṇam mad ācāryam pūjayet vipraḥ sarvadā ati prayatnāt hasti aśva ratha ratnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāni ca bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi dhānyāni ca dhanāni ca na kurvīta yadi icchet mantram jñānam ca eva krameṇa tu evam tuṣṭaḥ guruḥ śiṣyam pūjakam vatsara uṣitam mahā bhūtam anahaṃkāram snātam śucim upoṣitam snāpayitvā viśuddhi artham pūrṇa kumbha ghṛtena vai alaṃkṛtya su veṣam ca gandha sraj vastra bhūṣaṇaiḥ puṇyāham vācayitvā ca brāhmaṇān abhipūjya ca samudra tīre nadyām ca goṣṭhe devālaye api vā anugṛhya tatas dadyāt jñānam mama yathāvidhi śivam ca astu śubham ca astu śobhanaḥ astu priyaḥ astu iti evam dadyāt guruḥ mantram ājñām ca eva tatas param evam labdhvā guroḥ mantram ājñām ca eva samāhitaḥ japet akṣara lakṣam vai catur guṇitam ādarāt nakta āśī saṃyamī yaḥ saḥ pauraścaraṇikaḥ smṛtaḥ yaḥ puraścaraṇam kṛtvā nitya jāpī bhavet punar snānam kṛtvā śucau deśe baddhvā rucira mānasam tvayā mām hṛdi saṃcintya saṃciṃtya sva gurum tatas udak mukhaḥ prāñc mukhaḥ vā maunī ca ekāgra mānasaḥ mantra nyāsa ādikam kṛtvā saphalīkṛta vigrahaḥ mayoḥ vigrahau dhyāyan prāṇa apānau niyamya ca vidyā sthānam svakam rūpam ṛṣin chandaḥ adhidaivatam bījam śaktim tathā vākyam smṛtvā pañcākṣarīm japet uttamam mānasam jāpyam upāṃśum ca eva madhyamam adhamam vācikam prāhuḥ āgama artha viśāradāḥ yat ucca nīca svaritaiḥ spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa pada akṣaraiḥ mantram uccārayet vācā vācikaḥ ayam japaḥ smṛtaḥ jihvā mātra parispandāt īṣat uccāritaḥ api vā aparaiḥ aśrutaḥ kiṃcid śrutaḥ vā upāṃśuḥ ucyate dhyā yat akṣara śreṇyā varṇāt varṇam padāt padam bhūyas kathyate mānasaḥ japaḥ vācikaḥ tu ekaḥ eva syāt upāṃśuḥ śatam ucyate sāhasram mānasaḥ proktaḥ sagarbhaḥ tu śata adhikaḥ praśasyate catvāriṃśat samāvṛttīḥ prāṇān āyamya saṃsmaret mantram mantra artha vid dhīmān aśaktaḥ śaktitas japet pañcakam trikam ekam vā prāṇāyāmam samācaret eṣu pañcavidheṣu ekaḥ karttavyaḥ śaktitas japaḥ rekhayā aṣṭaguṇam vidyāt putrajīvaiḥ daśa adhikam śatam syāt śaṅkha maṇibhiḥ pravālaiḥ tu sahasrakam padmākṣaiḥ daśa lakṣam tu sauvarṇaiḥ koṭiḥ ucyate triṃśat akṣaiḥ kṛtā mālā dhana dā japa karmaṇi saptaviṃśati saṃkhyātaiḥ akṣaiḥ puṣṭi pradā bhavet pañcaviṃśati saṃkhyātaiḥ kṛtā muktim prayacchati aṅguṣṭham mokṣa dam vidyāt tarjanīm śatru nāśinīm madhyamām dhana dām śāntim karoti eṣā hi anāmikā aṣṭottaraśatam mālā tatra syāt uttamottamā mālā pañcāśadbhiḥ tu madhyamā catuḥ pañcāśat akṣaiḥ tu hṛd śreṣṭhā hi prakīrtitā iti evam mālayā kuryāt japam kasmai na darśayet kaniṣṭhā kṣariṇī proktā japa karmaṇi śobhanā aṅguṣṭhena vinā japyam kṛtam tat aphalam yatas viduḥ puṇya araṇye tathā ārāme sahasraguṇam ucyate ayutam parvate puṇye nadyām lakṣam udāhṛtam viprāṇām ca gavām ca eva saṃnidhau śasyate japaḥ tad pūrva abhimukham vaśyam dakṣiṇam ca ābhicārikam paścimam dhanadam vidyāt auttaram śātidam bhavet sūrya agni vipra devānām gurūṇām api saṃnidhau anyeṣām ca prasaktānām mantram na vimukhaḥ japet uṣṇīṣī kuñcukī namraḥ mukta keśaḥ gala āvṛtaḥ trīṇi niṣṭhīvana vijṛmbhaṇe darśanam ca śva nīcānām varjayet japa karmaṇi mām ācamet sambhave teṣām smaret vā mām tvayā saha jyotīṃṣi ca prapaśyet vā kuryāt vā prāṇasaṃyamam tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat yāna śayyā adhirūḍhaḥ vā cintā vyākulitaḥ atha vā sat ācāraḥ japan śuddham dhyāyan bhadram samaśnute ācāraḥ paramaḥ dharmaḥ ācāraḥ paramam dhanam puruṣaḥ loke bhavati ninditaḥ paratra ca sukhī na syāt tasmāt ācāravān bhavet tasya tena samācāraḥ sat ācāraḥ na ca itaraḥ sat ācārasya tasya āhuḥ āstikyam mūla kāraṇam māstikaḥ ced pramāda ādyaiḥ sat ācārāt avicyutaḥ na duṣyati naraḥ nityam tasmāt āstika tām vrajet yathā iha asti sukham duḥkham sukṛtaiḥ duṣkṛtaiḥ api na vācyam yasya kasya api nāstikasya atha vā paśoḥ pañcākṣarāt param na asti paritrāṇam kalau yuge aśuceḥ vā śuceḥ vā api mantraḥ na ca niṣphalaḥ anācāravatām puṃsām aviśuddha ṣaḍadhvanām an ādiṣṭaḥ api guruṇā mantraḥ ayam na ca niṣphalaḥ asādhitaḥ sādhitaḥ vā sidhya tvena na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt mantra antarān tyaktvā sa apāyā anadhikārāt āśramet paramām vidyām sākṣāt pañcākṣarām budhaḥ ye doṣāḥ sarva mantrāṇām na te asmin saṃbhavanti api sahasā viniyuṅkta tasmāt eṣa mahā balaḥ evam sākṣāt mahādevyai mahādevena śūlinā hitāḥ jagantām uktaḥ pañcākṣara vidhiḥ yathā yaḥ idam kīrtayet bhaktyā śṛṇuyāt vā samāhitaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe paṃcākṣaramahimavarṇanam nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca tad prayoga vidhānam ca sākṣāt śruti samam yathā idānīm śrotum icchāmi śiva saṃskāram uttamam saṃskāram paramam puṇyam śivena pati bhāṣitam samyak kṛta adhikāraḥ syāt pūjā ādiṣu naraḥ yatas yena vijñānam kṣīyate pāśa bandhanam tasmāt saṃskāraḥ eva ayam dīkṣā iti api ca kathyate māntrī ca eva śiva āgame dīkṣā upadiśyate tredhā śivena paramātmanā guroḥ āloka mātreṇa sparśāt saṃbhāṣaṇāt api sadyas saṃjñā bhavet jantoḥ pāśa upakṣaya kāriṇī sā dīkṣā śāmbhavī proktā sā punar bhidyate dvidhā tīvrā tīvratarā ca iti pakṣaya bhedāt yayā syāt nirvṛtiḥ sadyas sā eva tīvratarā matā tīvrā tu jīvatā atyantam puṃsaḥ pāpa viśodhakā śaktī jñānavatī dīkṣā śiṣya deham praviśya tu kriyate māntrā kriyāvatī dīkṣā kuṇḍa maṇḍala pūrvakā manda mandatara uddeśāt kartavyā guruṇā bahis śaktipāta anusāreṇa śiṣyaḥ anugraham arhati śaiva dharma anusārasya tad mūla tvāt samāsatas tasmāt liṅgāni saṃvīkṣya śaktipātasya bhūyasaḥ jñānena kriyayā vā atha guruḥ śiṣyam viśodhayet tasmāt sarva prakāreṇa guruḥ śiṣyam parīkṣayet sā yasmāt paramā śaktiḥ prabodha ānanda rūpiṇī hi yathā syāt kampa romāñca svara netra aṅga vikriyāḥ hi śiṣyaḥ api lakṣaṇaiḥ ebhiḥ kuryāt guru parīkṣaṇam tad samparkaiḥ śiva arcā ādau saṃgataiḥ vā atha tad gataiḥ śiṣyaḥ tu śikṣaṇīya tvāt guroḥ gaurava kāraṇāt yaḥ guruḥ sa śivaḥ proktaḥ yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ guruḥ vā śivaḥ eva atha vidyākāreṇa saṃsthitaḥ yathā śivaḥ tathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ śiva vidyā gurūṇām ca pūjayā sadṛśam phalam tasmāt sarva prayatnena yasya ājñām śirasā vahet yadi guru ājñām manasā api na laṃghayet aśnute samakṣam yadi kurvīta sarvam ca anujñayā guroḥ bhavet guruḥ devaḥ yatas sākṣāt tat gṛham deva mandiram pāpinām ca yathā saṅgāt tad pāpāt patitaḥ bhavet tathā pāpam vilīyeta hi ācāryasya samīpatas tathā ayam api santuṣṭaḥ guruḥ pāpam kṣaṇāt dahet manasā karmaṇā vācā guroḥ krodham na kārayet tasya krodhena dahyante hi āyuḥ śrī jñāna satkriyāḥ tad krodha kāriṇaḥ ye syuḥ teṣām yajñāḥ ca niṣphalāḥ yamaḥ ca niyamāḥ ca eva na atra kāryā vicāraṇā manasā karmaṇā vācā gurum uddiśya yatnatas hreyaḥ arthī ced naraḥ dhīmān na mithyā ācāram ācaret guroḥ hitam priyam kuryāt ādiṣṭaḥ vā na vā sadā asamakṣam samakṣam vā tasya kāryam samācaret guruḥ ced guṇavān prājñaḥ parama ānanda bhāsakaḥ na punar nāma mātreṇa saṃvid ārahitaḥ tu yaḥ anyonyam tārayet naukā kim śilā tārayet śilām etasyāḥ nāma mātreṇa muktiḥ vai nāmamātrikā paśubhiḥ preritaḥ ca api paśu tvam na ativartate yāvat vijñāyate tāvat sevanīyaḥ mumukṣubhiḥ jñāte tasmin sthirā bhaktiḥ yāvat tattvam samāśrayet vatsarāt api śiṣyeṇa saḥ anyam gurum upāśrayet tatra ādau upasaṃgamya brāhmaṇam vedapāragam gurum ārādhayet prājñam śubhagam priya darśanam sarva abhaya pradātāram karuṇā ākrānta mānasam toṣayet tam prayatnena manasā karmaṇā girā tasmāt dhanāni ratnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi yāna śayyā āsanāni ca etāni gurave dadyāt bhaktyā vitta anusārāt vitta śāṭhyam na kurvīta yadi icchet paramām gatim nivedya paścāt sva ātmānam sa anvayam sa parigraham yadā śivāya sva ātmānam dattavan deśika ātmane guruḥ ca sva āśritam śiṣyam varṣam ekam parīkṣayet brāhmaṇam kṣatriyam vaiśyam dvi varṣam ca tri varṣakam prāṇa dravya pradāna ādyaiḥ ādeśaiḥ ca sama asamaiḥ uttamān ca adhame kṛtvā nīca anuttama karmaṇi saḥ tāḍitāḥ vā api ye viṣādam na yānti api te yogyāḥ saṃyatāḥ śuddhāḥ śiva saṃskāra karmaṇi ṛjavaḥ mṛdavaḥ su acchāḥ vinītāḥ sthira cetasaḥ hita ācāra samāyuktāḥ śiva bhaktāḥ dvijātayaḥ evam vṛtta samopetāḥ vā manaḥ kāya karmabhiḥ śodhyāḥ bodhyāḥ yathānyāyam iti śāstreṣu niścayaḥ na adhikāraḥ svatas nāryāḥ śiva saṃskāra karmaṇi tathā eva putra ādeḥ abhyanujñayā adhikāraḥ bhavati eva kanyāyāḥ pituḥ ājñayā śūdrāṇām martya jātīnām patitānām viśeṣataḥ tathā saṃkara jātīnām na adhva śuddhiḥ vidhīyate pāda udaka pradāna ādyaiḥ kuryuḥ pāpa viśodhanam tatra anuloma jātāḥ ye yuktāḥ eva dvijātiṣu teṣām adhva viśuddhi ādi kuryāt mātṛ kula ucitam yā tu kanyā sva pitṛ ādyaiḥ śiva dharme niyojitā sā bhaktāya pradātavyā na aparāya virodhine kṛtakṛtyā abhavat pūrvam tapasā ārādhya śaGkaram yathā nārāyaṇam devam tapasā ārādhya pāṇḍavān tad asvātantrya kṛtaḥ doṣaḥ na iha asti paramārthāt śiva dharme niyuktāyāḥ śiva śāsana gauravāt yasya saṃjāyate prajñā tasya na asti parājayaḥ kriyāvān yaḥ tu saṃskāraḥ kuṇḍa maṇḍapa pūrvakaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe dīkṣāvidhāne gurumāhātmyam nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ deśikaḥ prathamam kuryāt saṃskāram samaya āhvayam parīkṣya bhūmim vidhivat gandha varṇa rasa ādibhiḥ śilpi śāstra ukta mārgeṇa maṇḍapam tatra kalpayet kṛtvā vedim ca tad madhye kuṇḍāni parikalpayet aṣṭa dikṣu tathā dikṣu tatra aiśānyām punar kramāt pradhāna kuṇḍam kurvīta yat vā paścima bhāgāt pradhānam ekam eva atha kṛtvā śobhām prakalpayet vitāna dhvaja mālābhiḥ vividhābhiḥ anekaśas vedi madhye tatas kuryāt maṇḍalam śubha lakṣaṇam rakta hema ādibhiḥ cūrṇaiḥ īśvara āvāhana ucitam sindūra śālinī vāra cūrṇaiḥ eva atha nirdhanaḥ eka hastam dvi hastam vā sitam vā raktam eva vā eka hastasya padmasya karṇikā aṣṭa aṅgulā matā bhesarāṇi tad ardhāni śeṣam ca aṣṭadala ādikam kṛtvā śobha upaśobhā āḍhyam aiśānyām tasya kalpayet vrīhi taṇḍula siddhārtha tila puṣpa kuśa āstṛte tatra lakṣaṇa saṃyuktam śiva kumbham prasādhayet sauvarṇam rājatam vā api tāmra jam mṛd mayam tu vā sita sūtra āvṛtam kaṇṭhe nava vastra yuga āvṛtam muddha ambu pūrṇam utkūrcam sa dravyam sa pidhānakam mṛGgāram vardhanīm ca api śaṅkham ca cakram eva vā vinā sūtra ādikam sarvam padma pattram atha api vā maṇḍalasya tatas prācyām mantra kumbhe ca pūrvavat kṛtvā vidhivat īśasya mahā pūjām samācaret atha arṇavasya tīre vā nadyām goṣṭhe api vā girau kṛtvā pūrva uditam sarvam vinā vā maṇḍapa ādikam maṇḍalam pūrvavat kṛtvā sthaṇḍilam ca vibhāvasoḥ praviśya pūjā bhavanam prahṛṣṭa vadanaḥ guruḥ mahā pūjām maheśasya kṛtvā maṇḍala madhyatas tathā bhūyas āvāhya pūjayet paścima abhimukham dhyātvā yajñarakṣakam īśvaram yat kṛtvā mudrā ādikam sarvam mantra yāgam samācaret tatas śiva anale homam kuryāt deśika sattamaḥ pradhāna kuṇḍe paritas juhuyuḥ ca apare dvijāḥ ācāryāt pādam ardham vā homaḥ teṣām vidhīyate pradhānakuṇḍe eva atha juhuyāt deśika uttamaḥ japam ca vidhivat ca anye śiva bhakti parāyaṇāḥ nṛtyam gītam ca vādyam ca maṅgalāni aparāṇi ca pūjanam ca sadasyānām kṛtvā samyak vidhānāt puṇyāham kārayitvā atha punar saṃpūjya śaṃkaram prārthayet deśikaḥ devam śiṣya anugraha kāmyayā mocaya enam viśveśaiḥ ghṛṇayā ca ghṛṇā nidhe atha ca evam karomi iti labdha anujñaḥ tu deśikaḥ mānīya upoṣitam śiṣyam haviṣya āśinam eva vā eka aśanam vā viratam snātam prātar kṛta kriyam japantam praṇavam devam dhyāyantam kṛta maṅgalam dvārasya paścimasya agra maṇḍale dakṣiṇasya vā āsane mukham svayam prāñc vadanaḥ tiṣṭhan ūrdhva kāyam kṛta añjalim puṣpa kṣepeṇa santāḍya badhnīyāt locanam guruḥ tatas praveśayet śiṣyam guruḥ dvāreṇa maṇḍalam tena īritaḥ śambhoḥ ācaret tris pradakṣiṇam tatas suvarṇa sammiśram dattvā puṣpa añjalim prabhoḥ prāñc mukhaḥ ca udañc mukhaḥ vā praṇamet daṇḍa vat kṣitaḥ sa dṛṣṭvā maṇḍalam bhūyas praṇamet sa añjaliḥ prabhum atha āsīnam śiva ācāryaḥ maṇḍalasya tu dakṣiṇe upaveśya ātmanaḥ savye śiṣyam darbha āsane guruḥ mahādevam śiva hastam pravinyaset śiva tejaḥ mayam pāṇim śiva mantram udīrayet sarva aṅga ālaṃbanam ca eva kuryāt tena eva deśikaḥ mahā api praṇamet bhūmau deśikā kṛtam īśvaram huta āhuti trayam śiṣyam upaveśya yathā purā darbha agraiḥ saṃspṛśan tam ca vidyayā ātmānam āviśet namaskṛtya mahādevam nāḍīsaṃdhānam ācaret śiva śāstra ukta mārgeṇa kṛtvā prāṇasya nirgamam hiṣya deha praveśam ca smṛtvā mantrān tu tarpayet heyāḥ tisraḥ tathā aṅgānām aṅgaiḥ eva yathākramam tatas pūrṇāhutim dattvā prāyaścittāya deśikaḥ punar saṃpūjya deveśam samyak ācamya deśikaḥ hutvā ca eva yathānyāyam sva jātyā vaiśyam uddharet tasya evam janayet kṣātram uddhāram ca tatas punar rājanyam ca evam uddhṛtya kṛtvā vipram punar tayoḥ prokṣaṇam tāḍanam kṛtvā śiśoḥ sva ātmānam ātmani nāḍyā yathā uktayā vāyum recayet mantratas guruḥ nirgamya praviśet nāḍyā śiṣyasya hṛdayam tathā tam ādāya tayā nāḍyā mantrī saṃhāra mudrayā na pūrakeṇa niveśya enam ekībhāva artham ātmanaḥ tathā nāḍyā recakena yathā purā tasmāt ādāya śiṣyasya hṛdaye tat niveśayet hutvā paścāt dadyāt pūrṇāhutim tatas devasya dakṣiṇe śiṣyam upaveśya varāsane svastika āsanam ārūḍham vidhāya svayam samādāya ghaṭam pūrṇam pūrṇam eva prasāditam dhyāyamānaḥ śivam śiṣyam ābhiṣiṃceta deśikaḥ atha apanudya snāna ambu paridhāya sita ambaram vrajet upaveśya yathāpūrvam tam guruḥ darbha viṣṭare saṃpūjya maṇḍalam devam kara nyāsam samācaret samālabheta pāṇibhyām śiśum śivam udīrayet sakalīkaraṇam kṛtvā mātṛkā nyāsa vartmanā tatas śiva āsanam dhyātvā śiṣya mūrdhani deśikaḥ tatra āvāhya yathānyāyam arcayet manasā śivam iti vijñāpya tam śambhoḥ tejasā bhāsuram smaret saṃpūjya atha śivam śaivām ājñām prāpya śiva ātmakām tathā udīrayet sa tu baddhāñjaliḥ śrutvā mantram tad gata mānasaḥ śanais tam vyāharet śiṣya śiva ācāryasya śāsanāt tatas śāktam ca saṃdiśya mantram mantra vicakṣaṇaḥ uccārayitvā ca sukham tasmai maṅgalam ādiśet tatas samāsāt mantra artham vācya vācaka yogāt samadiśya īśvaram rūpam yogam āsanam ādiśet atha guru ājñayā śiṣyaḥ śiva agni guru saṃnidhau bhaktyā evam abhisaṃdhāya dīkṣā vākyam udīrayet varam prāṇa parityāgaḥ chedanam śirasaḥ api vā tāvat ārādhayet devam tad niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ tatas sa samayaḥ nāma bhaviṣyati śiva āśrame labdha adhikāraḥ guru ājñā pālakaḥ tad vaśaḥ bhavet dadyāt śiṣyāya mūlena rudrākṣam ca abhimantritam pratimā vā api devasya gūḍha deham atha api vā pūjā homa japa dhyāna sādhanāni ca sambhave saḥ api śiṣyaḥ śiva ācāryāt labdhāni bahu mānāt hi ādadīta ājñayā tasya deśikasya na ca anyathā mahilam śirasi ādhāya bhaktitaḥ rakṣayet pūjayet śambhum maṭhe vā gṛhe eva vā atas param śiva ācāram ādiśet asya deśikaḥ bhakti śraddhā anusāreṇa prajñāyāḥ ca anusārāt yat uktam yat samājñātam yat ca eva anyat prakīrtitam mahā ācāryeṇa samaye tat sarvam śirasā vahet mahā āgamasya grahaṇam vācanam śravaṇam tathā deśika deśāt kuryāt na sva icchāyāḥ na ca anyatas iti saṃkṣepāt proktaḥ saṃskāraḥ samaya āhvayaḥ sākṣāt śiva pura prāptau nṝṇām parama sādhanam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śiṣyasaṃskāravarṇanam nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atas param samāvekṣya guruḥ śiṣyasya yogyatām kalām tattvam ca bhuvanam varṇam padam atas param mantraḥ ca iti samāsena ṣaḍadhvā paripaṭhyate nivṛttya ādyāḥ kalāḥ pañca kalādhvā kathyate budhaiḥ vyāptāḥ kalābhiḥ itare tu adhvānaḥ pañca pañcabhiḥ śivatattva ādi bhūmi antam tattvādhvā samudāhṛtaḥ ṣaḍviṃśat saṃkhyayā upetaḥ śuddha aśuddha ubhaya ātmakaḥ prakīrtitaḥ pañcāśat rudra rūpāḥ tu varṇāḥ varṇa adhva saṃjñitāḥ aneka bheda saṃpannaḥ padādhvā samudāhṛtaḥ yathā śivaḥ na tattveṣu gaṇyate tattva nāyakaḥ ca eva na śakyate tasmāt adhva svarūpam ca vyāpya vyāpaka tām tathā tatra kṛtvā yathā purā dvi hasta mānam kurvīta prācyām kalaśa maṇḍalam tatas snātaḥ śiva ācāryaḥ sa śiṣyaḥ kṛta naityakaḥ praviśya maṇḍalam śambhoḥ pūjām pūrvavat ācaret tatra āḍhaka āvaraiḥ siddham taṇḍulaiḥ pāyasam prabhoḥ puratas kalpite vā atha maṇḍale varṇi maṃḍite sthāpayet pañca kalaśān dikṣu madhye ca deśikaḥ teṣu brahmāni mūla arṇaiḥ bindu nāda samanvitaiḥ madhyame kumbhe puruṣam puratas sthite aghoram dakṣiṇe vāme vāmam sadyam ca paścime rakṣām vidhāya mudrā ca baddhvā kumbha abhimantraṇam bhet śiva analaiḥ homam prārabhet yathā purā yat ardham pāyasam pūrvam homa artham parikalpitam tarpaṇa antam ca mantrāṇām kṛtvā karma yathā purā hutvā pūrṇāhutim teṣām tatas kuryāt pradīpanam okārāt anu pradakṣiṇa yogena bhrāmayet mūlavidyayā bhavet puṣpa añjalim paścāt upahārān nivedayet pānīyam ca tatas dadyāt dattvā vā ācamanam punar prokṣayet prokṣaṇīyāni gāna nāṭyāni kārayet liṅga ādau śivayoḥ cintām kṛtvā śakti ajapet śivam pradakṣiṇam praṇāmam ca stavam ca ātmasamarpaṇam vijñāpanam ca kāryāṇām kuryāt vinaya pūrvakam arghyam puṣpa añjalim dattvā baddhvā mudrām yathāvidhi paścāt kṣamāpayet svairam na niṣkṛtiḥ paredyus śaktitas dattvā suvarṇa ādyam śivāya ca śiva bhaktāya vā kṛtvā mahā pūjām śuciḥ bhavet iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe
