puṭāḥ dhyeyāḥ samāsīnāḥ yathāsukham sarva āvaraṇa devānām sva abhidhānaiḥ namas yutaiḥ puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjanam kuryāt natvā sarvān yathākramam eva api yajet haviḥ ca ṣaḍvidham deyam śuddham mudga annam eva ca pāyasam dadhi sammiśram gauḍam ca madhunā āplutam eteṣu ekam anekam vā nānā vyañjana saṃyutam bhakṣyāṇi apūpa mukhyāni svādumanti phalāni ca raktacandana puṣpa āḍhyam pānīyam ca ati śītalam mṛdu elā rasa aktam ca khaṇḍam pūga phalasya ca dalāni nāgavallyāḥ ca yuktāni khadira ādibhiḥ gaurāṇi svarṇa varṇāni vihitāni śivāni ca mahat eva sitam cūrṇam na ati rūkṣam na dūṣitam pūram ca atha kaṅkolam jāti ādi ca navam śubham syāt kastūrikā kuṅkumam ca rasaḥ mṛgamada ātmakaḥ puṣpāṇi surabhīni eva pavitrāṇi śubhāni ca nirgandhāni ugra gandhāni dūṣitāni uṣitāni ca svayam eva viśīrṇāni na deyāni śiva arcane vāsāṃsi ca mṛdūni eva tapanīya mayāni ca sarvāṇi etāni karpūra niryāsa aguru candanaiḥ mādhūpitāni puṣpa oghaiḥ vāsitāni samantataḥ candana aguru karpūra kāṣṭha guggulu cūrṇikaiḥ nityam pradīpitāḥ dīpāḥ śastāḥ karpūra saṃyutāḥ bhoḥ iṣṭam snāne ca pānake suvarṇa ratna yuktāni citrāṇi āstaraṇāni ca mṛdu upadhāna yuktāni sūkṣma tūla mayāni ca uccāvacāni ramyāṇi śayanāni sukhāni ca nadyaḥ samudra gāminyāḥ naṭāt vā ambhaḥ samāhṛtam śītam ca vastra pūtam tat viśiṣṭam snāna pānayoḥ chattram śaśi nibham cāru muktā dāma virājitam cāmare ca site sūkṣme cāmīkara pariṣkṛte rājahaṃsa dvaya ākāre ratna daṇḍa upaśobhite samantāt ratna sañchannam sraj vairaiḥ ca api bhūṣitam āsva pṛṣṭha ādi deśeṣu ratna cāmīkara ācitaḥ ca ramyāṇi nānā nāda karāṇi ca suvarṇa nirmitāni eva mauktika alaṃkṛtāni ca bherī mṛdaṅga muraja timiccha paṭaha ādayaḥ samudra kalpa sat nādāḥ kalpanīyāḥ prayatnāt bhāṇḍāni api ca ramyāṇi pattrāṇi api ca kṛtsnaśas tad ādhārāṇi sarvāṇi sauvarṇāni eva sādhayet maheśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ rāja āvasatha vat kalpyam śilpa śāstra ukta lakṣaṇam ucca prākāra saṃbhinnam bhūdhara ākāra gopuram tapta jāmbūnada mayam ratna stambha śata āvṛtam muktā dāma vitāna āḍhyam vidruma dvāra toraṇam cāmīkara mayaiḥ divyaiḥ mukuṭaiḥ kumbha lakṣaṇaiḥ rājanya arha nivāsaiḥ ca rāja vīthi ādi śobhitaiḥ procchrita prāṃśu śikharaiḥ prāsādaiḥ ca samantataḥ atyanta alaṃkṛta prāntam antara āvaraṇaiḥ iva uttama strī sahasraiḥ ca nṛtya geya viśāradaiḥ rakṣitam rakṣibhiḥ vīraiḥ gaja vāji ratha anvitaiḥ aneka puṣpa vāṭībhiḥ anekaiḥ ca sarovaraiḥ yad yad yad tad tattva jñaiḥ śiva śāstra parāyaṇaiḥ śiva āśrama rataiḥ bhaktaiḥ śiva śāstra ukta lakṣaṇaiḥ śāntaiḥ smita mukhaiḥ sphītaiḥ sat ācāra parāyaṇaiḥ śaivaiḥ māheśvaraiḥ ca eva śrīmadbhiḥ sevita dvijaiḥ sthāne śilā maye dānte dārave ca iṣṭakā maye kevalam mṛd maye vā api puṇya araṇye atha vā girau nadyām devālaye anyatra deśe vā atha gṛhe śubhe māḍhyaḥ vā atha daridraḥ vā svakām śaktim avañcayan bhaktyā vitta anusāreṇa śivam uddiśya yat kṛtam sarvatra dānam adhyayanam sarve bhāva artham na atra saṃśayaḥ cāndrāyaṇa sahasraiḥ ca prājāpatya śataiḥ tathā māsa upavāsaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ca śiva bhaktasya kim punar abhaktāḥ mānavāḥ ca asmin loke giri guhāsu ca rājasam siddhi dam kuryuḥ karmiṇaḥ rajasā āvṛtāḥ asurāḥ rākṣasāḥ ca eva tamas guṇa samanvitāḥ tādṛśāḥ tāmasam rājasam vā api sāttvikam bhāvam eva ca manas āśritya bhaktyā pūjā ādyam kurvan bhadram samaśnute yatas pāpa arṇavāt trātum bhaktiḥ nauḥ iva nirmitā śivam prapannaḥ ced kṛṣṇaiḥ pūjyaḥ sarva sura asuraiḥ teṣām abhuktānām kvacid api phalam na asti yatas tatas śru iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śivaśāstroktapūjanavarṇanam nāma paṃcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ brahma ghnaḥ vā surāpaḥ vā steyī vā gurutalpa gaḥ mātṛ hā pitṛ hā vā api vīra hā bhrūṇa hā api vā saṃpūjya amantrakam bhaktyā śivam parama kāraṇam tebhiḥ tebhiḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyeta varṣaiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ kramāt bhaktaḥ ced na aparaḥ kaścid bhikṣā āhāraḥ jita indriyaḥ tu pūjayet yadi deveśam tasmāt pāpāt pramucyate abbhakṣāḥ vāyubhakṣāḥ ca ye ca anye vrata karśitāḥ teṣām etaiḥ vrataiḥ na asti śiva loka samāgamaḥ bhaktyā pañcākṣareṇa eva yaḥ śivam sakṛt arcayet tasmāt tapāṃsi yajñān ca sarve sarva sva dakṣiṇāḥ śiva mūrti arcanasya ete koṭi aṃśena api no samāḥ baddhaḥ vā api atha muktaḥ vā paścāt pañcākṣareṇa ced pūjayan mucyate bhaktaḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā yaḥ sakṛt patitaḥ vā api mūḍhaḥ vā mucyate naraḥ ṣaḍakṣareṇa vā devam sūkta mantreṇa pūjayet alabdhāt labdhaḥ eva atra viśiṣṭaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ tasmāt nityam śivam bhaktyā sūkta mantreṇa pūjayet eka kālam dvi kālam vā tri kālam nityam eva vā ye arcayanti mahādevam vijñeyāḥ te maheśvarāḥ mad bhagavant śivaḥ sa ciram saṃsarati asmin saṃsāre duḥkha sāgare durlabham prāpya mānuṣyam mūḍhaḥ na arcayate śivam teṣām hi saphalam janma kṛtārthāḥ te nara uttamāḥ bhavanāni manojñāni vibhrama ābharaṇāḥ striyaḥ dhanam ca atṛpti paryantam śiva pūjā vidheḥ phalam ye vāñchanti mahā bhogān rājyam ca tridaśālaye te vāñchanti sadākālam harasya caraṇa ambujam saubhāgyam kāntimat rūpam sattvam tyāga ārdra bhāva tā tasmāt sarvam parityajya śiva eka āhita mānasaḥ mahā pūjā vidhim kuryāt yadi icchet śivam ātmanaḥ tvaritam jīvitam yāti tvaritam yāti yauvanam tvaritam vyādhiḥ abhyeti tasmāt pūjyaḥ pinākadhṛk yāvat na āyāti maraṇam yāvat na ākramate jarā iti vijñāya yatnena pūjanīyaḥ sadāśivaḥ dvāra yāgam javanikām parivāra bali kriyām puṣpam dhūpam ca dīpam ca dadyāt annam jalaiḥ saha tatas dadyāt mahā pīṭhe tiṣṭhan balim udañc mukhaḥ tat sarvam sa avaśeṣam vā caṇḍāya vinivedayet hutvā ca vidhivat paścāt pūjā śeṣam samāpayet bhṛtvā prayogam vidhivat yāvat mantram japam tatas nitya utsavam prakurvīta yathā uktam śiva śāsane astram pāśupatam divyam tatra āvāhya samarcayet hi śivasya āropyaḥ tat pātram dvijasya alaṃkṛtasya ca nyasta astra vapuṣā tena dīpta yaṣṭi dharasya ca nṛtya geya ādibhiḥ ca eva saha dīpadhvaja ādibhiḥ pradakṣiṇa trayam kṛtvā na drutam ca avilambitam mahā pīṭham samāvṛtya tris pradakṣiṇa yogāt punar praviṣṭaḥ dvāra sthaḥ yajamānaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ ādāya abhyantaram nītvā hi astram udvāsayet tatas pradakṣiṇa ādikam kṛtvā yathāpūrva uditam kramāt mādāya ca aṣṭa puṣpāṇi pūjām atha samāpayet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe sāṃgopāṅgapūjāvidhānavarṇanam nāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha agni kāryam vakṣyāmi kuṇḍe vā sthaṇḍile api vā vedau vā hi āyase pātre mṛd maye vā nave śubhe mādhāya agnim vidhānena saṃskṛtya ca tatas param mānam dvi hasta mānam vā hasta mātram atha api vā vṛttam vā catur asram vā kuryāt vedim ca maṇḍalam tad madhye aṣṭadala ambujam aṅgulaiḥ kathyate sadbhiḥ caturviṃśatibhiḥ karaḥ mekhalānām trayam vā api dvayam ekam atha api vā yathāśobham prakurvīta ślakṣṇam iṣṭam mṛdā sthiram mekhalā madhyatas kuryāt paścime dakṣiṇe api vā śobhanām agneḥ kiṃcid nimnām unmīlikām śanais agreṇa kuṇḍa abhimukhīm kiṃcid utsṛjya mekhalām na utsedha niyamaḥ vedyāḥ sā mārdī vā atha saikatī maṇḍalam go śakṛt toyaiḥ mānam pātrasya na uditam puṇḍam ca mṛd mayam vedim ālipet gomaya ambunā prakṣālya tāpayet pātram prokṣayet anyat ambhasā sva sūtra ukta prakāreṇa kuṇḍa ādau villikhet tatas arcana artham ca homa artham sarva dravyāṇi sādhayet prakṣālya kṣālanīyāni prokṣaṇyā prokṣya śodhayet maṇi jam kāṣṭha jam vā atha śrotriya āgāra sambhavam anyam vā abhyarhitam vahnim tatas sa ādhāram ānayet tris pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya kuṇḍa ādeḥ upari kramāt mahnibījam samuccārya tu ādadhīta agnim āsane yoni mārgeṇa vā tadvat ātmanaḥ sammukhena vā niyogaḥ pradeśa sarvam kuṇḍam kuryāt vicakṣaṇaḥ nirgamya pāvake līnam bimba ākṛti smaret hi śiva mūrtim samabhyarcya tatas dakṣiṇa pārśvatas nyasya mantram ghṛte mudrām darśayet dhenu saṃjñitām pāra ārṣa ṛcya sva sūtra ukta krameṇa śiva pūrvakaiḥ bhruṃ stuṃ bruśruṃ krameṇa eva puṃḍrandram iti atas param bījāni sapta saptānām jihvānām anupūrvaśas tri śikhā madhyamā jihvā bahu rūpa samāhvayā raktā āgneyī nairṛtī ca kṛṣṇā anyā suprabhā matā atiriktā marujjihvā sva nāma anuguṇa prabhā sva vija anantaram vācyā svāhā antaḥ ca yathākramam sarpiṣā vā samidbhiḥ vā pariṣecanam ācaret evam kṛte śiva agniḥ syāt smaret tatra śiva āsanam tatra āvāhya yajet devam ardhanārīśvaram śivam dīpa antam pariṣicya atha samidh homam samācaret tāḥ pālāśāḥ parāḥ vā api yājñiyāḥ dvādaśa aṅgulāḥ avakrāḥ na svayam śuṣkāḥ sa tvacaḥ nirvraṇāḥ samāḥ daśa aṅgulāḥ vā vihitāḥ kaniṣṭhā aṅguli saṃmitāḥ prādeśa mātrāḥ vā alābhe hotavyāḥ sakalāḥ api dūrvā pattra sama ākārām catur aṅgulam āyatām dadyāt ājya āhutim paścāt annam akṣa pramāṇāt lājān tathā sarṣapān ca yavān ca eva tilān tathā sarpiṣā aktāni bhakṣyāṇi lehya coṣyāṇi sambhave daśa eva āhutayaḥ tatra pañca vā tritayam ca vā hotavyāḥ śaktitas dadyāt ekam eva atha vā āhutim madhuveṇa ājyam samitya ādyā srucā aśeṣāt kareṇa vā tatra divyena hotavyam tīrthena ārṣeṇa vā tathā tatas homa viśiṣṭena ghṛtena āpūrya vai srucam nidhāya puṣpam tasya agre śruveṇa adhomukhena tām vauṣaṭ antena juhuyāt dhārām tu yava saṃmitām ittham pūrṇāhutim kṛtvā pariṣiṃcet ca pūrvavat tam api udvāsya vā nābhau yajet saṃdhāya nityaśas athavā vahnim ānīya śiva śāstra ukta vartmanā vāgīśā garbha saṃbhūtam saṃskṛtya vidhivat yajet anvādhānam punar kṛtvā paridhīn paridhāya ca pātrāṇi dvandva rūpeṇa nikṣipya iṣṭvā śivam tatas saṃśodhya prokṣaṇī pātram prokṣyatāni tat ambhasā praṇītā pātram aiśānyām vinyasya ā pūritam jalaiḥ mājya saṃskāra paryantam kṛtvā saṃśodhya sraj sruvau tvā pṛthak pṛthak hutvā jātam agnim vicintayet tri pādam sapta hastam ca catur śṛṅgam dvi śīrṣakam raktam rakta ambara ālepam mālya bhūṣaṇa bhūṣitam tomaram tālavṛntam ca ghṛta pātram tathā itaraiḥ hi jātam dhyātvā evam ākāram jātakarma samācaret na ālāpa nayanam kṛtvā tatas saṃśodhya sūtakam śiva agni ruci nāmā asya kṛtvā āhuti puraḥsaram tu mājya dhārā ādi homam ca kṛtvā sviṣṭakṛtam tatas brahma viṣṇu śiva īśānām lokeśānām tathā eva ca tad astrāṇām ca paritas kṛtvā pūjām yathākramam sādhayitvā ājya pūrvāṇi dravyāṇi punar eva ca kalpayitvā āsanam vahnau tatra āvāhya yathā purā saṃpūjya devam devīm ca tatas pūrṇa antam ācaret atha vā sva āśrama uktam tu vahni karma śiva arpaṇam buddhvā śiva āśramī kuryāt na ca tatra aparaḥ vidhiḥ kapilāyāḥ śakṛt śastam gṛhītam gagane patat na klinnam na ati kaṭhinam na durgandham na śoṣitam upari adhas parityajya gṛhṇīyāt patitam yadi piṇḍīkṛtya śiva agni ādau tat kṣipet mūlamantrāt ādāya vā samāloḍya bhasma ādhāre vinikṣipet taijasam dāravam vā api mṛd mayam śailam eva ca anyat vā śobhanam śuddham bhasma ādhāram prakalpayet na saṃspṛśet ca nīca aṅgaiḥ na upekṣeta na laṃghayet tasmāt bhasitam ādāya viniyuṅjīta mantrataḥ teṣu ukteṣu na anyatra na ayogyebhyaḥ pradāpayet udvāsane kṛte yasmāt caṇḍa bhasma prajāpate agni kārye kṛte paścāt śiva śāstra ukta mārgāt vidyā kośam pratiṣṭhāpya yajet puṣpa ādibhiḥ kramāt tatra āsana varam kṛtvā puṣpa ādyaiḥ gurum arcayet niveditam ca vā deve tat śeṣam ca ātma śuddhaye na tu tatra śivaḥ asmi iti buddhim kuryāt vicakṣaṇaḥ bhuktvā ācamya śivam dhyātvā hṛdaye mūlam uccaret pāla śeṣam nayet yogyaiḥ śiva śāstra kathā ādibhiḥ rātrau vyatīte pūrva aṃśe kṛtvā pūjām manoharām hi śivayoḥ śayanam tu ekam kalpayet ati śobhanam bhakṣya bhojya ambara ālepa puṣpa mālā ādikam tathā manasā karmaṇā vā api kṛtvā sarvam manoharam pratyūṣa samayam buddhvā mātrām ādyām udīrayet praṇamya manasām devam sa ambam sa gaṇam avyayam deśa kāla ucitam kṛtvā śauca ādyam api śaktitas nirvartya śivayoḥ pūjām prārabheta purā uditam iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe agnikāryavarṇanam nāma saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi śiva āśrama niṣeviṇām tābhyām ca caturdaśyām tathā parvāṇi ca kramāt ayane viṣuve ca eva grahaṇeṣu viśeṣataḥ kartavyā mahatī pūjā hi adhikā vā api śaktitas māsi māsi yathānyāyam brahmakūrcam prasādhya tu snāpayitvā śivam tena pibet śeṣam upoṣitaḥ brahmahatyā ādi doṣāṇām atīva mahatām api niṣkṛtiḥ brahmakūrcasya pānāt na anyā viśiṣyate pauṣe puṣya nakṣatre kuryāt nīrājanam vibhoḥ caitre citrā paurṇamāsyām dolām kuryāt yathāvidhi kuryāt mūla ākhya nakṣatre śītakumbham pradāpayet māsāḍhe ca uttarāṣāḍhe pavitra āropaṇam tathā prakalpayet śraviṣṭhā ākhye tu nakṣatre prauṣṭhapadyām tatas param prokṣayet ca jala krīḍām pūrvāṣāḍhā āśraye dine māśvayujyām tatas dadyāt pāyasam ca navodanam kārttikyām kṛtikā yoge dadyāt dīpa sahasrakam mārgaśīrṣe tathā ārdrāyām ghṛtena snāpayet śivam aśaktaḥ teṣu kāleṣu kuryāt utsavam eva vā mahā pūjām adhikam vā samarcanam āvṛtte api ca kalyāṇe praśasteṣu api karmasu daurmanasye durācāre duḥsvapne duṣṭa darśane snāna pūjā japa dhyāna homa dāna ādikāḥ kriyaḥ nirmita anuguṇāḥ kāryāḥ puraścaraṇa pūrvikāḥ divyam śrīkaṇṭhanāthasya sthānam ādyam sa gacchati saṃprāpya vaiṣṇavam brāhmam rudra lokam viśeṣataḥ tatra uṣitvā ciram kālam bhuktvā bhogān yathā uditān śrīkaṇṭhāt jñānam āsādya tasmāt śaiva puram vrajet paścāt jñānam samāsādya śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt saṃprāpya pauruṣam raudra sthānam adri indrajāpateḥ puṇya kṣaye kṣitim prāpya kule mahati jāyate tatra api pūrva saṃskāra vaśena sa mahā dyutiḥ bhogān ca vividhān bhuktvā vidyeśvara padam vrajet punar tatas labdhvā śiva jñānam parām bhaktim avāpya ca yaḥ ca atīva śive bhaktaḥ viṣaya āsakta citta vat eka āvṛttaḥ dvis āvṛttaḥ tris āvṛttaḥ nivartakaḥ tasmāt śiva āśritaḥ bhūtvā yena kena api hetunā saṃsāra kāraṇam yeṣām na praroḍhum alam bhavet prakṛti anuguṇam tasmāt vimṛśya etat aśeṣatas iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe nityanaimittikavidhivarṇanam nāma aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca bhagavant tvad mukhāt eva śrutam śruti samam mayā sva āśritānām śiva proktam nityanaimittikam tathā idānīm śrotum icchāmi śiva dharma adhikāriṇām aihika āmuṣmikam ca api tat ca pañcavidham punar tathā bhinnam homa dāna arcana kramāt sarva śaktimatām eva na anyeṣām saphalam bhavet haktiḥ ca ājñā mad īśasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ tasmāt kāmyāni karmāṇi kuryāt ājñādhara udvijaḥ śaivaiḥ māheśvaraiḥ ca eva kāryam antar bahis kramāt yathā tathā na bhidyante śaivāḥ māheśvarāḥ api bhiva āśritāḥ hi te śaivāḥ jñāna yajña ratāḥ narāḥ māheśvarāḥ samākhyātā karma yajña ratāḥ bhuvi tasmāt ābhyantare kuryuḥ śaivāḥ māheśvarāḥ vahis parīkṣya bhūmim vidhivat gandha varṇa rasa ādibhiḥ tu pralipte mahī pṛṣṭhe darpaṇa udara saṃnibhe prācīm utpādayet pūrvam śāstra dṛṣṭena vartmanā bhavet bhavet bhavet bhavet bhavet ālikhet vimalam padmam aṣṭa pattram sa karṇikam ratna hema ādibhiḥ cūrṇaiḥ yathā sambhava saṃbhṛtaiḥ pañca āvaraṇa saṃyuktam bahu śobhā samanvitam daleṣu siddhayaḥ kalpyāḥ kesareṣu sa śaktikāḥ rudrāḥ vāma ādayaḥ tu aṣṭa pūrva ādi dalāt kramāt karṇikāyām ca vairāgyam bījeṣu nava śaktayaḥ skande śiva ātmakaḥ dharmaḥ nāle jñānam śiva āśrayam pañca āvaraṇa saṃyuktam pūjayet ambayā saha śuddha sphaṭika saṃkāśam prasannam śītala dyutim vidyut valaya saṃkāśa jaṭā mukuṭa bhūṣitam mārdūla carma vasanam kiṃcid smita mukha ambujam sarva lakṣaṇa saṃpannam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam pañcavaktram daśa bhujam candra khaṇḍa śikhāmaṇim asya pūrva mukham saumyam bāla arka sadṛśa prabham trilocana aravinda āḍhyam kṛta bāla indu śekharam dakṣiṇam nīla jīmūta samāna rucira prabham bhrukuṭi kuṭilam ghoram rakta vṛtta īkṣaṇa trayam daṃṣṭra karālam durdharṣam sphurita adhara pallavam uttaram vidruma prakhyam nīla alaka vibhūṣitam sa vilāsam trinayanam candra ābharaṇa śekharam savye ca nāga nārāca ghaṇṭā pāśa aṅkuśa ujjvalam tad ajānu saṃbaddha māna ābhyāḥ ca pratiṣṭhayā ākaṇṭham vidyayā tadvat ālalāṭam tu śāntayā tad ūrdhvam śānti atīta ākhya kalayā parayā tathā pañcādhva vyāpinam sākṣāt kalā pañcaka vigraham mukuṭam devam puruṣa ākhyam purātanam ca tad mūrtim aṣṭatriṃśat kalā mayam mātṛkā mayam īśānam pañca brahma mayam tathā okāra ākhya mayam ca eva haṃsa śaktyā samanvitam tathā icchā ātmakayā śaktyā samārūḍha aṅka maṇḍalam jñāna ākhyayā dakṣiṇatas vāmatas ca kriyā ākhyayā tattva traya mayam sākṣāt vidyā mūrtim sadāśivam mūrti mūlena saṃkalpya sakalīkṛtya ca kramāt saṃpūjya ca yathānyāyam argha antam mūlavidyayā mūrtimantam kharasya uṣṭrasya ca ubhayayoḥ māraṇa uccāṭane kuryāt rohi bījaiḥ tila anvitaiḥ vidveṣaṇam ca tailena kuryāt lāṅgalakasya tu tuṣa saṃyuktaiḥ kārpāsa asthibhiḥ eva ca jvara upaśānti dam kṣīram saubhāgya phala dam tathā taṇḍulaiḥ ca eva caruṇā kevalena vā śāntikam pauṣṭikam vā api saptabhiḥ samidh ādibhiḥ dravyaiḥ viśeṣataḥ home vaśyam ākarṣaṇam tathā ca eva śrī padam ca viśeṣataḥ samidhaḥ śānti kāryeṣu pālāśa khadira ādikāḥ paravīra arka jāḥ kraurye kaṇṭakinyaḥ ca vigrahe praśāntaḥ śāntikam kuryāt pauṣṭikam ca viśeṣataḥ atīva duravasthāyām pratīkāra antaram na ced mātatāyinam uddiśya prakuryāt ābhicārikam sva rāṣṭra patim uddiśya na kuryāt ābhicārikam manasā karmaṇā vācā yaḥ api kaḥ api śiva āśritaḥ sva rāṣṭra patim uddiśya śivā śritam atha api vā sva rāṣṭra pālakam tasmāt śiva bhaktam ca kañcana na hiṃsyāt abhicāra ādyaiḥ yadi icchet sukham ātmanaḥ anyam kam api ca uddiśya kṛtvā vai māraṇa ādikam paścāttāpena saṃyuktaḥ prāyaścittam samācaret bāṇaliṅge api vā kuryāt nirdhanaḥ dhanavān api svayaṃbhūte atha vā liṃge ārṣake vaidike api vā kvacid aṃśe tu yaḥ śaktaḥ tu aśaktaḥ kvacid aṃśake tat sarvam gurave dadyāt dakṣiṇām ca tatas pṛthak yaḥ svayam sādhayet śaktyā guru ādi nirapekṣayā api evam ācaret atra na gṛhṇīyāt svayam punar svayam gṛhṇāti yaḥ lobhāt pūjā aṅga dravyam uttamam mūḍhaḥ na labhet mūḍhaḥ na atra kāryā vicāraṇā arcitam yat tu tad liṅgam gṛhṇīyāt vā navā svayam api śatrubhiḥ ākrāntaḥ vyādhibhiḥ vā api anekaśas mṛtyoḥ āsya gataḥ ca api mucyate nirapāyāt tat pūjāyate ati kṛpaṇaḥ riktaḥ vaiśravaṇāyate yate virūpaḥ api vṛddhaḥ api taruṇāyate yat amṛtam viṣam api amṛtāyate mahīdharāyate śvabhram sa ca śvabhrāyate giriḥ padmākarāyate vahniḥ saraḥ vaiśvānarāyate siṃhāyate mṛgaḥ kṣudraḥ siṃhaḥ krīḍāmṛgāyate striyaḥ abhisārikāyante lakṣmīḥ sucaritāyate svairapreṣyāyate vāṇī kīrtiḥ tu gaṇikāyate svairācārāyate medhā vajrasūcīyate manaḥ mahāvātāyate śaktiḥ balam mattagajāyate te śatru pakṣāyate arīṇām sarvaḥ eva suhṛd janaḥ śatravaḥ kuṇapāyante jīvantaḥ api sa bāndhavāḥ pannaḥ gata ariṣṭaḥ svayam khalu amṛtāyate aniśam kriyamāṇā api ratiḥ tu abhinavāyate anāgata ādikam sarvam karasthāmalakāyate iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe aihikasiddhikarmavarṇanam nāma dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atas param pravakṣyāmi kevala āmuṣmikam vidhim puṇya atiśaya saṃyuktaḥ sarvaiḥ devaiḥ anuṣṭhitaḥ brahmanā viṣṇunā ca eva rudreṇa ca viśeṣataḥ śveta agastya dadhīca ādyaiḥ asmābhiḥ ca śiva āśritaiḥ nandīśvara mahākāla bhṛṅgīśa ādyaiḥ gaṇeśvaraiḥ pātāla vāsibhiḥ daityaiḥ śeṣa ādyaiḥ ca mahā uragaiḥ svam svam padam anuprāptam sarvaiḥ ayam anuṣṭhitaḥ brahmā brahmatvam āpannaḥ viṣṇuḥ viṣṇu tvam āgataḥ gaṇeśaḥ ca gaṇeśa tvam anena vidhinā gataḥ sitacandana toyena liṅgam snāpya śivam śivām tatra padmāsanam ramyam kṛtvā lakṣaṇa saṃyutam aṅguṣṭha pratimam ramyam sarva gandha mayam śubham tu uttare candanam dadyāt haritālam tu pūrvatas dhūpam kṛṣṇa agurum dadyāt sarvatas ca sa guggulam vāsāṃsi ca ati sūkṣmāṇi vikāśāni nivedayet pāyasam ghṛta sammiśram ghṛta dīpān ca dāpayet praṇamya bhaktyā deveśam stutvā ca ante kṣamāpayet sarva upahāra sammiśram tatas liṅgam nivedayet śivāya śiva mantreṇa dakṣiṇāmūrtim āśritaḥ deyam ca śiva bhaktebhyaḥ śivena kathitam purā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe āmuṣmikakarmavidhivarṇanam nāma trayastriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sā sarvā labhyeta sadyas liṅgabera pratiṣṭhayā tasmāt pratiṣṭhite liṅge bhavet sarvam pratiṣṭhitam brahmaṇā viṣṇunā vā api rudreṇa anyena kena vā kim anyat iha vaktavyam pratiṣṭhām prati kāraṇam partiṣṭhitam śivena api liṅgam vaiśveśvaram yatas sthāpayet parameśasya liṅgam beram atha api vā śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca kim idam liṅgam ākhyātam katham liṅgī maheśvaraḥ avyaktam liṅgam ākhyātam triguṇa prabhava apyayam anādi anantam viśvasya yat upādānakāraṇam tat eva mūlaprakṛtiḥ māyā ca gagana ātmakā ca eva śuddham yat śuddha aśuddham ca tat tridhā tatas śivaḥ maheśaḥ ca rudraḥ viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ bhūtāni ca indriyaiḥ jātāḥ līyante atra śiva ājñayā atas eva śivaḥ liṅgaḥ liṅgam ājñāpayet yatas yatas na tat anājñātam kāryāya prabhavet svatas liṅgam ca śivayoḥ dehaḥ tābhyām yasmāt adhiṣṭhitam liṅga vediḥ mahādevī liṅgam sākṣāt maheśvaraḥ tat eva paramā śaktiḥ śivasya paramātmanaḥ yat ādatte prasūte tat carācaram yena ādau mohitau syātām brahma nārāyaṇau api suṣvāpa an ākulaḥ sukham dadarśa puṇḍarīkākṣam svapantam tam an ākulam māyayā mohitaḥ śambhoḥ viṣṇum āha pitāmahaḥ sa tu hasta prahāreṇa tīvreṇa abhihataḥ kṣaṇāt iti viṣṇu vacaḥ śrutvā prabhu tva guṇa sūcakam iti kutas brūṣe mām na jānāsi kim nātham prapañcaḥ yasya mama kṛtiḥ tridhā ātmānam vibhajya idam sṛṣṭvā atha paripālyate saṃharāmi name kaścid sraṣṭā jaganti vidyate iti ukte sati saḥ api āha brahmānam viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ bhavān api mama eva aṅgāt avatīrṇaḥ purā avyayāt mad niyogāt tvam ātmānam tridhā kṛtvā jagattrayam vismṛtaḥ asi jagannātham nārāyaṇam anāmayam tava api janakam sākṣāt mām evam avamanyase te aparādhaḥ na asti atra bhrāntaḥ asi mama māyayā mad prasādāt iyam bhrāntiḥ apaiṣyati te acirāt jvālā mālā sahasra āḍhyam aprameyam anaupamam tasya jvālā sahasreṇa brahma viṣṇū vimohitau visṛjya yuddham kim tu etat iti aciṃtayatām tadā tadā samudyatau syātām tasya ādi antam parīkṣitum tatra haṃsa ākṛtiḥ brahmā viśvatas pakṣa saṃyutaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ api viśvātmā līlāñjana caya upamam vārāham amitam rūpam asthāya gatavan adhas evam varṣa sahasram tu tvaran viṣṇuḥ adhas gataḥ na apaśyat alpam api asya mūlam liṅgasya sūkaraḥ tāvatkālam gataḥ ca ūrdhvam tasya antam jñātum icchayā mad adhas pitāmahaḥ tathā eva bhagavant viṣṇuḥ śrāntaḥ saṃvigna locanaḥ samāgatau atha anyonyam vismaya smera vīkṣaṇau māyayā mohitau śambhoḥ kṛtya akṛtyam na jagmatuḥ pṛṣṭhatas pārśvatas tasya ca agratas ca sthitau ubhau praṇipatya kim ātmā idam iti aciṃtayatām tadā iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe harividhimohavarṇanam nāma catustriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha āvirabhavat tatra sa nādam śabda lakṣaṇam tat api aviditam tāvat brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā a u mā iti tri mātrābhiḥ parastāt ca ardha mātrayā tatra ākāraḥ śritaḥ bhāge jvalat liṅgasya dakṣiṇe ardha mātrā ātmakaḥ nādaḥ śrūyate liṅga mūrdhani veda ātmanā tadā avyaktaḥ praṇavaḥ vikṛtim gataḥ makāraḥ sāma saṃjātaḥ nādaḥ tu ātharvaṇā śrutiḥ ṛgayam sthāpayāmāsa samāsāt tu artham ātmanaḥ rajas guṇeṣu brahmānam mūrtiṣu ādyam kriyāsu api sṛṣṭim lokeṣu pṛthivīm tattveṣu ātmānam avyayam liṅga bhāgeṣu adhobhāgam bīja ākhyam kāraṇa traye catuḥṣaṣṭi guṇa aiśvaryam bauddham yat aṇima ādiṣu atha upasthāpayāmāsa sva artham daśavidham yajuḥ sattvam guṇeṣu viṣṇum ca mūrtiṣu ādyam kriyāsu api sthitim lokeṣu antarikṣam vidyām tattveṣu ca triṣu pratiṣṭhām ca vāmam brahmasu pañcasu madhyam tu liṅga bhāgeṣu yonim ca triṣu hetuṣu prākṛtam ca yathā aiśvaryam tasmāt viśvam yajus mayam tatas upasthāpayāmāsa sāma artham daśadhā ātmanaḥ tamas guṇeṣu atho rudram mūrtiṣu ādyam kriyāsu ca saṃhṛtim triṣu lokeṣu tattveṣu śivam uttamam liṅga bhāgeṣu pīṭha ūrdhvam bījinam kāraṇa traye pauruṣam ca tathā aiśvaryam ittham sāmnā tatam jagat tatas maheśvaram sākṣāt mūrtiṣu api sadāśivam bhū kriyāsu niṣkriyasya api śivasya paramātmanaḥ śāntim ca śāntyatītām ca vyāpakām kalāsu api tatpūruṣam tathā īśānam brahma brahmasu pañcasu yatra āvāhya samārādhyaḥ kevalaḥ niṣkalaḥ śivaḥ traya atītāt māyā vikṣobha kāraṇāt tasmāt śuddhavidyāyāḥ parastāt ca maheśvarāt sarva vidyā īśvara adhīśāt na parasmāt ca sadāśivāt pañcavaktrāt daśa bhujāt sākṣāt sakala niṣkalāt tatas parāt niśādhīśān nāda ākhyāt ca tatas parāt tatas parāt suṣumnā īśāt brahmarandhra īśvarāt api paramam kāraṇam sākṣāt svayam niṣkāraṇam śivam ca dhātāram dhyātārām dhyeyam avyayam sarva aiśvaryeṇa saṃpannam sarva īśvaram anīśvaram aiśvaryāt ca api māyā iyāt aśuddhāt mānuṣa ādikāt aparāt ca parāt tyājyāt adhiśuddha adhva gocarāt tad parāt śuddhavidyā ādyāt unmanā antāt parātparāt apāram apara adhīnam nirasta atiśayam sthiram yasmāt garīyāḥ tasmāt viśvam vyāptam atharvaṇāt ṛgvedaḥ punar āha idam jāgrat rūpam mayā ucyate bhogya ātmanā pariṇatāḥ vidyā vedyāḥ yatas mayi sāma ca āha suṣupti ākhyam evam sarvam mayā ucyate mama arthena śivena idam tāmasena abhidhīyate turāya ākhyam turīyātītam eva ca tu tritayam śiva vidyā ātma saṃjñitam tat traiguṇyam trayī sādhyam saṃśodhyam ca pada eṣiṇā adhva atītam turīya ākhyam nirvāṇam paramam padam dvayoḥ pramāpakaḥ nādaḥ nadāntaḥ ca mada ātmakaḥ tasmāt mama artha svātantryāt pradhānaḥ parameśvaraḥ śivaḥ hi praṇavaḥ hi eṣa praṇavaḥ hi śivaḥ smṛtaḥ eka akṣarāt akāra ākhyāt ātmā brahma abhidhīyate eka akṣarāt ukāra ākhyāt dvidhā viṣṇuḥ udīryate eka akṣarāt makāra ākhyāt śivaḥ rudraḥ udāhṛtaḥ dakṣiṇa aṅgāt maheśasya jātaḥ brahmā ātma saṃjñikaḥ hṛdayāt nīlarudraḥ bhūt śivasya śiva saṃjñikaḥ sṛṣṭyāḥ pravartakaḥ brahmā sthityāḥ viṣṇuḥ vimohakaḥ traya hetuḥ ca śivaḥ parama kāraṇam bhṛcaḥ yajūṃṣi sāmāni śākhāḥ ca anyāḥ sahasraśas svapna anubhūtam iva tat tābhyām na adhyavasīyate liṅge api mudritam sarvam yathā vedaiḥ udāhṛtam tat dṛṣṭvā mudritam liṅge prasādāt liṅginaḥ tadā utpattim vilayam ca eva yathātmyam ca ṣaḍadhvanām tatas parataram dhāma dhāmavantam ca pūruṣam niruttarataram brahma niṣkalam śivam īśvaram paśu pāśa mayasya asya prapañcasya sadā patim nirasta atiśayam śaśvat viśva loka vilakṣaṇam prakāśa eka rasam śāntam prasannam satata uditam sarva kalyāṇa nilayam śaktyā tādṛśayā anvitam jñātvā devam virūpākṣam brahma nārāyaṇau tadā racayitvā añjalim mūrdhani bhītau tau vācam ūcatuḥ ajñaḥ vā aham abhijñaḥ vā tvayā ādau deva nirmitaḥ hi īdṛśām bhrāntim āpannaḥ iti kaḥ atra aparādhyati mama idam ajñānam tvayi sannihate prabho uvāca stotum deva na vāc asti mahimnaḥ sadṛśā tava prabhoḥ agre vidheyānām tūṣṇīṃbhāvaḥ vyatikramaḥ tvayā dattam vismṛtam te māyayā mohitaḥ ahaṃkṛtaḥ ca api punar eva asmi śāsitaḥ vijñāpitaiḥ kim bahuṣu bhītaḥ asmi bhṛśam īśvara tvām uśanti mahādevam bhītānām ārti nāśanam iti vijñāpitaḥ tābhyām īśvarābhyām maheśvaraḥ paraḥ īśvaraḥ uvāca tatas chinnā prajā sṛṣṭiḥ jagat kāraṇa bhūtayoḥ evam nivārita avadya liṅga āvirbhāva līlayā tasmāt bhūyas vivādam ca vrīḍām ca utsṛjya kṛtsnaśas purā mama ājñayā sārdham samasta jñāna saṃhitāḥ yuvābhyām hi mayā dattā kāraṇa tva prasiddhaye mantra ratnam ca sūtra ākhyam pañcākṣara mayam param dadāmi ca punar sarvam yathāpūrvam mama ājñayā yatas vinā yuvam tena na kṣamau sṛṣṭi rakṣaṇe evam uktvā mahādevaḥ nārāyaṇa pitāmahau mantrarājam dadau tābhyām jñānasaṃhitayā saha tau labdhvā mahatīm divyām ājñām māheśvarām parām mahārtham mantra ratnam ca tathā eva sakalāḥ kalāḥ daṇḍa vat praṇatim kṛtvā devadevasya pādayoḥ tiṣṭhatām vīta bhayau ānanda astimitau tadā liṅgam kvāpi tirobhūtam na tābhyām upalabhyate tatas prabhṛti śakra ādyāḥ sarve eva sura asurāḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca narāḥ nāgāḥ nāryaḥ ca api vidhānāt liṅga pratiṣṭhā kurvanti liṅge rasa aktayā lakṣitam lakṣaṇam śilpa śāstreṇa vilikhet tatas aṣṭa mṛd salilaiḥ vā atha pañca mṛd salilaiḥ tathā piṇḍikā sārdham pañcagavya ca śodhay nītvā adhivāsayet tatra liṅgam piṇḍikayā saha sa samānīya sarva maṅgala niḥsvanaiḥ saha piṇḍikayā āveṣṭya śāyayet ca yathā purā vidyeśa kalaśān nyasyet madhye śaivīm ca vardhanīm te ca aṣṭa mūrtayaḥ kalpyāḥ pūrva ādi paritas sthitāḥ catvāraḥ ca atha hutvā ghṛtena aṣṭa uttaram śatam hutvā a hutvā spṛśet liṅgam vedikām ca punar punar pūrṇāhutim tatas hutvā kramāt dadyāt ca dakṣiṇām ācāryāt pādam ardham vā hotR̥ṇām sthapateḥ api tatas śvabhre vṛṣam dīptam liṅgam anusmaret māvāhayet śivau sākṣāt prāñjaliḥ prāñc udañc mukhaḥ vṛṣa adhirājam āruhya vimānam vā nabhastalāt alaṃkṛtam saha āyāntam devyā devam anusmaran sarva ābharaṇa śobhā āḍhyam sarva maṅgala nisvanaiḥ brahma viṣṇu maheśa arka śakra ādyaiḥ deva dānavaiḥ tatas pañca upacārān ca kṛtvā pūjām samāpayet na atas parataraḥ kaścid vidhiḥ pañca upacārakāt pratiṣṭhām liṅga vat kuryāt pratimāsu api sarvatas jala adhivāse śayane śāyayet tāntu adhomukhām kumbha uda śāyitām mantraiḥ hṛdi tām san niyojayet tad ālayām parām āhuḥ pratiṣṭhām akṛta ālayāt mataḥ kṛta ālayaḥ paścāt pratiṣṭhā vidhim ācaret aśaktaḥ ced pratiṣṭhāpya liṅgam beram atha api vā ālayam ca punar vakṣye bhavat kṛtvā liṅgam vā lakṣaṇa anvitam devīm kṛtvā śubhe deśe tatra abjam pūrvavat likhet pañca brahmāni tad bījaiḥ teṣu pañcasu pañcabhiḥ viśodhya liṅgam beram vā mṛd toya ādyaiḥ yathā purā nidhāya puṣpam śirasi prokṣayet prokṣaṇī jalaiḥ taiḥ kumbhaiḥ īśāna vidyā antaiḥ snāpayet mūlavidyayā tatas pañcakalā nyāsam kṛtvā pūjām ca pūrvavat nyasya padma antare sarvam śeṣam pūrvavat ācaret liṅgāni bāṇa saṃjñāni sthāpanīyāni vā na vā tāni pūrvam śivena eva saṃskṛtāni yatas tatas śeṣāṇi sthāpanīyāni yāni dṛṣṭāni bāṇa vat a pīṭhe pīṭham āveśya kṛtvā saṃprokṣaṇam vidhim yajet tatra śivam teṣām pratiṣṭhā na vidhīyate dagdham ślatham kṣata aṅgam ca kṣipet liṅgam jalāśaye saṃdhāna yogyam saṃdhāya pratiṣṭhā vidhim ācaret berāt vā vikalāt liṅgāt deva pūjā puraḥsaram udvāsya hṛdi saṃdhānam tyāgam vā yuktam ācaret dvi rātre ca mahā pūjām saṃprokṣaṇam atas param māsāt ūrdhvam aneka aham pūjā yadi vihanyate pratiṣṭhā procyate kaiścid kaiścid saṃprokṣaṇa kramaḥ saṃprokṣaṇe tu liṅga ādeḥ devam udvāsya pūrvavat aṣṭa pañca krameṇa eva snāpayitvā mṛd ambhasā prokṣayet prokṣaṇī toyaiḥ mūlena aṣṭa uttaram śatam sa puṣpam sa kuśam pāṇim nyasya liṅgasya mastake pañca vāram japet mūlam aṣṭottaraśatam tatas tatas mūlena mūrdha ādi pīṭha antam saṃspṛśet api pūjām ca mahatīm kuryāt devam āvāhya pūrvavat iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe ptatiṣṭhāvidhivarṇanam nāma ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca jñāne kriyāyām caryāyām sāram uddhṛtya saṃgrahāt mayā vac bhagavatā sarvam śrutam śruti samam mayā idānīm śrotum icchāmi yogam parama durlabham sa adhikāram ca sa aṅgam ca sa vidhim sa prayojanam yadi asti maraṇam pūrvam yoga ādi anupamardāt sadyas sādhayitum śakyam yena syāt na ātma hā naraḥ tat ca tat kāraṇam ca eva tad kāla karaṇāni ca sthāne pṛṣṭam tvayā kṛṣṇa sarva praśna artha vedinā tatas krameṇa tat sarvam vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ yā vṛttiḥ sa samāsena yogaḥ saḥ khalu pañcadhā avyākṣepā manaḥ vṛttiḥ mantra yogaḥ udāhṛtaḥ prāṇāyāma mukhā sā eva sparśe yogaḥ abhidhīyate vilīna avayavam viśvam rūpam saṃbhāvyate yatas abhāva yogaḥ saṃproktaḥ anābhāsāt vastunaḥ sataḥ śiva svabhāvaḥ eva ekaḥ cintyate nirupādhikaḥ dṛṣṭe tathā ānuśravike viraktam viṣaye manaḥ viṣaya dvaya doṣāṇām guṇānām īśvarasya ca darśanāt eva satatam viraktam jāyate manaḥ aṣṭa aṅgaḥ vā ṣaṣ aṅgaḥ vā sarva yogaḥ samāsatas prāṇāyāmaḥ pratyāhāraḥ dhāraṇā dhyānam eva ca samādhiḥ iti yogāṅgāni aṣṭa uktāni sūribhiḥ māsanam prāṇa saṃrodhaḥ dhāraṇā dhyānam samādhiḥ yogasya ṣaṣ aṅgāni samāsatas pṛthak lakṣaṇam eteṣām śivaśāstre samīritam mahā āgameṣu ca anyeṣu viśeṣāt kāmika ādiṣu yoga śāstreṣu api tathā purāṇeṣu api keṣu ca śaucam tuṣṭiḥ tapaḥ ca eva japaḥ praṇidhiḥ eva ca iti pañca prabhedaḥ syāt niyamaḥ sva aṃśa bhedāt paryaṅkam ca yatheṣṭam ca proktam āsanam aṣṭadhā prāṇaḥ sva deha jaḥ vāyuḥ tasya āyāmaḥ nirodhanam nāsikā puṭam aṅgulyā pīḍya ekam apareṇa tu audaram recayet vāyum tathā ayam recakaḥ smṛtaḥ nāsā puṭena apareṇa pūraṇāt pūrakam matam na muṃcati na gṛhṇāti vāyum antar bahis sthitam saṃpūrṇam kumbha vat tiṣṭhet acalaḥ saḥ tu kumbhakaiḥ recaka ādiṣu yaḥ bhyāsaḥ nāḍī śodhana pūrvakaḥ yakā ādi krama vaśāt prāṇāyāma nirodhanam tat caturddhā upadiṣṭam syāt mātrā guṇa vibhāgāt uttamaḥ tu tris uddhātaḥ ṣaḍviṃśat mātrakaḥ paraḥ sveda kampa ādi janakaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ tad uttaraḥ ānanda udbhava romāñca netra aśrūṇām vimocanam jānum pradakṣiṇīkṛtya na drutam na vilaṃbitam aṅguli sphoṭanam kuryāt sā mātrā iti prakīrtitā mātrā krameṇa vijñeyāḥ ca udvāta krama yogāt nāḍī viśuddhi pūrvam tu prāṇāyāmam samācaret agarbhaḥ ca sagarbhaḥ ca prāṇāyāmaḥ dvidhā smṛtaḥ agarbhāt garbha saṃyuktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ śata adhikaḥ prāṇasya vijayāt eva jīyante deha vāyavaḥ prāṇaḥ samānaḥ ca hi udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca nāgaḥ kūrmaḥ ca kṛkalaḥ devadattaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ prayāṇam kurute yasmāt tasmāt prāṇaḥ abhidhīyate yat āhāra ādi bhujyate vyānaḥ vyānaśayati aṅgāni aśeṣāṇi vivardhayan udvejayati marmāṇi iti udānaḥ vāyuḥ īritaḥ samam nayati sarva aṅgam samānaḥ tena gīyate udgāre nāgaḥ ākhyātaḥ kūrmaḥ unmīlane sthitaḥ kṛkalaḥ kṣavathau jñeyaḥ devadattaḥ vijṛmbhaṇe na jahāti mṛtam ca api sarvavyāpī dhanaṃjayaḥ tad eva abhyasyamānā iyam prāṇāyāma pramāṇavān viṣ mūtra śleṣmaṇām tāvat alpa bhāvaḥ prajāyate laghu tvam śīghra gāmi tvam utsāhaḥ svara sauṣṭhavam sarva roga kṣayaḥ ca eva balam tejaḥ surūpa tā tapāṃsi pāpa kṣaya tā yajña dāna vrata ādayaḥ prāṇāyāmasya tasya ete kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśām indriyāṇi prasaktāni yathāsvam viṣayeṣu iha ucyate namas pūrvāṇi indriyāṇi svargam narakam eva ca nigṛhīta nisṛṣṭāni svargāya narakāya ca tasmāt sukha arthī matimān jñāna vairāgyam āsthitaḥ indriya aśvān nigṛhya āśu sva ātmanā ātmānam uddharet tat tat tat tat tatra sthānam ca śivaḥ eva ekaḥ na anyat doṣa trayam yatas kālam kaṃca avadhīkṛtya sthāne avasthāpitam manaḥ na tu pracyavate lakṣyāt dhāraṇā syāt na ca anyathā manasaḥ prathamam sthairyam dhāraṇāyāḥ prajāyate tasmāt dhīram manaḥ kuryāt dhāraṇa abhyāsa yogāt cintāyām smṛtaḥ dhātuḥ śiva cintā muhur muhur avyākṣiptena manasā dhyānam nāma tat ucyate paraḥ dhyeyaḥ samāpta ātharvaṇā śrutiḥ tathā śivā parā dhyeyā sarva bhūta gatau śivau dhyātā dhyānam tathā dhyeyam yat ca dhyāna prayojanam bhātvā yogam yuñjīta yoga vid nirmamaḥ ca sadā utsāhī dhyātā ittham puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ punar dhyāyet dhyānāt śrāntaḥ punar japet dhāraṇā dvādaśa āyāmā dhyānam dvādaśa dhāraṇam hyāna dvādaśakam yāvat samādhiḥ abhidhīyate samādhiḥ nāma yoga aṅgam antimam parikīrtitam svarūpa śūnya vat bhānam samādhiḥ abhidhīyate nirvāṇa anala vat yogī samādhi sthaḥ pragīyate na śṛṇoti na ca āghrāti na jalpati na paśyati na ca sparśam vijānāti na saṃkalpayate manaḥ evam śive vilīna ātmā samādhi sthaḥ iha ucyate tathā tasmāt na vicalet sudhīḥ tad antarāyāḥ naśyanti vighnāḥ sarve śanais śanais iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīya saṃhitāyām vāyu naimiṣeya ṛṣi saṃvāde uttara khaṇḍe yogagativarṇanam nāma saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ālasyam vyādhayaḥ tīvrāḥ pramādaḥ sthāna saṃśayaḥ duḥkhāni daurmanasyam ca viṣayeṣu ca lola tā daśā ete yuñjatām puṃsām antarāyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ dhātu vaiṣamya jāḥ doṣāḥ vyādhayaḥ karma doṣa jāḥ pramādaḥ nāma yogasya sādhanā nāma bhāvanā idam vijñānam sthāna saṃśayaḥ duḥkham ajñāna jam puṃsām cittasya ādhyātmikam viduḥ kṛtaiḥ ādhidaivikam ākhyātam aśani astra viṣa ādikam icchā vighāta jam mokṣam daurmanasyam pracakṣate śānteṣu eteṣu vighneṣu yoga āsaktasya yoginaḥ pratibhā śravaṇam vārttā darśana āsvāda vedanāḥ sūkṣme vyavahite atīte viprakṛṣṭe tu anāgate śravaṇam sarva śabdānām śravaṇe ca aprayatnāt mārttāḥ vārttāsu vijñānam sarveṣām eva dehinām darśanam nāma divyānām darśanam ca aprayatnāt tathā āsvādaḥ ca divyeṣu raseṣu āsvādaḥ ucyate sparśana adhigamaḥ tadvat vedanā nāma viśrutā gandha ādīnām ca divyānām ābrahma bhuvana adhipāḥ rasāyanāni sarvāṇi divyāḥ ca oṣadhayaḥ tathā yat kṛśa tā sthūla tā bālyam vārddhakyam ca eva yauvanam nānā cāti svarūpam ca caturṇām dehadhāraṇam pārthiva aṃśam vinā nityam surabhiḥ gandha saṃgrahaḥ evam aṣṭaguṇam prāhuḥ paiśācam pārthivam padam rasa ādikam bhavet ca anyat trayāṇām dehadhāraṇam tat idam ṣoḍaśaguṇam āpyam aiśvaryam adbhutam śarīrāt agni nirmāṇam tad tāpa bhaya varjanam sthāpanam vā analasya apsu pāṇau pāvaka dhāraṇam dvābhyām deha vinirmāṇam āpya aiśvarya samanvitam manojava tvam bhūtānām kṣaṇāt antar praveśanam parvata ādi mahā bhāra dhāraṇam ca aprayatnāt ca dvātriṃśat guṇam aiśvaryam mārutam kavayaḥ viduḥ chāyā hīna viniṣpattiḥ indriyāṇām adarśanam mahā ākāśa laṅghanam ca eva sva dehe tad niveśanam ākāśapiṇḍīkaraṇam aśarīra tvam eva ca anila aiśvarya saṃyuktam catvāriṃśadguṇam mahat yathākāma upalabdhiḥ ca yathākāma vinirgamaḥ bhava anurūpa nirmāṇam vaśitvam priya darśanam chedanam tāḍanam ca eva bandhanam mocanam tathā sarva prasādaḥ ca api sarveṣām mṛtyu kāla jayaḥ tathā mānikam aiśvaryam prājāpatyam pracakṣate etat cāndramasaiḥ bhogaiḥ ṣaṭpañcāśadguṇam mahat sargaḥ saṃkalpa mātreṇa trāṇam saṃharaṇam tathā sva adhikāraḥ ca sarveṣām bhūta citta pravartanam asādṛśyam ca sarvasya nirmāṇam jagantaḥ pṛthak śubha aśubhasya karaṇam prājāpatyaiḥ ca saṃyutam brāhmam aiśvaryam ca pracakṣate bauddhāt asmāt param gauṇam aiśvaryam prākṛtam viduḥ vaiṣṇavam tat samākhyātam tasya eva bhuvana sthitiḥ tat pauruṣam ca gauṇam ca gaṇeśam padam aiśvaram viṣṇunā tat padam kiṃcid jñātum anyaiḥ na śakyate vijñāna siddhayaḥ ca eva sarvāḥ eva aupasargikāḥ pratibhāseṣu aśuddheṣu guṇeṣu āsakta cetasaḥ tasmāt guṇān ca bhogān ca deva asura mahībhṛtām yathākāmam guṇān bhogān bhuktvā muktim prayāsyati atha prayogam yogasya vakṣye śṛṇu samāhitaḥ śubhe kāle śubhe deśe śiva kṣetra ādike punar mukta puṣpa samākīrṇe vitāna ādi vicitrite na agni abhyāśe jala abhyāśe śuṣka parṇa caye api vā na daṃśa maśaka ākīrṇe sarpa śvāpada saṃkule na ca duṣṭa mṛga ākīrṇe na bhaye durjana āvṛte maśāne caitya valmīke jīrṇāgāre catuṣpathe nadīnada samudrāṇām tīre rathyā antare api vā na jīrṇa udyāna goṣṭha ādau na aniṣṭe na ca nindite na ajīrṇa amla rasa udgāre na ca viṣ mūtra dūṣite na chardi āma atisāre vā na atibhuktau śrama anvite na ca ati citta ākulitaḥ na ca ati kṣudh pipāsitaḥ yukta āhāra vihāraḥ ca yukta ceṣṭaḥ ca karmasu mṛdulam ramyam vipulam su samam śuci na ātiṣṭhet śiṣṭa locanaḥ paśyat kiṃcid unnāmita śirāḥ dantaiḥ dantān na saṃspṛśet danta agra saṃsthitā jihvām acalām sanniveśya ca pārṣṇibhyām vṛṣaṇau rakṣan tathā prajananam punar ūruvoḥ upari saṃsthāpya bāhū tiryañcam ayatnāt dakṣiṇam kara pṛṣṭham tu nyasya vāma tala upari unnāmya śanakais pṛṣṭham uraḥ viṣṭabhya ca agratas saṃprekṣya nāsikā agram svam diśaḥ ca anavalokayān saṃbhṛta prāṇa saṃcāraḥ pāṣāṇaḥ iva niścalaḥ sva deha āyatanasya antar viciṃtya śivam ambayā hṛd padma pīṭhikā madhye dhyāna yajñena pūjayet mūle nāsā agratas nābhau kaṇṭhe vā tālu randhrayoḥ bhrū madhye dvāra deśe vā lalāṭe mūrdhani vā smaret parikalpya yathānyāyam śivayoḥ parama āsanam tatra sa āvaraṇam vā api nirāvaraṇam eva vā vā dvādaśa are yathāvidhi daśa are vā ṣaṣ asre vā catur asre śivam smaret ṣoḍaśa ārasya pattrāṇi svarāḥ ṣoḍaśa tāni vai pūrva ādīni kramāt etat padmam kandasya mūlāt kakāra ādi ṭakāra antāḥ varṇāḥ parṇāni anukramāt go kṣīra dhavalasya uktāḥ ḍa ādi pha antāḥ yathākramam yad vidhūma aṅgāra varṇasya varṇāḥ vādyāḥ ca la antimāḥ mūlādhāra aravindasya hema ābhasya yathākramam vakāra ādi sakāra antāḥ varṇāḥ parṇa mayāḥ sthitāḥ eteṣu atha aravindeṣu yatra eva abhiratam manaḥ tatra eva devam devīm ca ciṃtayet dhīrayā dhyā aṅguṣṭha mātram amalam dīpyamānam samantataḥ śuddha dīpa śikhā ākāram sva śaktyā pūrṇa maṇḍitam indu rekhā sama ākāram tārā rūpam atha api vā nīvāra śūkaḥ sadṛśam bisa sutrābham eva vā kadamba golaka ākāram tuṣāra kaṇikā upamam tad kṣiti ādi tattva vijayam dhyātā yadi api vāñchati tad tad tattva adhipām eva mūrtim sthūlām viciṃtayet sadāśiva antāḥ brahma ādya bhava ādyāḥ ca aṣṭa mūrtayaḥ śivasya mūrtayaḥ sthūlāḥ śivaśāstre viniścitāḥ ghorā miśrā praśāntāḥ ca mūrtayaḥ tāḥ muni īśvaraiḥ phala abhilāṣa rahitaiḥ cintyāḥ cintā viśāradaiḥ ghorāḥ ced ciṃtitāḥ kuryuḥ pāpa roga parikṣayam saumye muktiḥ viśeṣeṇa śāntiḥ prajñā prasidhyati sidhyanti siddhayaḥ ca atra kramaśas na atra saṃśayaḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe yogagatau vighnotpattivarṇanam nāma aṣṭatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ śrīkaṇṭha nātham smaratām sadyas sarva artha siddhayaḥ hi śive tu ciṃtite sākṣāt sarvāḥ sidhyanti siddhayaḥ mūrti antareṣu dhyāteṣu śiva rūpam viciṃtayet dhyānam ādau sa viṣayam tatas nirviṣayam jaguḥ tatra nirviṣayam dhyānam na asti iti eva satām matam tasmāt sa viṣayam dhyānam bāla arka kiraṇa āśrayam sūkṣma āśrayam nirviṣayam na aparam paramārthāt yat vā sa viṣayam dhyānam tat sa ākāra samāśrayam nirākāra ātma saṃvittiḥ dhyānam nirviṣayam matam nirākāra śraya tvena sa ākāra āśrayāt tathā tasmāt sa viṣayam dhyānam ādau kṛtvā sa bījakam prāṇāyāmena sidhyanti devyāḥ śānti ādayaḥ kramāt śāntiḥ praśāntiḥ dīptiḥ ca prasādaḥ ca tatas param maḥ sarva āpadām ca eva śāntiḥ iti abhidhīyate tamasaḥ anta bahis nāśaḥ praśāntiḥ parigīyate svastha tā yā tu sā buddhaḥ prasādaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ca sarvāṇi sa bāhya abhyantarāṇi ca dhyātā dhyānam tathā dhyeyam yat vā dhyāna prayojanam etat catuṣṭayam jñātvā dhyātā dhyānam samācaret śraddadhānaḥ prasanna ātmā dhyātā sadbhiḥ udāhṛtaḥ cintāyām smṛtaḥ dhātuḥ śiva cintā muhur muhur yoga abhyāsaḥ tathā alpe api yathā pāpam vināśayet dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇa mātram vā śraddhayā parameśvaram mahā dhyānasya pūrṇasya sākṣāt uktam prayojanam yasmāt saukhyam ca mokṣam ca dhyānāt abhayam āpnuyāt na asti dhyānam vinā jñānam na asti dhyānam ayoginaḥ dhyānam jñānam ca yasya asti tīrṇaḥ tena bhava arṇavaḥ prasannam ekāgram aśeṣa upādhi varjitam prakṣīṇa aśeṣa pāpānām jñāne dhyāne bhavet matiḥ pāpa upahata buddhīnām tad vārttā api su durlabhā yathā vahniḥ mahā dīptaḥ śuṣkam ārdram ca nirdahet tathā śubha aśubham karma dhyāna agniḥ dahate kṣaṇāt ati alpaḥ yathā dīpaḥ su mahat nāśayet tamaḥ mahā pāpam vināśayet dhyāyataḥ kṣaṇa mātram vā śraddhayā parameśvaram na asti dhyāna samam tīrtham na asti dhyāna samam tapaḥ na asti dhyāna samaḥ yajñaḥ tasmāt dhyānam samācaret tīrthāni toya pūrṇāni devān pāṣāṇa mṛd mayān yoginām ca vapuḥ sūkṣmam bhavet pratyakṣam aiśvaram yathā sthūlam ayuktānām mṛd kāṣṭha ādyaiḥ prakalpitam yathā iha antar carāḥ rājñaḥ priyāḥ syuḥ na bahis carāḥ tathā antar dhyāna niratāḥ priyāḥ śambhoḥ na karmiṇaḥ tadvat atra api karmiṇaḥ mahā jijñāsuḥ api yogasya yām gatim labhate naraḥ dvijānām veda vidvasām koṭim saṃpūjya yat phalam bhikṣā mātra pradānena tat phalam śiva yogine ye ca apavādam kurvanti vimūḍhāḥ śiva yoginām śrotṛbhiḥ te prapadyante narakeṣu ā mahī kṣayāt tasmāt śrotā ca pāpīyāḥ daṇḍyaḥ su mahatām mataḥ te vidanti mahā bhogān ante yogam ca śāṃkaram bhoga arthibhiḥ naraiḥ tasmāt saṃpūjyāḥ śiva yoginaḥ pratiśraya anna pāna ādyaiḥ śayyā prāvaraṇa ādibhiḥ deśaḥ bhavet pūtaḥ sa pūtaḥ iti kim punar sarva duḥkha prahāṇāya śiva yogam samabhyaset siddha yoga phalaḥ yogī lokānām hita kāmyayā bhogān bhuktvā yathākāmam viharet vā atra vartatām yaḥ tu āsannām mṛtim martyaḥ dṛṣṭa ariṣṭam ca bhūyasā saḥ yoga ārambha nirataḥ śiva kṣetram samāśrayet prāṇān vinā api roga ādyaiḥ svayam eva parityajet kṛtvā api anaśanam ca eva hutvā ca aṅgam śiva anale tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tatra sadyas eva vimucyeta na atra kāryā vicāraṇā roga ādyaiḥ vā atha vivaśaḥ śiva kṣetram samāśritaḥ yathā hi maraṇam śreṣṭham uśanti anaśana ādibhiḥ manasā kriyate yatas hatvā pīḍitaḥ svayam eva vā yaḥ tyajet dustyajān prāṇān na saḥ bhūyas prajāyate mahā nindā ratam hantum aśaktaḥ yaḥ svayam mṛtaḥ śiva arthe yaḥ tyajet prāṇān śiva bhakta artham eva vā na tena sadṛśaḥ kaścid mukti mārga sthitaḥ naraḥ tasmāt śīghratarā muktiḥ tasya saṃsāra maṇḍalāt na eva āśaucam prapadyeta tad putra ādi viśeṣāt śiva cāra artham athavā śiva vidyā artham eva vā khanet vā bhuvi tad deham dahet vā śucinā agninā kṣipet vā apsu śivāsu eva tyajet vā kāṣṭha loṣṭa vat bhaktān ca tarpayet iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe śaivayogavarṇanam nāma ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tatas prabhāta samaye naimiṣīyāḥ tapodhanāḥ tadā brahma samādeśāt devī sākṣāt sarasvatī prasannā svādu salilā prāvartata nadī śubhā sarasvatīm nadīm dṛṣṭvā munayaḥ hṛṣṭa mānasāḥ atha santarpya deva ādīn tadīyaiḥ salilaiḥ śivaiḥ smarantaḥ pūrva vṛttāntam yayuḥ vārāṇasīm prati tadā te himavat pādāt pantatīm dakṣiṇāmukhīm dṛṣṭvā bhāgīrathī tatra snātvā tad tīrāt yayuḥ tatas vārāṇasīm prāpya muditāḥ sarve eva te tadā uttara pravāhāyām gaṅgāyām avagāhya ca avimukteśvaram liṅgam dṛṣṭvā abhyarcya vidhānāt sūrya koṭi pratīkāśam tejaḥ divyam mahā adbhutam atha pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ bhasma sañchanna vigrahāḥ tathā vilīyamāneṣu tapasviṣu mahātmasu tat dṛṣṭvā mahat āścaryam naimiṣīyāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ prāk eva eṣām tu gamanāt pavanaḥ loka pāvanaḥ darśanam naimiṣīyāṇām saṃvādaḥ taiḥ mahātmanaḥ śuddhām buddhim tatas teṣām sa ambe sa anucare śive samāptim ca api satrasya dīrghapūrvasya sattriṇām tadā anavasarāt eva dvāḥsthaiḥ dvāri nivāritāḥ munayaḥ brahma bhavanāt bahis pārśvam upāviśan atha tumburuṇā gāne samatām prāpya nāradaḥ sāhacaryeṣu anujñātaḥ brahmanā parameṣṭhinā tyaktvā paraspara sparddhām maitrīm ca paramām gataḥ upavīṇayitum devam nakuli īśvaram īśvaram bhavanāt niryayau dhātuḥ jaladāt aṃśumant iva tam dṛṣṭvā ṣaṭkulīyāḥ te nāradam muni go vṛṣam praṇamya avasaram śambhoḥ papracchuḥ parama ādarāt tena te viviśuḥ veśma piṇḍībhūyāṃḍa janmanaḥ praviśya dūratas devam praṇamya bhuvi daṇḍa vat samīpe tad anujñātāḥ parivṛtya upatasthire tān tatra avasthitān pṛṣṭvā kuśalam kamalāsanaḥ vṛttāntam vaḥ mayā jñātam vāyuḥ eva āha naḥ yatas bhavadbhiḥ kim kṛtam paścāt māruta antarhite sati gamanam yātrām vārāṇasīm prati darśanam tatra liṅgānām sthāpitānām sureśvaraiḥ mahataḥ tasya tejas rāśeḥ ca darśanam munīnām vilayam tatra nirodham tejasaḥ tatas yāthātmya vedanam tasya ciṃtitasya api ca ātmabhiḥ munibhiḥ kathitam śrutvā viśvakarmā caturmukhaḥ kaṃpayitvā śiraḥ kiṃcid prāha gambhīrayā girā pratyāsīdati vaḥ siddhiḥ āmuṣmikā parā prasāda abhimukhaḥ bhūtaḥ iti bhūtārtha sūcitam tu tat liṅga saṃjñitam sākṣāt tejaḥ māheśvaram param tatra līnāḥ ca munayaḥ śrauta pāśupata vratāḥ muktāḥ babhūvuḥ svasthāḥ ca naiṣṭhikāḥ dagdha kilbiṣāḥ sa ca ayam arthaḥ sūcyeta yuṣmad dṛṣṭena tejasā prayāta dakṣiṇam meroḥ śikharam deva sevitam pratīkṣya āgamanam sākṣāt bhūtanāthasya nandinaḥ purā sanatkumāraḥ api dṛṣṭvā api parameśvaram ajñānāt sarva yogi indra mānī vinaya dūṣitaḥ tatas aparādhāt kruddhena mahā uṣṭraḥ nandinā kṛtaḥ upāsya devam devīm ca nandinam ca anunīya vai kathaṃcid uṣṭra tā tasya prayatnena nivāritā prāpitaḥ hi yathāpūrvam sanatpūrvām kumāra tām avajñāya hi mām eva tathā aham kṛtavan muniḥ brahmaṇaḥ pūrvajaḥ putraḥ mām mūḍhaḥ iva saṃsmaran saḥ evam vyāhṛtaḥ bhūyas sarva bhūta gaṇāgraṇī yat para ājñāpanam mūrdhnā prātar pratigṛhītavan prasāda artham gaṇasya asya tapaḥ carati duścaram draṣṭavyaḥ ca iti yuṣmābhiḥ prāk gaṇeśa samāgamāt tad prasāda artham acirāt nandī tatra āgamiṣyati iti satvaram ādiśya preṣitāḥ viśvayoginā meroḥ dakṣiṇam munayaḥ yayuḥ iti śrī śiva mahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe naimiṣarṣiyātrāvarṇanam nāma catvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca amṛta svādu śiśira svacchāḥ gādha laghu udakam samantataḥ saṃghaṭitam sphaṭikaḥ pala saṃcayaiḥ taraṃgaiḥ abhra saṃkāśaiḥ ākāśam iva bhūmi gam sukha avataraṇa ārohaiḥ sthalaiḥ nīla śilā mayaiḥ sopāna mārgau ruciraiḥ śobhamāna aṣṭa diś mukham tatra avatīrṇaiḥ ca yathā tatra uttīrṇaḥ ca bhūyasā snātaiḥ sita upavītaiḥ ca śukla a kaupīna valkalaiḥ muṇḍaiḥ tripuṇḍra kṛta maṇḍanaiḥ ghaṭaiḥ kamalinī pattra puṭaiḥ ca kalaśaiḥ śivaiḥ tādṛśaiḥ karaka ādibhiḥ ātma artham ca para artham ca devatā artham viśeṣataḥ māna salilam ātta puṣpam ca nityaśas antar jala śilā ārūḍhaiḥ nīcānām sparśa śaṅkayā munibhiḥ kṛta bhasma aṅga dhūsaraiḥ itas tatas majjadbhiḥ iṣṭa śiṣṭaiḥ śilā gataiḥ sthāne sthāne kṛta aneka bali puṣpa samīraṇaiḥ kvacid ca tṛṣayā āyāta mṛgī mṛga turaṃgamam kvacid pīta jana uttīrṇa mayūra vara vāraṇam kvacid kṛta taṭa āghāta vṛṣa prativṛṣa ujjvalam kvacid kāraṇḍava ravaiḥ kvacid sārasa kūjitaiḥ snāna pāna ādi karaṇaiḥ sva saṃpad druma jīvibhiḥ praṇayāt prāṇibhiḥ taiḥ taiḥ bhāṣamāṇam iva asakṛt taiḥ ivāniśam ātapa upahatān sarvān na amantrayat ivāniśam vedau vajra śilā mayyām mṛdule mṛga carmaṇi sanatkumāram āsīnam śaśvat bāla vapurdharam tad kāla mātra uparatam samādheḥ acala ātmanaḥ dadṛśuḥ naimiṣeyāḥ te praṇatāḥ ca upatasthire procuḥ dadṛśe tad kṣaṇe tasmin vimānam bhānu saṃnibham apsaras gaṇa saṃkīrṇam rudra kanyābhiḥ āvṛtam mṛdaṅga muraja udghuṣṭam veṇu vīṇā rava anvitam citra ratna vitāna āḍhyam muktā dāma virājitam nṛtyadbhiḥ ca eva gāyadbhiḥ vādayadbhiḥ ca saṃvṛtam kṛta gopura satkāram ketunā mānya hetunā divya siṃhāsana ārūḍham devyā suyaśayā saha śriyā ca vapuṣā ca eva tribhiḥ ca api vilocanaiḥ prākāraiḥ abhikṛtyānām pratyabhijñāpakam prabhoḥ sarva anugrahaṇam śambhoḥ sākṣāt iva puras sthitam śilāda tanayam sākṣāt śrīmat śūla vara āyudham viśvasya api vidhātR̥ṇām nigraha anugraha kṣamam catur bāhum udāra aṅgam candra rekhā vibhūṣitam kaṇṭhe nāgena maulau ca śaśāṅkena api alaṃkṛtam samāptam iva nirvāṇam sarvajñam iva saṃgatam dṛṣṭvā prahṛṣṭa vadanaḥ brahma putraḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ praṇamya daṇḍa vat devam stutvā vyajñāpayat munīm ṣaṭkulīyāḥ ime dīrgham naimiṣe satram āsthitāḥ māgatāḥ brahmaṇā ādiṣṭāḥ pūrvam eva abhikāṃkṣayā śrutvā vākyam brahma putrasya nandī chittvā pāśān dṛṣṭipātena sadyas mahā bhāga ca aiśvaram jñāna yogam dattvā bhūyas deva pārśvam jagāma sanatkumāreṇa ca tat samastam vyāsāya sākṣāt gurave mama uktam na a veda vidbhyaḥ kathanīyam etat purāṇa ratnam puraśāsanasya na abhakta śiṣyāya ca nāstikebhyaḥ dattam hi mohāt nirayam dadāti mārgeṇa sevā anugatena yaiḥ tat dattam gṛhītam paṭhitam śrutam vā atas gamiṣye aham avāpta kāmaḥ samastam eva astu śivam sadā naḥ sūte kṛta āśiṣi gate munayaḥ su vṛttāḥ yāge ca paryavasite mahati prayoge bāle kalau ca viṣayaiḥ kaluṣāyamāṇe vārāṇasī parisare vasatim vinetuḥ atha ca te paśu pāśa mumukṣayā akhila tayā kṛta pāśupata vratāḥ uvāca etat śiva purāṇam hi samāptam hitam ādarāt nāstikāya na vaktavyam aśraddhāya śaṭhāya ca tasmāt punar punar ca eva śrotavyam hi mumukṣubhiḥ pañca āvṛttiḥ prakartavyā purāṇasya asya sat dhyā param phalam samuddiśya tat prāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ purātanāḥ ca rājānaḥ viprāḥ vaiśyāḥ ca sattamāḥ śroṣyati atha api yaḥ ca idam mānavaḥ bhakti tatparaḥ etat śiva purāṇam hi śivasya ati priyam param vaktuḥ śrotuḥ ca sarvadā sa gaṇaḥ sa sutaḥ sa ambaḥ śam karotu saḥ śaṃkaraḥ iti śrī śivamahāpurāṇe saptamyām vāyavīyasaṃhitāyām uttara khaṇḍe vyāsopadeśaśrīśivamahāpurāṇamāhātmyavarṇanam nāma ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ māptaḥ ayam granthaḥ
